Soviet Russia Lodges Another Protest with Poland

Japan United, Moscow, 1st -- Regarding the case of someone plotting to bomb the Warsaw Labor and Peasant Embassy in April, the Polish government has already stated that it is making every effort to arrest the perpetrators. The Labor and Peasant Government is still not satisfied and today submitted a new note to the Polish government.

All Japan Labor Union Federation

Japan United, Osaka, 2nd -- The inaugural meeting of the All Japan Labor Union Federation opened at 10:00 AM yesterday at the Osaka Central Public Hall. 751 representatives and delegates attended. The new alliance is composed of the Japan Labor Union Federation, the former National Labor Union Alliance, the Hokkaido Labor General Alliance, and other local organizations. Its members come from three prefectures and sixteen counties, with 90 organizations and a total of 41,990 union members. The types of occupations are as follows: metal, silk manufacturing, spinning, electrical, gas, transportation, transshipment, communications, industry, civil engineering, construction, chemical, lumber, production, mining, maritime and river affairs, and street labor.

British Conservative Party Promotes Policies

Advocates Implementing Protective Tariffs

Reuters, London, 1st -- Conservative Party leader Baldwin stated in a speech in Leeds yesterday that when the future Conservative Party regains power and proposes levying taxes on foreign food to give preferential treatment to imperial food, a national plebiscite will be held. Only in this way can public opinion be accurately known, and the government can act according to public opinion, so that later governments will not deem it necessary to abolish existing economic contracts. Baldwin also said that those who implement the McKenna protective tariffs are entrusted by the people and have the support of the majority of Parliament. The Conservative Party did not expect that today's minority Labor government would want to eliminate them.

Issue of Supreme Command

Atmosphere in the Japanese Military Still Ominous

Electrics Communication, Tokyo, 2nd -- Although yesterday was Sunday, Minister of the Navy Zaibu summoned senior naval officials to his official residence at 12:30 PM to exchange important opinions. Although the content of the meeting was not made public, veteran generals with combat experience, while not directly dissenting from the contents of the London Naval Treaty, raised rather severe questions about the Minister of the Navy's report on the details of the decision on supreme command and military strength. Furthermore, after the meeting, at 6:30 PM, the Minister of the Navy summoned Lieutenant General Sakonji, Director of the Naval Affairs Bureau Kori, and others to discuss future countermeasures for over an hour. The atmosphere in the military does not seem easy to ease.

Another Telegram: The government views the decision of the military council and official meetings regarding supreme command as a problem within the Navy Ministry, not a dispute between the government and the military. Moreover, the government is not bound by the decisions of the military council, so it holds an optimistic view. However, many in the Privy Council attach great importance to the future of this issue, as their interpretation is as follows: (1) The decision on military strength by the supreme organ of the navy, the military council, must have the consent of the Chief of the Naval General Staff to be definitive. The Minister of the Navy, who complies with this regulation, clearly holds a different view from Prime Minister Hamaguchi. (2) Director Kato, in light of the intentions of the military council, believes he is unworthy of his position and is determined to resign. (3) The above has a significant impact on the fate of the government. Although the Minister of the Navy has stated that even if Director Kato resigns, he himself will not resign, he cannot submit Director Kato's resignation alone due to his responsibility. The government fears that the problem will become serious and plans to postpone it until Full-Power Minister Wakatsuki returns home. However, what kind of waves the joint military council meeting of the Navy and Army will cause after Wakatsuki returns home will be enough to determine the fate of the government, so the government is paying great attention to this.

Merger of Two Major British Liberal Newspapers

Reuters, London, 1st -- The Daily Chronicle and the Daily News will merge tomorrow. The combined daily circulation of the two newspapers will be 1.6 million copies. After the merger, the two newspapers will become a major newspaper of the Liberal Party.

Important News

Central Party Headquarters and National Government Weekly Memorial Service

Central Party Headquarters: At 9:00 AM on the 2nd, the Central Party Headquarters held its 62nd weekly memorial service for the late Dr. Sun Yat-sen in the auditorium. Central Committee members Dai Chuanxian, Chen Guofu, Shao Yuanchong, Chen Lifu, Yu Jingtang, and others, as well as staff and guests from various departments, totaling approximately 500 people, attended. Chairman Dai Chuanxian presided over the ceremony. The chairman reported, stating that among the recent resolutions of the Central Committee, there were two of significant importance, which he specifically presented for the report to all comrades. (1) Every nation-building party has a central force. In a long history, it continues to be responsible for national political reforms and progress, creating the pillars of the country and consolidating the foundation of the country, so that politics does not go astray and the country can be long-lasting and stable. Otherwise, it is enough to cause chaos. The responsibilities of political parties in countries such as Britain and the United States are all like this. The Chinese Kuomintang has more than 40 years of revolutionary history and bears the sole responsibility of nation-building. The final success depends on the comrades of the party having an independent and unyielding spirit, intensifying their work, and firming their will. Therefore, it has been decided to first set an example from the Central Party Headquarters, concentrating its own strength. All comrades serving in the party headquarters will voluntarily contribute a portion of their income to help create a new construction with extreme glory and extreme value, to be completed within two years, to create the most magnificent new memorial for the party. Currently, during the period of political tutelage, the position of the party is to train the people and exercise political power. The so-called new construction is to infuse the party's nation-building plan and spirit into the general public, so that everyone understands the location of political responsibility and further enables the country, society, and nation to achieve great unity. When the constitutional period arrives, political power will be returned to the people, completing the nation-building strategy. This kind of preparatory work is extremely important. In this way, after the return of political power to the people, the party will have the eternal glory of not being replaced, and the people will still believe in its leadership and always display great effects. (2) All national commemorations must have significant meaning and permanent and universal characteristics, so that the people can concentrate their spirit and increase their patriotic movement. The Central Committee believes that it is necessary to re-regulate all kinds of memorial days that China currently has. It has now been decided to reduce or merge memorial days according to their history and nature and specifically designate them as national memorial days. The principles of these national memorial days are: one, those with permanent commemorative nature; two, those with universal commemorative nature; and three, those with important significance related to national independence. However, matters that have commemorative value for a part of the people and matters that can be jointly commemorated internationally, if they do not conflict with the party's ideology and are under the leadership of the party's policies, can also be freely commemorated without being prohibited. The above two matters are very important, so it is hoped that all comrades will pay attention to them. After the report was finished, the meeting adjourned at 10:30 AM.

National Government: At 10:00 AM on the same morning, the National Government held a weekly memorial service for the late Dr. Sun Yat-sen. Those present included Tan Yankai, Gu Yingfen, Zhu Peide, Chen Shaokuan, Zhou Yawei, Zhang Nanxian, Wei Daoming, Liu Ruiheng, Jiang Menglin, Niu Yongjian, Zhang Wohua, Chen Yu, Zhu Jingxi, Yi Peiji, Li Zhonggong, Chen Yi, Zhang Xiqian, Li Jinglun, Fan Guang, and others, as well as over 300 staff members from the National Government's civilian and military offices. Chairman Tan Yankai presided over the ceremony. Secretary Qian Changzhao gave the following political report: "The military situation at the front is very smooth, but recently, foreign-language newspapers in Shanghai have published many unfounded rumors. It has been found that the origin of the rumors is either from the Tianjin-Beijing area or from fabrications. In the Tianjin-Beijing area, foreign mendicants such as Simpson have been bought off by Yan Xishan to do his propaganda, creating unfavorable news about the Central Government all day long, and foreign-language newspapers in Shanghai republish these news. Rumors that originate from fabrications, such as Minister Liu of the Ministry of Health going to the front to inspect hospital work, and foreign-language newspapers in Shanghai spreading rumors that Chairman Chiang was injured, are ridiculous and hateful. Now is a time of war, and such rumors can cause social unrest and shake people's hearts, so it is necessary to prohibit them. I hope that foreign-language newspapers in Shanghai will be particularly cautious when publishing news in the future, otherwise they will be punished. The Law on the Preservation of Antiquities was passed and promulgated at the State Council meeting last Friday. This law is of great importance to our country's culture, and I am specifically bringing it up today for discussion. Antiquities themselves can represent the national culture of the past and naturally have value for research. Researching the national culture of the past can help us promote the national spirit of the present and observe the national trends of the future. Its importance is self-evident. Some say that the national question in recent times is not a question of national bloodlines, but a question of national culture. This statement has insightful. However, to understand the national culture issues of the present, one must first study the national culture of the past. Especially in China, which has a history of four or five thousand years, we cannot suddenly leave the society of historical inheritance. Then, the national culture of the past should be fundamentally understood, and the preservation of antiquities representing the national culture of the past should not be neglected. In the past, our country paid too little attention to the preservation of antiquities. As a result, countless antiquities were destroyed, ruined, or transported to foreign countries. Even if some are still well-preserved, they are only used as antiques and toys, losing the true use and value of antiquities. I will now briefly talk about the most common six points. (1) The general public lacks common sense, and often very valuable antiquities are thought to have little value, and as a result, they are destroyed and ruined. For example, the Thousand Buddha Cliff of Qixia Mountain is decorated with cement, making it unbearably vulgar, what a pity. (2) Private collections of antiquities are either not well-preserved, resulting in a large number of damages, or

Page 9

Continuing Important News

they are well-preserved but not made public to the public, either as research materials or as commodities to be sold for a good price, resulting in them falling into the hands of foreigners. These are all bad phenomena. (3) Public institutions that collect antiquities lack responsible custodians, and as a result, very valuable items are stolen or replaced with counterfeit products. Sometimes, institution staff even embezzle, and the central and local governments do not pay attention, so batches of antiquities are smuggled into the market. (4) Some merchants have short-sighted eyes. They search everywhere, and through fraudulent means and low prices, they buy very valuable antiquities and then transport them to Shanghai, Tianjin, and other places to sell to foreigners. Few Chinese are willing to spend large sums of money to buy antiquities, or they directly transport them to our country, where they can obtain huge profits, but the national loss is not small. (5) Some unscrupulous foreigners, under the pretext of evangelism or cultural investigation, travel in the interior of our country, paying attention to antiquities at all times, either buying them at huge prices or even stealing them privately. Many things are missing from the Dunhuang stone chambers in this way. (6) Foreigners rely on political power to seize antiquities by taking advantage of opportunities, such as when the Eight-Nation Alliance entered Beijing. In addition to the countless antiquities that were destroyed and trampled, the number that were robbed was also considerable. Today, they are still displayed in famous foreign libraries and museums, which is heartbreaking to talk about. At this moment, we must think of ways to reverse the situation. For the first point, which is a matter of general public knowledge, it is not easy to remedy it in a short time. For the second point, we hope that all private collections of antiquities should improve their preservation methods and register with the local administrative authorities. We further hope that they will lend their antiquities to archaeologists, historians, and others for research, and the transfer of antiquities to foreigners will be absolutely prohibited. For the third point, if public institutions that preserve antiquities are negligent or fraudulent, the central and local administrative authorities should investigate the matter and impose severe penalties. For the fourth point, as long as the government enacts a law prohibiting the transfer of antiquities to foreigners, the danger can be reduced. For the fifth point, the central and local authorities should be responsible for paying attention to this at all times and in all places in the future. If it is discovered that foreigners are indeed engaged in illegal activities, negotiations should be initiated immediately. For the sixth point, our country is now striving to become stronger and should not be trampled by imperialists again. The governments of the countries that robbed antiquities during the last Eight-Nation Alliance invasion should return them all for the sake of promoting friendly relations. The above statements are all about the preservation of antiquities. When it comes to the excavation of antiquities, its nature is equally important. I believe that the academic institutions in charge of excavation should be clearly designated by the central government. The work of excavation, except in the frontier areas where it is very inconvenient for the central government to send people to excavate, should be undertaken by academic institutions directly under the central government. In this way, human and financial resources will be more economical, otherwise it will be both uneconomical and easy to cause conflicts. I will now give an example. The excavation of the Yin Ruins in Anyang, Henan, has been going on for 31 years since 1899. Because there has been no truly responsible organization for the excavation, there have been several unscientific collections, and the academic loss has been great. Since the year before last, the Academia Sinica has sent personnel to excavate, and progress has gradually been made, and works have been published. However, in the past year, local people have been causing trouble, and the work has been progressing very slowly, almost coming to a standstill, which is truly disheartening for academic researchers. When the central government formulates a complete plan for the excavation of antiquities, it should pay attention to this and ensure that the power of the excavation organization is unified to avoid obstacles."

Anniversary of the Establishment of the Ministry of Navy

Chen Shaokuan, Li Shijia, Wang Shouting, and others all gave speeches. The Ministry of Navy of the National Government officially established on June 1st last year, yesterday (the 1st) was its first anniversary. At 9:00 AM that morning, all members of the ministry and officers from various ships of the fleet in Beijing gathered in the auditorium of the ministry to hold a commemorative ceremony. Flags and decorations were hung inside and outside the ministry, creating a magnificent spectacle. The officers and soldiers were neatly dressed and in high spirits. Deputy Minister Chen Shaokuan presided over the ceremony. After the ceremony, Deputy Minister Chen delivered an opening speech, recalling the past and encouraging the future, with many sincere words that moved the entire audience. Next, Ministry member representative Li Shijia, Director of the General Affairs Department, and fleet representative Wang Shouting, captain of the Hai Rong warship, also gave speeches successively. The following is a record of Deputy Minister Chen's speech:

"Today is the first anniversary of the establishment of our ministry. Everyone is able to celebrate here, and to celebrate on such a grand scale, everyone must be very happy. However, everyone also has a deep understanding of the meaning of celebration and happiness. At the same time, they should work harder in accordance with this understanding. We still remember that our Ministry of Navy was sacrificed under the iron hooves of the warlords. They intended to destroy us, changing the Ministry of Navy to the Naval Bureau, and then changing the Naval Bureau to the Naval Office, step by step to eliminate us. In the end, they simply wanted to eliminate the navy completely. The water stoppage agency would not allow us to exist, and even the officers in the ministry were driven out completely, not one remaining in Peiping. It was not until the Northern Expedition of the National Revolutionary Army that the soldiers of our army worked extremely hard to fight the warlords, counter-revolutionaries, and imperialists to the end. Therefore, the central government, observing all the internal and external situations, believed that it was necessary to quickly establish a Ministry of Navy. So, on this day last year, the government resolutely ordered the establishment of the Ministry of Navy. Now, a year has passed. We can say that we have today as a result of everyone's efforts. In other words, with everyone's efforts, we can establish the Ministry of Navy. If we do not work hard from today onwards, then the collapse of the Ministry of Navy will be inevitable. The reason why the Ministry of Navy in Peiping ultimately collapsed was, of course, because the warlords oppressed us, but half of it was also because the former Ministry of Navy stood under the corrupt government in Peiping and was surrounded by its atmosphere, inevitably染污their bad habits. First, there was the cause of self-destruction, so it was easy for this result to occur. Now, the question of whether this Ministry of Navy under the National Government can exist depends on everyone's efforts. Regarding the work of the past year, the ministry has already prepared a general report, which will be published soon. I will now give a brief report. Since the establishment of the ministry, a great deal of effort has been put into formulating regulations by the officers. Everyone, regardless of the cold or heat, day or night, has created all the regulations. All that should be promoted and reformed has been demarcated. Therefore, so much has been achieved in the past year. At the same time, in recent times, we have built several warships. The repairs and modifications are not included. The Yixian warship, which was recently planned, is now being rushed to be built and is scheduled to hold the launching ceremony on the anniversary of the Premier's birth in the second half of the year. This ship has 1,600 tons, much larger than the ones previously built. We were able to build this warship by relying on diligence, thrift, and savings. As for the artillery power of the warships in the army, we have also replenished it fully during these times, and without spending a lot of money. At the same time, we have devoted all our energy to training and education. The fleet held a large-scale exercise last year. Many warships have freed up time to participate in the exercise. Those warships that did not have time to participate in the exercise also practiced various tactics and exercises in their own defense positions. Regarding the training of soldiers, we have 500 soldiers in our training camp and 100 signal soldiers, totaling 600, who are all being trained urgently. The soldiers who were originally serving on the warships are being transferred out in batches to learn about guns, artillery, torpedoes, and electricity. A training class is set up for each subject to allow them to practice and train them to achieve success. As for the general officials, we always encourage everyone to seek knowledge. The previous time, eight officials and twelve students were sent to England to study naval affairs. This year, we plan to send several batches of students to England and Japan. We have improved the regulations and rules of the existing naval schools one by one, and conscientiously recruited students, recruiting 100 new students, who have now started classes. For the members of the ministry, regarding the work of the ministry itself, on the fleet side, since the establishment of the ministry, we have mobilized the fleet and worked hard on combat, bandit suppression, and local defense. Not only on the Yangtze River, but everywhere depends on the navy to protect their peace. The waters of Fujian, Zhejiang, and the vicinity of Guangdong have not been spared by our warships in suppressing the Communists and bandits. We are also working extremely hard to move forward. In addition to the Yixian warship, which I just mentioned, we also plan to quickly build the Minsheng and Minzu warships, so that they can join the Minquan and realize the Three Principles of the People. The Minsheng will be started this autumn. I have just briefly reported on our work. The achievements are all due to the consistent efforts of the officers and staff of all departments. In the past year, because Minister Yang concurrently served as the chairman of the Fujian Provincial Government, and was also ill, he was unable to attend to the affairs of the ministry. I have been acting on his behalf. My talent is insufficient, so I only have this report today. I believe that if the minister is personally working in the ministry, then the work report and achievements in this year must be ten times more than this. From now on, I hope that our officers, staff, and all the soldiers of the army will work harder with one heart and one mind. Then, with our vigorous spirit, we will be afraid that we will have many more achievements every year. Here, I hope that everyone will continue to work hard based on love and sincerity, regardless of difficulties and hardships. This is the true color of our revolutionary navy. This is the ministry's fervent hope for the entire army, and it is also what I personally hope for our officers and soldiers."

Prohibition of Business Firms Concurrently Operating Savings Accounts

Order from the Executive Yuan to the Ministries of Industry and Commerce, and Finance, to Draft a Bill

Yesterday, regarding the matter of prohibiting business firms from concurrently operating savings accounts, the Executive Yuan issued an instruction to the Ministries of Industry and Commerce, and Finance, stating: "The National Government issued Instruction No. 1190, which included a letter from the Central Political Council stating that the Jiangsu Provincial Government had previously sent a letter, referring to a communication from the Ministry of Finance, regarding a report from the Shanghai Banking Association. The report stated that recently, various business firms in Shanghai have been engaging in savings operations as a way to attract business. The actual security of these savings is unknown, and these operations have not been approved by the government in advance. Should any negligence occur, it would greatly harm the livelihoods of ordinary people. They requested a decision on how to declare guarantees, restrict abuses, and generally oversee the savings business. The points raised were deemed to have merit. Besides communicating to the relevant departments, it was also specifically communicated to instruct the Finance and Construction Bureaus to thoroughly investigate and prohibit such activities in various counties and business associations, and to report back. However, the establishment of various savings associations originated with foreigners, and ordinary business firms have subsequently followed suit. The amount of capital they possess and how they operate is generally unknown. People who invest in these firms have no guarantee whatsoever. However, simply prohibiting them with empty words may not be effective. It was requested that the Economic Affairs Committee deliberate on a more thorough and far-reaching method and provide a prompt reply for compliance." This matter was submitted to the council. After being reviewed by the Economic Affairs Committee, it was stated that ordinary business firms engaging in savings business should be held accountable, and that the Ministries of Finance and Industry and Commerce should be tasked with drafting a savings law and submitting it to the Legislative Yuan. It was further decided at the 226th meeting of the council to approve the review opinion, record the matter, and send the original letter from the Jiangsu Provincial Government (in mimeographed form) to the Ministries of Finance and Industry and Commerce to follow and implement, and to report back. A copy of the original letter was attached and duly acknowledged. The matter was then submitted to the 76th National Affairs Conference of this government, and it was resolved to comply. In addition to issuing a reply, the original attachments were urgently copied and issued to the relevant departments, instructing them to follow, and to communicate to the Ministries of Finance and Industry and Commerce to follow, and to report back. Therefore, the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce were instructed to work together to draft a savings law and submit it for review."

Lu Diping Appointed Commander-in-Chief of the Ninth Route Army

Officially Assumes Office on June 1st

A dispatch from Nanchang on May 30th reported that after Zhang Guitang's remnant forces fled into southern Hunan, they intended to cross from Guidong and Rucheng into Lianhua and Yongxin in western Jiangxi, advancing towards Pingxiang and the Jiangxi-Hubei border, with their destination being Jiujiang and Wuhan. However, the central government had already made arrangements to deal with these remnant forces. In addition to the Sixth and Eighth Route Armies pursuing them from northern Guangdong and the Fourth Route Army engaging them head-on in southern Hunan, Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek, in order to quickly resolve the situation and prevent these forces from becoming roving bandits, specially appointed Lu Diping, the former commander of the Second Army and the current chairman of Jiangxi Province, as the commander-in-chief of the Ninth Route Army. All troops stationed in Jiangxi were placed under his command. Lu officially received Chiang's appointment on the 29th and is actively organizing the headquarters of the Ninth Route Army. He is scheduled to issue a circular telegram on June 1st to formally assume office and immediately launch an attack on Zhang Guitang's remnant forces. Of the defenses in this province, northern Jiangxi is the most important because Jiujiang is the hub of the Yangtze River, connecting to Wuhu and Anqing downstream and reaching Wuhan upstream. Currently, troops are stationed here, and numerous warships are anchored in the river, making the defenses extremely solid. It is reported that Commander-in-Chief Lu, after completing preparations on all sides, will lead his troops to advance towards the Hunan-Hubei border, with the aim of joining forces with the Fourth, Sixth, and Eighth Route Armies to eliminate Zhang Guitang's remnant forces in the shortest possible time.

Han Fuqu's Troops Besiege Qingcheng

Enemy Regiment at Taizi Surrenders

A dispatch from Jinan reported, according to a forward report obtained by the First Army Corps, that Han Fuqu is currently supervising the troops north of Zhangqiu City. The Jin forces that have crossed the river consist of a total of three regiments: one regiment at the Qidong Taizi Yellow River crossing and two regiments at Qingcheng. A battalion has been detached to be stationed in Boxing, and a company has been detached to be stationed in Gaoyuan. The regiment at Taizi engaged Sun Tongxuan's troops under Han Fuqu's command since dawn yesterday (the 29th). After fierce fighting until 12:00 noon, they were disarmed by Han's troops. A total of eight machine guns, ten mortars, and over a hundred rifles were seized. The Taizi Yellow River crossing is now occupied by Han's troops. Not only can the Jin forces no longer cross the river, but the enemy at Qingcheng and other places are fighting with their backs to the water, their retreat cut off. Qingcheng has been surrounded by Han's troops since last night, and the attack began this morning. It is expected to be resolved tonight. There has been no fighting on the Jinpu Railway front since noon yesterday until this morning. (30th)

Deployment of Enemy Troops on the Longhai Railway

Zhang Fang Establishes a Provincial Government Office in Guide

A dispatch from Xuzhou reported that there have been continuous fierce battles between the two armies on the Longhai Line, but there have been no major changes in the lines. The Feng and Yan armies on the Longhai and Pinghan lines are trying to establish contact, extending from Lanfeng in the north to Xuchang in the south, passing through Chenliu, Qixian, Tongxu, Weishi, Yuchuan, Changge, and other places, forming a rounded defensive line. The Lanfeng-Luowang line is the most fortified, with the Jin army and the troops of Sun Liangcheng and Ji Hongchang stationed on this line. Song Zheyuan is on the Qixian line. In addition to attacking Lanfeng, the Central Army is also attacking the northeast of Lanfeng and crossing the river with a portion of its forces to cut off their rear.

Regarding the affairs of Henan Province, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek previously telegraphed Zhang Fang, inviting him to go west to prepare to go to Bian. He has now ordered Zhang to act as chairman of Henan Province and appointed Zhang Honglie, the former director of education of Henan Province, to assist Zhang Fang in establishing a provincial government office to manage political affairs. Currently, the two Zhangs have established a temporary office in the Second Middle School in Guide and have temporarily carved a wooden seal, waiting for the progress of the front lines before going to Bian to take over provincial affairs. (31st)

Details of Xu Zhuoran's Assassination

A dispatch from Xiamen reported that Xu Zhuoran, who had a deep connection with the political situation in Fujian, was assassinated at 3:30 PM on the 28th in front of the Fengyi Money Exchange in Dashi Lane, Xiamen. He was shot five times and sent to the Xiusheng Hospital on Gulangyu for treatment. He died of his injuries at 5:30 AM on the 29th. This is a recent major incident in Fujian.

Page 10

During the political upheaval in Fujian Province, Xu happened to be in Guangdong. He then went to Beijing and Shanghai for an extended stay, returning to Xiamen only on May 2nd. In the past month, he frequently traveled between Zhangzhou, Xiamen, and Tongan, always traveling with only a light entourage. Plotters took advantage of this opportunity. On the 27th, Xu accepted an invitation from Xiao Shuxuan, the head of the Training Corps, and went from Xiamen to Tongan. At 5:00 PM, he visited Chen Yanxiang, a director of the Tongmei Bus Company, and then went with him to Jimei to visit Ye Yuan, a school board director of Jimei School. Commander Xiao had dispatched four guards to escort him. Xu spent the night at Jimei School. At 5:00 AM on the 28th, he went with Chen Yanxiang to Shuitou by car. At 11:00 AM, he returned to Tongan and spoke with Xiao Shuxuan. At 1:00 PM, he went with Chen to Jimei again, in response to Ye Yuan's invitation from the evening of the 27th. After arriving at Jimei, he received a name card left by Ye at the station, which read "Fengyi Money Exchange, Dashi Lane, Xiamen, telephone number..." This indicated that Ye had gone to Xiamen and was inviting Xu to meet him there. Xu went with Chen by ferry to Gaoqi and ordered the guards to return to the corps, taking only his servant Xu Mu. The three of them boarded a ship to Gaoqi and took a car to the Meirengong Station in Xiamen. Xu ordered his servant to take his luggage to the Nanhua Hotel first, while he and Chen took a rickshaw to the entrance of Hengsheng Street and alighted. Xu walked ahead, and Chen followed behind. Upon reaching Miaohou Street, Chen asked Xu if he knew the way to Fengyi in Dashi Lane. Xu said he didn't, so Chen walked ahead to guide him. Arriving at Fengyi, Chen entered first. Xu was still outside the door when gunshots suddenly rang out. Chen looked back and saw Xu staggering in, holding his chest and abdomen, exclaiming that he had been attacked by thugs. Chen hurriedly closed the iron gate and immediately reported the incident to the Public Security Bureau and Xu's family by telephone. Ye Yuan was also at Fengyi at the time. Soon, Huang Kun, the leader of the Public Security Bureau's detective team, rushed to the scene. Xu was still able to speak, saying that there were four assassins, three of whom were wearing black Xiangyunsha shirts and pants, and one wearing yellow Shuijie cloth clothes and pants. After speaking, he was in extreme pain and on the verge of fainting. Ye Yuan and Chen Yanxiang called for Dr. Chen Chunmu to treat him. Chen arrived, and Xu said that his injuries were severe and that he would not survive, so there was no use in trying. Soon, the director of the Tongshan Hospital also arrived to administer emergency treatment. At 5:00 PM, he was sent to the Xiusheng Hospital on Gulangyu. Lin Huanzhang, the director of the Public Security Bureau, and Wang Zongshi, the head of the Third Police Precinct, also went there. After discussions among the doctors, it was generally agreed that his condition was critical, but there was hope if they could operate to see if his intestines were injured. Dr. Xi, the director of the Hongning Hospital, Dr. Kinoshita, the director of the Xiusheng Hospital, and Dr. Xia Liwei (all Americans) performed the surgery from 7:30 PM to 8:45 PM. He had been shot five times. Two bullets severed his left finger and grazed his back, causing no harm. One bullet entered his back on the left side, penetrated his diaphragm, and exited one inch from the center, which was also not fatal. However, one bullet entered from the right, causing the meningeal blood vessels to rupture and bleed. The stomach wall was injured and bleeding, and the bullet pierced his left liver and left ribs, exiting one inch from the center, which was the most serious. After the surgery, his condition was not good. At 12:00 AM, his pulse was still stable, but around 3:00 AM, it changed drastically. The wound reopened and bled. At 5:10 AM, the wound was in extreme pain, and he tried to climb out of bed. His relatives and friends dissuaded him. Xu uttered a few intermittent words, saying, "Dying for the revolution, I am very willing to die, but there are many things that have not been finished, which is very regrettable." The last two sentences were spoken in a very low voice. A nurse comforted him, and Xu asked, "What is your surname?" She replied that it was Cai. Xu then said, "Mr. Cai, you don't know me, what am I still afraid of?" After only these few words, without mentioning his family or his affairs, he became silent and unable to speak. At 5:30 AM, he lost blood, trembled, and died.

When Xu was injured, his family believed that Ye Yuan had invited Xu to meet in Jimei, but then had already gone to Xiamen and invited him to meet at Fengyi. The assassins ambushed outside the Fengyi door, making him seem suspicious. The Public Security Bureau was requested to detain Ye Yuan for investigation. He was later released on bail pending further summons. Chen Yanxiang was also detained by the Gulangyu Public Works Bureau. On the 29th, he was extradited to the Siming Court. (30th)

Riot and Jailbreak in Xiamen

A dispatch from Xiamen reported that on the morning of the 25th of this month, dozens of rioters suddenly stormed the Siming County Prison, releasing 54 prisoners, killing one warden and one guard, and injuring Captain Hu and three soldiers of the garrison team. This is an unprecedented major case in Xiamen. According to eyewitnesses inside the prison, at 9:45 AM that morning, two men wearing long gowns came to the side gate of the prison, each carrying a foreign tin biscuit box, claiming to be visiting Zeng Wenbin. The gatekeeper let them in and turned to the iron gate. The warden, Lu Yongzhong, conducted a routine inspection, but the two men suddenly pulled out pistols from the tin boxes and shot at Lu. Lu ran back to the office hallway, where he was intercepted by a second group of rioters. He was shot once in each breast and died on the spot. When the first group of rioters entered the prison and started the attack, the second group of three men also just entered the side gate under the pretext of visiting Wan Yaonan, and they also responded with gunfire. At this point, the guards at the side gate were too frightened to move. The third and fourth groups of rioters continued to pour in, about ten or more people. The first group had already seized the keys to the No. 5 and No. 9 cell blocks, the prison workshop, and the women's prison. They opened the doors one after another and used two pairs of wire cutters they had brought to break the fetters of the prisoners. The second and third groups entered to assist, and they quickly finished, seized the prison, and rushed out. While the first, second, and third groups of rioters were infiltrating the prison, many people were also lying in ambush around the Siming Prison and the county government, some disguised as peddlers selling goods in front of the county gate, some dressed as students pretending to visit friends at the Education Bureau of the county government, and some pretending to bargain with peddlers in front of the county gate. When the attack inside the prison was launched and the gunshots suddenly rang out, the rioters outside acted in unison. Some selling bayberries immediately dumped the bayberries on the ground and pulled out guns from the basket, shooting at the guards at the county government gate. Guard Luo Yousheng was shot in the right arm and fell to the ground. At the same time, Pan Yongdi was shot in the left rib, and Chen Shihai, standing next to Pan, was shot in the right chest. All fell to the ground. At this point, the rioters rose up and fired their guns. All three guards at the gate were injured, and the county government gate was under the control of the rioters. Wu Guangcheng, the captain of the garrison team of the Siming County government, and Li Ruikai, a prison guard, heard the sound and came out to investigate, but were also attacked by the rioters who had rushed into the gate. Wu was seriously injured and fell to the ground, and Li died instantly. At this time, the rioters and prisoners inside the prison rushed out, merged with the rioters guarding outside, and escaped from the county government, scattering towards Dashizi, Xizaiwei, Qiaozaitou, and Nanyihe Street, leisurely escaping. After an investigation, of the 27 prisoners in the prison workshop, only two civil debtors did not escape. Among the remaining 25 escaped prisoners, 18 were suspected communists. Of the 140 or so prisoners in cell blocks No. 5 and No. 9, 18 escaped, including three suspected communists. Of the 18 prisoners in the women's prison, 11 escaped, including three suspected communists. In total, 54 prisoners escaped from the three locations, including 24 suspected communists. Later, court bailiffs and police arrested four suspected communists in the surrounding area: Cao Yousheng (male), Deng Sangu, Zeng Dagu, and Qiu Ergu (all female), as well as three other criminals. Two others voluntarily returned to prison. The whereabouts of the remaining 45 escaped prisoners are unknown. Afterwards, Deng Ji'an, the president of the Siming District Court, telegraphed the Fujian High Court in Fuzhou to report the prison break. The original telegram read: "To His Excellency Wang, President of the Fujian High Court in Fuzhou, This morning at 10:00 AM, dozens of communists suddenly broke into the Siming Prison from outside, armed with over a dozen Mauser pistols. They shot and killed one warden and one guard. The captain of the garrison team and three soldiers were seriously injured and are in critical condition. The military police were unable to provide timely assistance and were unable to resist. Fifty or sixty communist prisoners and other prisoners were seized and escaped. I heard the alarm and risked my life to go and supervise the defense. The remaining two hundred or so prisoners were prevented from escaping. Director Guo was fortunately away at the slaughterhouse to collect payments and was spared. In addition to reporting to the military and police agencies to strictly pursue the escaped prisoners and providing detailed information for a subsequent report, I respectfully report. [Signed] Deng Ji'an."

As for the direction in which the escaped prisoners fled, the court stated that according to the investigation, they boarded a motorboat from Yuhangkou and sailed far out to sea. According to reports, two motorboats were moored at Dashizi on the 24th night, and their traces have since disappeared, suggesting that they had prepared the motorboats in advance to escape. The Water Police Bureau stated that the bureau only had three patrol boats. Boat No. 1 was borrowed by the Salt Transport Office for anti-smuggling purposes, and Boat No. 3 was abolished due to insufficient funding. Only Boat No. 2, He'an, had just been repaired and left the dock. At 10:00 AM that morning, they received a call from the headquarters stating that the Siming County Prison had been broken into, ordering them to patrol the sea to intercept the prisoners. However, as soon as they set sail, the propellers broke down. They had to hire another boat and sail to Yuhangkou Dashizi to patrol, but by then the prisoners had already escaped, and there was nothing unusual on the sea. As for the court's claim about the motorboats at Dashizi on the 24th night, after investigation, it was not confirmed. Before the prison break, there was a blue motorboat at Yuhangkou, which then sailed back to Haihoutan. According to investigations, it belonged to Sanchun Store, and the boat could only carry ten people. The court's claim that the rioters escaped by motorboat has not been definitively proven. However, the Xiamen sea area is extremely vast, and the water police only have one patrol boat. Even if there were one or two motorboats, it would be difficult to investigate them in advance. The headquarters ordered a heightened state of alert that evening due to the escaped rioters, ordering theaters to stop performances at 11:00 PM, closing all transport at 12:00 AM, at sea and on land. On the morning of the 26th, the water police strictly inspected all small boats going to inland areas in Zhangzhou and Quanzhou, but found nothing. The search is still underway. Meanwhile, the headquarters has dispatched a platoon of soldiers to be permanently stationed at the prison for defense. The injured Wu Guangcheng, the captain of the garrison team, and the three soldiers were immediately sent to the hospital for treatment. Wu died of his injuries at 11:00 PM that night. The names of the escaped suspected communists are listed below: Li Tingsheng, Chen Junchang, Wan Yaonan, Xie Keshao, Zhou Wenliang, Chen Hualong, Zeng Wenbin, Wu Siwen, Zhang Hanzhong, Chen Jianquan, Zhang Gengtao, Xie Lingling, Xu Zhibao, Shi Tianyi, Lin Longsheng, Xie Yangtang, Weng Dehai, Zhang Binggui, Yang Qihui, Huang Lingang. Among them, Zhang Gengtao and Zhang Hanzhong are Xiamen University students who were arrested on March 18 for distributing reactionary leaflets in Zhongshan Park. Hanzhong was sentenced to one year in prison. (27th)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Yinglong Temple Robbed by Bandits: Yinglong Temple Town in Punan, a small market town on the border of Songjiang and Fengxian, was suddenly raided by over twenty armed bandits at twelve o'clock on the night of the 27th of last month. Feigning the accent of traveling merchants, they guarded both ends of the market and dispersed to search and rob. In the Songjiang territory, Zhang Yuanfa's Nanhua store owner Zhang Junliang was beaten and tortured by the bandits, suffering severe injuries. Next, Cai Siqi's entire family of three houses was robbed. In the Fengxian territory, He Hengji's Nanhua store and residence, Jiang Quantai's Nanhua store, and others were robbed. After several hours, they fired their guns and left. After receiving a report from the township head Zhang Canran, the Fifteenth District Office has reported the situation to the county government for investigation.

Garrison Headquarters Orders Investigation of Suspected Criminals: The Fengjing Garrison Office received an order from the Garrison Headquarters to investigate and report on Mao Yunhua and Mao Yunyu of the Fourth and Sixth Tu for clarification and handling. The office immediately arrested the two men. According to their confessions, they were mistakenly identified as bandits and sent to the bureau on the night of February 23rd when they invited a midwife for his wife's delivery. They were released after being proven innocent. Someone then anonymously reported them to the Garrison Headquarters with false accusations. The office is currently conducting a thorough investigation.

Summary of Party and Government Talks: The county party and government talks were held yesterday at the county party headquarters. (A) Proposals from the County Government: (1) Regarding how to effectively comply with the promulgated regulations for inspecting postal items in various counties and cities, it was decided that the county party headquarters would copy the regulations and send them to the county government for joint implementation. (2) Regarding the Construction Bureau's order to prepare for a domestic goods market, it was decided: (1) to organize a preparatory committee for the county's domestic goods market, (2) to designate eleven groups, including the party headquarters, as committee members and hold the first meeting on the 9th, (3) to task the county party headquarters, the county government, and the Construction Bureau to draft the charter, and (4) to borrow the Yue Temple as the venue. (3) It was decided that the Public Security Bureau would inspect suspicious travelers on land and water, as well as postal and telecommunications items, and reactionary propaganda. (B) Proposals from the County Party Headquarters: (1) It was decided to hold a summer training session. The county party headquarters will copy the budget and send it to the county government to seek funding. (2) It was decided that Songjiang Hospital should add an obstetrics department to meet urgent needs. The opening costs will be borne by the hospital director, and the county will increase the monthly subsidy by fifty yuan. (C) Proposals from the Rectification Committee, Mi Guangguo: (1) The method for supplementing the accommodation and treatment of wounded and sick soldiers was named the "National Revolutionary Army Rear Wounded and Sick Soldiers Songjiang County Treatment Center Office." The organization is divided into three departments: general affairs, supervision, and medical affairs. An office will be set up for operations.

Qingpu

Property Division and Separation Case Reopened: Shen Xiuwu, a woman from this county, previously hired a lawyer to file a complaint with the county government, accusing her husband, Zhi Shangjiu, of abandonment and requesting a property division and separation. After a court hearing, the trial officer instructed both parties to invite the original introducers, Chen Qizhou and Yang Luchun, as well as relatives, to mediate properly. If an agreement could not be reached within half a month, the case would be retried. The original introducers and relatives made every effort to mediate, hoping for a settlement, but the opinions of both sides were too far apart to produce any results. The court reopened the case for trial yesterday.

Bandit Attempted Robbery Failed: The family of Yao Gouqi, a villager in the Yangjiaqiao area of Qingpu, is known as a well-to-do family. Bandits had coveted them for a long time, but were unable to succeed due to strict precautions. On the night before last, at about 11:00 PM, over a dozen bandits suddenly came, speaking with a Jiangbei accent, their faces painted black, and armed with guns and knives. They broke down the door and entered. At that time, Yao Gouqi and his son, having heard the loud noise, knew that something was wrong and secretly slipped out the back. While the bandits were rummaging through boxes and cabinets, suddenly, shouts of "Catch the thieves!" rang out from nearby and continued to grow louder. The bandits knew that things were not good and dared not carry out their robbery. They abandoned their loot and fled eastward. After a careful inspection, there were no losses.

Yangzhou

Arrest of a Fugitive with a Large Amount of Embezzled Funds: Sun Zigeng and Hu Yukun, accountants at the Yi'an Supervision Bureau in Bengbu, were found to have embezzled four thousand yuan and fled to Yangzhou, hiding at No. 12 Denglong Lane. A special letter was sent to the Jiangdu County Government requesting their arrest. Now, Sun Zigeng, having heard the news, feared punishment and secretly returned to his private residence on the Yangzi Bridge, where he committed suicide by poisoning. Yesterday (the 31st), the county detectives Tang Jinrong and others, along with Inspector Rao of the First Branch, led police officers to the address and arrested Hu Yukun and a suspect surnamed Xia at No. 12 Denglong Lane. They were taken to the First Branch for preliminary interrogation for further investigation.

The Situation of the Old Dragon Boat Festival in Yangzhou: Today (the 1st) is the old Dragon Boat Festival. The Chamber of Commerce and the Commercial Rectification Association complied with the government's order to reform bad habits and abolish the Dragon Boat Festival closure, and specially notified the shops in advance not to close at noon. However, small shops in remote areas still inevitably showed signs of closing their doors. Private industries have also stopped work. All agencies and schools, etc., are closed as usual due to the weekend, which is not a problem. All accounts will also be closed once, it is said.

Local Correspondence Two

Suzhou

Minor Uproar at the Third Branch Prison Again: The Jiangsu Third Branch Prison on Siqian Street has experienced two prison riots in November of last year and March of this year. The ringleaders, including Jiang Yingcheng, have been sent to the Wuxian District Court for trial and sentenced to additional imprisonment. However, Jiang continued in his wickedness, refusing to repent. On the night before last, he suddenly started a fight on purpose. When a guard tried to stop him, Jiang refused to obey and put the chamber pot prepared in the cell over the guard's head. The guard, seeing that Jiang was beyond reason, took him out and handcuffed him. Jiang continued to curse endlessly. Later, Section Chief Yu of the prison reprimanded and stopped him.

Bandits Plunder Zhouzhuang: After the Taihu gang of bandits were repeatedly suppressed and defeated by the naval and land military police, they slightly disappeared. Yesterday (the 2nd), suddenly, about two hundred bandits from the Henan and Haizhou gangs joined forces in Zhejiang and moved to Zhouzhuang, Jinze, and other places along the Taihu Lake, intending to cause trouble. After being informed by the spies, Gong Guoliang, the district chief of the Third District of the Suzhou Water Public Security Bureau, immediately ordered Captain Xu Boying of the Eleventh Team to lead the team to suppress the bandits and sent four guerrilla ships, towed by the Zhenwei patrol boat, to set off and join the Eleventh Team in pursuit.

Zhong Shicai Has Hope of Recovery: Zhong Shicai, an investigator from the Central Party Headquarters, committed suicide by taking tranquilizer pills at the Wujun Hostel outside Changmen on May 30th. Pu Yiyun, the hotel's bookkeeper, discovered him and sent him to Suyong Hospital on Guangji Bridge for treatment. He has already recovered and is no longer in danger. However, Zhong has been suffering from mental illness and is currently recuperating quietly in the hospital. The Wujun Hostel has sent letters to Ye Xiufeng, a member of the Jiangsu Provincial Party Committee, and Li Fu, the younger brother of Chen Guofu, a member of the Central Committee, requesting them to send someone to Suzhou to take Zhong back to avoid staying in a foreign land.

Wounded Soldiers Come to Suzhou for Treatment: The General Headquarters sent military escorts to wounded soldiers from Nanjing to Suzhou yesterday (the 2nd). They arrived at the station at about 1:00 PM in the afternoon. The Yongcheng steamboat, pre-hired by the county government, towed 35 civilian boats to transport the wounded soldiers to the old site of the Fengqiao Fort Camp for resettlement. The General Headquarters sent personnel to Suzhou to prepare for the establishment of the Seventeenth Rear Hospital and set up an office in the Ai Zi room of the Suzhou Hotel.

Wuxi

A Robbery Occurs in Kaiyuan Township: Residents of Dongguanshe Mountain in Kaiyuan Township (Fourth District) of the county, Feng Peifang, were suddenly visited around 1 a.m. the previous morning by eight or nine robbers dressed in short clothes and white headscarves. Speaking in a Jiangbei accent, they carried flashlights, wooden sticks, and other tools, scaled the wall, entered, and ransacked the place for an hour before fleeing with their loot. After inspection, it was found that they had stolen 65 silver dollars, clothes, jewelry, beads, and other items, worth over 1,000 dollars.

Important News about the Establishment of Electrical Enterprises: According to recent news from the National Government Construction Committee in the capital, the committee has decided to use Boxer Indemnity funds to expand the scope of electrical enterprise development. A large-scale power plant will be established in Jiangyin, and fully connected to the Qishuyan Power Plant to transmit electricity to Wujin and Wuxi counties. At the same time, the electricity from the Jiangyin Power Plant will be used to establish tram systems in the five counties of Wuxi, Changshu, Yixing, Wujin, and Jiangyin to facilitate transportation. The first agricultural irrigation area in Wuxi and Wujin counties will be expanded to include the five counties of Wuxi, Changshu, Yuyao, and Chengjiang, and the situation will be considered to continue forming the second and third agricultural irrigation area committees in Wujiang, Wuxian, and other places to promote the project.

Attempted Suicide Due to Unsuccessful Debt Collection: Xie E, a 24-year-old resident of Taibo City, Daqiangmen in this county, currently residing at No. 11 Gaosi Lane, Suzhou, was previously an employee at Hengtaiyuan Silk Shop on Guanqian Street in Suzhou. Recently, as the end-of-May settlement period approached, Xie urged a friend to collect debts owed to him for transactions he had handled. Unexpectedly, the friend was raising funds to go to his hometown. Xie believed that the friend was making excuses to avoid paying the debts, and that he would inevitably be unable to collect them. In desperation, he conceived the idea of ​​ending his life. So, the afternoon before yesterday, he came to Wuxi from Suzhou and stayed in room 50 of Qitai Inn on Tongyun Road outside Guangfu Gate, claiming to be named Shi Dele, a homophone for "happy to die." That night, Xie wrote two suicide notes in advance, one to Wanxingchang Grocery Store outside the Suspension Bridge, and the other to Zou Qingyuan. One note was left with the inn's accounting department, stating that he had come to their establishment to make it his final resting place, and asked them not to request a court inspection, etc. Later, he went to the Sino-British Pharmacy outside the North Gate of this county, purchased a bottle of "Baoshui Kerona calming water," and returned to the inn, drinking it all. Around 10 a.m. yesterday morning, the inn's tea boy saw that Shi had not yet gotten up, and became suspicious. He knocked on the door, but there was no response. He peeked through the window and saw Shi lying stiffly on the bed, with a strange expression. He quickly broke the window and entered, finding an empty bottle of calming medicine and two letters on the table, realizing that he had taken poison. He immediately reported to the accounting department, who carried Shi to Tongren Hospital for treatment. At the same time, Shi's letter to Zou Qingyuan in Suzhou was sent by express mail. After Shi was sent to the hospital, the hospital's doctors tried their best to rescue him, and fortunately, he soon woke up, and his spirits gradually recovered. In the evening, Zou Qingyuan and Xie's cousin came to Wuxi to visit him at Tongren Hospital. Today (the 2nd), they will accompany Xie back to Suzhou for recuperation.

A Strange Tale of Triplets: Dong Wangqing, a resident of Yuelou Lane, Gedi Bridge, Kaihua Township in this county, has been working as a geomancer and his family is relatively well-off. His wife, Mrs. Mou, is nearly forty years old and has a ten-year-old daughter. Last year, Mrs. Mou became pregnant again, and her abdomen gradually expanded. Until around 7 a.m. the day before yesterday (the 1st), she felt labor pains and knew she was about to give birth. Dong Wangqing hired a midwife to come to his home to assist with the delivery. Soon, she gave birth to a boy. Unexpectedly, the abdominal pain continued, and successively gave birth to two girls. Dong's wife, Mrs. Mou, due to excessive childbirth, was unable to sustain her energy, and died of exhaustion at the time, but the three children were all well. After hearing the news, the villagers in the area went to see, and were amazed. Yesterday, Dong Wangqing had already prepared a coffin for his wife and buried her. At the same time, he hired a wet nurse to come to his home to breastfeed and raise the three children.

A Record of the Trial of a Boat with Four Lives: Xu Jianshan, a resident of Xu Lane, Nianjiushi Tu, Kaihua Township, Fourteenth District, hired a boat to transport goods on the 19th of last month from Renzi Port to Luzhu in Xishan, Dongting. The boat was robbed on Taihu Lake, and Xu Jianshan and the boatman Shao Qiaosheng and his son were killed. The boat has now been found by the Rescue Bureau, and the body of Shao Qiaosheng has also been recovered, all of which have been reported to the county government for verification. And the corpse brother Xu Mingqi, induced the suspect Wang Jie, reported the police to untie the county to take the confession. Yesterday, the hearing was held by the trial officer. According to Wang Jie's confession, he is from Lujiang, Anhui, and has served in the water police and the army. In the first month of this year, he came to Wuxi with his family and stayed in the upstairs room of the Gu family in Dalou Lane. The landlord, Mrs. Gu Yang, is my adoptive mother. A few days ago, he went to Nanfangquan to collect 80 yuan from a teahouse for Mrs. Gu. He went with Zhang Mengxi. 23 yuan has been received for this money. Regarding the case of Xu Jianshan and others being robbed, he firmly claimed that he did not know and recounted that he was in a certain place on a certain day, and that doctor Gu Zijing and young master Sun could testify. Yu Jun, according to the confession, ordered him to be remanded in custody, pending the summoning of Gu and Sun to the case for verification.

Jiangyin

Utilizing the Yarn Factory to Temporarily Resume Work: The male and female workers of the Liyong Yarn Factory demanded an increase in rice subsidies. The county reorganization committee member, Zhong Jianhui, mediated and the workers proposed twelve conditions to be resolved. Because of the signing by the aide-de-camp Zhu Danqing on behalf of the manager Wang Yiyun, the next day, Wang expressed his opposition, saying that the conditions must be approved by the board of directors, resulting in the failure to start work. The workers marched and held meetings. It happened to be the May 30th Martial Law, and reactionary slogans were found at the same time. Li County Magistrate led the military police to conduct a major search. Because the representative Ren Ruisheng and others were suspected of committing crimes, they were detained, and will be released after the resumption of work. Yesterday (the 1st), Wu Yiyun and others met with Li County Magistrate. Li persuaded them to start work quickly to maintain the livelihoods of the workers. Wu Yu’er temporarily agreed to resume work on the 2nd. However, regarding the conditions, because the representatives were detained, they were suspected of being reactionary. Since they have been returned to the judiciary, they should be negotiated after a resolution is reached. After writing to the county party department, the party department rejected the reply, saying that there was no reason. Since the conditions had been signed by Zhu Danqing, they should be accepted immediately. Therefore, although Liyong was able to start work, the conditions regarding rice subsidies have not been resolved. Last night, the Propaganda Department of the Central Party Department was showing the film of the Prime Minister's burial on the Nanjin parade ground. Suddenly, a large number of red reactionary leaflets appeared, with absurd words such as helping the Liyong workers' strike. The on-site business group immediately searched, but did not find the person who issued the leaflets.

Famous Opera Singer Mr. Jiang Junjia Arrives in Cheng: The County Party Department and all sectors of society are raising funds to rebuild Zhongshan Park. They have specially invited the famous opera singer Jiang Junjia from Wujin and the Bin She opera troupe to come to Cheng for a performance. Mr. Jiang has agreed to sing for three days. However, Chen Daoan, the master of the Huqin, did not agree to come to Cheng, and was replaced by his son Xiaocun.

Jiashan

Being Abducted for Collecting Accounts for a Pawnshop: Dongfangjia Pawnshop in Xitang Beitang has been doing well in recent years. During this Dragon Boat Festival, there were many accounts in the surrounding villages. Therefore, they sent Xiao Fang, the manager, and Lu Gengshu, a partner, to collect them together. Unexpectedly, they have not returned. They have been searching everywhere, but there is no news of them. Recently, they received a message from the bandits, demanding 15,000 yuan before they would allow them to be redeemed. They are currently trying to rescue them.

Two Bandits Captured: The water police of the 7th team of Ganyao obtained confessions from previously captured bandits regarding their accomplices. They then arrested two bandits, surnamed Xu and Zhang, at their addresses. Their confessions were evasive. It is heard that these two bandits are respected figures in the local area. The remaining bandits are still being hunted.

Organizing a Reception Center for Wounded Soldiers: The county magistrate of this county received a telegram from the province, informing them that a large number of wounded soldiers, about a thousand, would be coming to Shan for recuperation. Therefore, at 1 p.m. on the 1st, he convened an emergency meeting of the heads of various agencies and local gentry. It was decided at the meeting that the county would allocate 5,000 yuan specifically for the provision of wounded soldiers, and a reception center would be established as a single authority. Xin'an Guild Hall and other places have been designated as residences for the wounded soldiers.

Jiaxing

A Compilation of Robberies Occurring in the County: At the home of Lu Yongfa in Namingyang Village, Tanghui District, Jiaxing, more than a dozen robbers suddenly arrived around midnight the day before yesterday. Speaking in mixed accents and holding iron rulers and wooden sticks, they broke down the door and entered, overturning boxes and looting at will. They robbed nine shi of rice and one shi of rapeseed, along with clothes and ornaments, and tied up Lu Yongfa, beating him severely with weapons, causing him to be covered in injuries. The robbers then went to the home of Yu Sanfu next door to search and rob, taking clothes and stones of rice. Later, the robbers went to the homes of Wu Zhanglin and Wu Shenggao in Taoshazha Village, Wuqiao Village, and robbed them separately, with considerable losses. The next day, the victims reported to the local public security bureau for investigation. Also, the home of Ni Changsheng in Qianwei Village, Hantang District, was also visited by many robbers last night, who robbed at will. On the same day, Fang's family, a large family in Chenjiaqiao, was also broken into by robbers, who stole many ornaments.

Sports

Detailed Record of the 9th Far Eastern Games (4)

Japanese Referee Policy

The Shamelessness and Unreasonableness of Referees

(From Qu, Tokyo)

The Japanese have dead effort but no living talent in sports. They are quite good at track and field events that require long-term training. However, they simply have natural deficiencies in basketball, volleyball, and football. At this Far Eastern Games, our country's volleyball strength far surpasses that of Japan. However, Japan came up with a fanciful idea to implement its "referee policy" to make up for its shortcomings. What is "referee policy?" This is a term unique to the Japanese. Please refer to the following facts for an explanation.

During the China-Japan basketball game, the Japan Sports Association invited an obscure elementary school physical education teacher from a remote county to be the referee. During the refereeing, he seemed to be instructed by others and temporarily formulated a novel basketball rule: whenever a Chinese team member dribbled the ball and came into contact with a Japanese team member, the Chinese team member would be penalized for a foul, with arbitrary penalties of one or two points. This went on for 40 minutes, and Japan "turned defeat into victory."

On the third day of the Far Eastern Games (the 26th), at 3 p.m., the China-Japan volleyball game was held. Japan thought that the "referee policy" in Hong Kong had been effective, so today they intensified their efforts. They invited a Mr. Yuan, named Liulang, to be the referee. He was about 50 years old, extremely crude, and based on his general knowledge, it seemed that he had not completed middle school. During the refereeing, he specialized in being shameless and unreasonable. When the Japanese team served, and our team counterattacked, every time the ball was touched, it was pointed out as touching the net (Touchnet) or as a held ball (Hoesie). When our team scored a point on a serve, it was pointed out as a foul and canceled. There were more prohibitions than hairs on an ox, but Japan never committed a single one. This happened dozens of times, and the audience was in an uproar. Even the slightly knowledgeable Japanese could not stand it. The reporter's neighbor was a Japanese news reporter group. Every time Yuan Liulang was shameless, they would scold him, saying, "This is too outrageous!" But Yuan Liulang remained stubborn and cunning. Our athletes repeatedly questioned him, but he was stiff and did not know how to answer. Fortunately, our country's volleyball coaches Zhao Shanwei and Liu Quanda persuaded them, saying that the competition was related to the honor of the country. Since he was being shameless and unreasonable, he was only tarnishing the reputation of his country. We should be patient and dignified. Mr. Brown, the West Secretary of the Tokyo Youth Association of Japan, was also present. He said to people, "Japan could have won this Games, and we deeply congratulate them. But with this referee, Japan's reputation has been swept away. This is why the American immigration law has a 'gentleman's agreement.'" This atmosphere of dissatisfaction with the referee has permeated the entire stadium. Later, a sensible Japanese gentleman took the opportunity to privately give Yuan Liulang a hint. Yuan Liulang was guilty of faking and knew that he was wrong, so his momentum was slightly restrained. In the second and third sets, our team won a great victory over Japan by 21 to 8. Japan's weakness can be proven by this. If it were not for Yuan Liulang's injustice, purely comparing skills, Japan would not have avoided a "zero defeat," because if it were as Yuan Liulang did, the victory or defeat of the competition would not be determined by the superiority of the athletes, but only by a referee. After the competition, the reporter asked Mr. Yanagida Toru, an official of the meeting for an inquiry into the origins and experiences of Yuan Liulang, asking "Where did Yuan Liulang come from?" Mr. Yanagida reluctantly and slowly replied, "He is not from Tokyo. You have already won, forget about it." The reporter said, "I admire Yuan Liulang very much as a person, because he is very patriotic." Mr. Yanagida smiled bitterly and did not answer. "Patriotism" must first "care about face," and "losing face" is "humiliating the country." Yuan Liulang is simply "losing face" and "humiliating the country." I pity Japan, I am ashamed for Japan.

Tokyo is the capital of Japan, with a flourishing talent pool and a more open atmosphere, but the referee for volleyball must be sought from Yuan Liulang, a remote village. The Japan Sports Association must have another intention. I cannot name it, I respectfully name it the "Japanese Referee Policy."

In the past, when one side was dissatisfied with the other side's referee, it always contained elements of misunderstanding and resentment. This article was written on the spot because I was very angry at the time, and there are many biased emotional words. It also seems to have a "non-gentlemanly" tendency. I have made some deletions later, but the ugliness of the Japanese referee policy has not been fully revealed, so I dare to take responsibility for the text.

The First China-Philippines Women's Volleyball Match

(Xu Minhui from Tokyo)

Result: China wins two to zero

China's spiking is very good

But they don't know the weaknesses of the attacker

The first women's volleyball exhibition match between China and the Philippines was held at 1 p.m. on the 24th at the Meiji Jingu Gaien Volleyball Court. In this match, China and the Philippines fought each other. As soon as the weapons were launched, the Chinese women's army was exceptionally brave. Captain Deng Zhihao's serves were fierce, and the Filipina generals only had the skill to parry, but no strength to return fire. The Chinese generals spiked hard, the forwards were smooth, and the coordination was quite skilled. Going smoothly, they immediately scored five to zero. Unfortunately, Deng was careless for a moment and made two mistakes, sending the ball to the other side. Fortunately, the generals bravely regained the serve, and Li Cuimei took over. Her serves were no less fierce than Deng's, so she also scored five straight, with the score being ten to zero. The ball was then taken away by the Filipina women. Not long after, it was taken back again. Lü served, and her momentum was not weak. After getting one point, they had to change sides. Seeing that the situation was not good, the enemy team stood up and fought hard, winning one point. After several fierce battles, they gained some victories. However, they had lost too much in the first half, and the general trend was gone, so the Chinese team won with a score of 21 to 8. After a minute of ceasefire, they continued with the

Second set: After winning the first set, the Chinese team became arrogant and scattered, and the formation was in chaos. The Philippine team took advantage of this, leading to a score of eight to four, and eleven to seven. The Philippine Islands had the upper hand. The team was panicked and did not know what to do. The score increased to thirteen to eight. The bystanders were worried about them. Fortunately, the captain was alert and announced a ceasefire. On the one hand, it could reduce the enemy's morale, and on the other hand, it could discuss tactics and change methods, and reorganize the team. So they regained their vitality. Situ Wei made the first extraordinary contribution, winning three points in a row. Xiao Huiling continued her efforts and scored five points in a row, taking the lead with sixteen to thirteen. The morale was even more invigorated. Overseas Chinese gave help and often shouted to cheer them on. Although the Philippine team resisted desperately, it was ultimately ineffective. The result was 21 to 17, and our team won.

In this match, our team's spiking was very good, and the setting was also quite appropriate. However, it was slightly inaccurate and did not know the weaknesses of the enemy. Moreover, the defense was slightly poor, and there were often improper serves, and there were often two failures, sending the ball to the other side. These are all the weaknesses of our team. In addition, they are contemptuous of the enemy when they win, and panicked when they lose. If they do not remove these weaknesses in the future when competing with us, the enemy's Japanese team, they may fail because of this. May you all be diligent! (Evening of May 24th)

The Second Day of the Track and Field Competition

Japan Wins the Championship with 131.5 Points

Our Country Gets Fourth in the Triple Jump, with Only One Point

The second day of the track and field competition was the day for the finals of each event (i.e., May 25). The audience was even more crowded than the first day. There was almost no room to stand in a large square. There were at least about 100,000 people. The competition started at 0:20 p.m. Our country only got the most precious one point in the final triple jump, with Mr. Situ Guang jumping fourth. This is better than the zero points in the first competition. However, the Japanese said that Nanbu Chuhei gave up the competition and let China get one point for the sake of appearances. The mockery can be said to be extreme. The second day of the competition is described below.

(1) 100-Meter Final

The 100-meter final has always been won by the Philippine army. This time, Japan's Yoshioka actually surpassed the Philippine army's Long Gong Shige and won the championship. This is truly a groundbreaking achievement for Japan. Gong Shige started the race too slowly. By the 50-meter mark, he had already overtaken Yoshioka. In the end, Yoshioka chased him down, about one meter apart. The result was 10.8 seconds. If our country's Liu Changchun had not injured his Achilles tendon, it would have been an easy matter to win first place. Third place went to Japan's Nambu, and fourth place went to the Philippines' Pinipa Heiersi.

First Japan-Philippines Baseball Game

(Qian Hua)

10 to 4, Japan Wins

Tokyo Dispatch: The first baseball game between Japan and the Philippines was held at the baseball field on the afternoon of the 25th at 2:30 PM. Because it was a Sunday, the weather was clear and sunny. Seeing their national team play, a crowd of Japanese spectators gathered, and tickets were sold out. There was almost no standing room in the field, making it an unprecedented spectacle since the Waseda-Keio baseball games. The umpire was Ikeda, and the base umpires were Miyake, Tenchi, and Fujita. The Philippine team batted first.

Score: Japan 28000000X 10

Philippines 000102010 4

In the first three innings, the Philippine team struggled to make progress against pitcher Miyatake's varied ball speed, which was difficult to read. When the Japanese team began their offense, they scored two points. By the second inning, they were doing as they pleased, hitting the ball at will, and scoring five consecutive points. The difference in strength and skill was vast. At this time, dark clouds filled the sky, and soon it rained heavily. The game was declared suspended. After ten minutes, the rain stopped and play resumed. The Philippine team changed pitchers, but still couldn't stop the Japanese offensive. The Japanese frequently loaded the bases, creating many dangerous situations. In this inning, Japan scored eight points, sealing the victory early. Afterwards, Miyatake's pitch lost some power due to conserved energy, so the Philippine team seized the opportunity to counterattack. The top five batters all got hits, successively scoring four points in the fourth, sixth, and eighth innings. In the end, Japan won a great victory with a score of 10 to 4.
