Anecdotes from the Games

Unexpectedly Similar Cheers: The Chinese cheering squad at the basketball court would erupt in cheers or slogans whenever a player entered the field or scored points. When playing against the Philippines, the Philippine team would also cheer in response. The Chinese team came up with a new trick, temporarily setting numbers like "1234554321" to music and singing it, while the Philippine team wouldn't be outdone, repeatedly singing "AB." Thus, "A" "B" "AAA" "BBB" "BA" "AB" "BBBBBB" left the audience in stitches.

Unable to Stop the Tears: Two girls' schools performed basketball at the venue, and one won while the other lost. The losing team was extremely sad and indignant. After leaving the field, they sat together on the grass, facing each other and weeping. Also, during a performance by two other girls' schools, a girl was hit in the chest and cried loudly. This was perhaps also a kind of embellishment.

China-Japan Table Tennis Match

Japan Wins in Both Team and Individual Events

Chinese Performance is Excellent

China Wins in Numazu

(Tokyo Dispatch) The table tennis team arrived in Tokyo on the 24th. Individual matches were held on the 25th, and team matches were held on the 26th. The opening ceremony began with a report by Kido, followed by speeches by Count Arima. At ten o'clock, the referee, Ginka, blew the whistle, and applause thundered. After five hours of fierce competition, the individual championship was won by Murabayashi of the Japanese team. The team competition was divided into five groups. The results and skills are detailed below.

Chinese Team Japanese Team Result

(2) Lu Zhongqiu Morita 3 to 0

Chen Jiaqiu, Right Winger, Passes the Ball to Dai Linjing in the China Victory Soccer Match

Zhou Jianwen unfortunately encountered Murabayashi, the individual champion. Murabayashi is the essence of all of Japan, good at both attacking and defending. In the individual final against Fukushi, he drew the ball forty-six times in a row, and Fukushi actually returned it, resulting in victory over Fukushi, showing his superb skill. Zhou's defeat was therefore inevitable. Lu Zhongqiu versus Morita, Morita is the Osaka individual champion, good at both drawing and hitting. He has defeated thousands of strong players in Osaka. Now, Lu surprisingly beat him with a drawn ball, setting a new record for Chinese table tennis. Huang Xiangfa versus Aizawa, although Huang Xiangfa lost, his performance still lived up to the name of a veteran. Lu Xiuli versus Fukushi, because Fukushi's skill was excellent, although Lu tried his best to draw the ball, there was no gap to enter. Lu Shentong versus Fujimura, Lu has always been good at close returns, and in the eyes of the Chinese, he was sure to win against the Japanese. Unexpectedly, he was completely out of form that day, returning the ball too high and losing more balls. The opponent's drawing and defending were effective, leading to defeat. Overall, in this match, if the Chinese team had made proper predictions and placed their strongest players at the back, the result would have been better. The Chinese are known for their defensive play, but they did a lot of drawing today, which surprised the Japanese. Japan was completely defensive, waiting for an opportunity, and the Chinese team was exhausted from the long journey, not sleeping all night on the train. They had only one day of rest before having to fight, so their defeat was not a sin of war. The battle of Numazu can prove this. After the competition on the 26th, Count Arima, chairman of the Japanese Table Tennis Association, held a get-together. The Japanese team mostly expressed their friendly intentions. Lin Zecang and Yu Binqi of the Chinese team also expressed the magnanimity of the Chinese people. They didn't say goodbye until sunset.

Closing Stages of Elementary School Volleyball Group B

Xicheng Wins 2 to 0 Against Shihua

Yesterday at 4:30 PM, the final act of the Group B round-robin tournament of the municipal elementary school volleyball competition was held at the Municipal No. 1 Public Sports Field. The participants were the Xicheng and Shihua teams. Although the championship of that group had already belonged to the invincible Tangwan, both sides still arrived on time and fought bravely. New Work in the Scientific Community

Summer Marine Biology Research Conference Scheduled to Open

Co-organized by Xiamen University and the China Foundation for the Promotion of Education and Culture

As a Prelude to Building a Marine Biology Museum in China

(Xiamen Dispatch) Xiamen University and the Board of Directors of the China Foundation for the Promotion of Education and Culture, in order to further advance the progress of Chinese biological science in recent years, have specially organized a "Summer Marine Biology Research Conference" this year. The China Foundation for the Promotion of Education and Culture is responsible for providing funds of 5,000 yuan, and Xiamen University is responsible for preparation and providing research institutes and all work equipment. The conference has invited well-known biology experts from various universities in the country to participate in the research work. Those who have responded include professors of biology from Guangdong Zhongshan University, Lingnan University, Northeastern University, Yenching University, Peking Union Medical College, Jinling University, Ginling Women's College, Soochow University, Shanghai University, St. John's University, Guanghua University, Zhijiang University, and Fuzhou Union University, totaling about twenty-five people. The conference is scheduled to open on July 14th. It is said that the important mission of the conference is, first, to seek progress in biological science from an organizational perspective, and also to plan the establishment of a marine biology museum in China. Recently, biological science has unanimously recognized the maxim of "studying living things, not reading dead books." European and American countries are competing to establish marine biology museums, and Japan already has two. Only our country lacks them, which is truly a great regret for the biological science community. However, establishing a marine biology museum requires two conditions: a building near the sea and abundant marine products. In our country's coastal areas, from Beigudao in the north to the south, along Yantai, Qingdao, Zhoushan, Shantou to Guangzhou, some areas have abundant marine products but no buildings, while others have buildings but are not near the sea. It is impossible to establish a marine biology museum at once. Only Xiamen University has magnificent buildings and is located right by the sea, and the abundance of marine products in the surrounding area surpasses all other places. This is truly the most suitable and easy place to build a marine biology museum in China. This year, the experts participating in the research conference are all shouldering this important responsibility, and after a month of discussion and planning,

Situation at the Start of the 10,000 Meter Final

It is bound to lead to some clues. Therefore, this research conference can also be said to be a prelude to the Chinese Marine Biology Museum. Xiamen Port has very rich marine products such as sea urchins, starfish, marine protozoa, and fish. The production of lancelets (Amphioxus) in Liuwudian is the highest in the world, so the area can provide everything needed for biological research. The address of the School of Biological Science of Xiamen University is on a small hill in the southeast corner of the school, next to the Zhenhai Customs built by Zheng Chenggong at the end of the Ming Dynasty. The building has three floors. The first floor is the animal room, the second floor is the plant room, and the third floor is the office. This year's research conference will temporarily use the first floor as a laboratory, with three large laboratories and six small laboratories, with flowing seawater to facilitate the study of living marine animals. It is also said that all travel expenses and accommodation costs for the experts participating in the conference will be provided by the conference. In addition to discussing the organization and establishment of the biological museum this year, each person will choose their own research topic without a fixed curriculum. When the second conference is held next year, various research classes can be opened, such as protozoa, marine animals, general physiology, embryology, etc., one or two classes, so that high school teachers, university teaching assistants, and advanced students can all participate, etc.

Jiangsu Slaughter Tax Temporarily Postponed

The Jiangsu slaughter tax is designated as a special fund for education in Jiangsu Province, which was not originally a problem. Since the division of municipalities and counties, the two special municipalities of Nanjing and Shanghai have considered the tax revenue within the city limits to be city-owned, and have therefore strongly argued for the tax to belong to the city. However, provincial schools are located in urban areas, and the dispute over the tax has led to the desire to transfer all provincial schools and educational institutions in urban areas to the city. This matter has been disputed by the province and the city for a long time and has not been resolved. Now it is heard that the central government has decided to maintain the original plan, and the slaughter tax will not be changed for the time being, and will still be used as a special fund for provincial education. The city will also temporarily postpone the takeover of provincial educational institutions in urban areas. The name of the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office will also not be changed. However, it is heard that the education directors of the two special municipalities of Nanjing and Shanghai will join the Jiangsu Education Funding Committee as new members.

Ministry of Education Drafts Agricultural, Industrial, and Commercial Curricula

The Curriculum Standards Drafting Committee for Primary and Secondary Schools convened by the Ministry of Education has already finalized and printed the general curriculum. However, the various vocational subjects have not yet been completed. It is now heard that the courses for the various industrial groups are being drafted. The draft courses for the commercial subjects have been completely submitted by the drafting committee members, and the Ministry of Education will hold a review meeting in about a week or so, which can be approved and announced. The agricultural courses were previously presided over by Mr. Qian Tianhe, who hired various members to draft them separately. They are divided into groups such as "Agriculture," "Animal Husbandry," "Sericulture," and "Forestry." Except for the animal husbandry group, which has not yet completed the draft, most of the others are roughly ready. Recently, the Ministry of Education sent a letter urging the drafting committee members to send the drafted courses to the ministry as soon as possible, so that they can be grouped and hold meetings to complete them as soon as possible.

School directors who attended included Mr. Zhang Zhongren, Pan Ziqi, Song Youpei, Jin Ji, Yu Yang, and Wei Yu. The meeting began at 10:00 AM. Mr. Maguelre Gave a Speech at Labor University Yesterday

Yesterday, the National Labor University invited Dr. Maguelre of France to give a speech. The doctor came to the school with Ding Zhaoqing and Zhu Shaoping at 9:00 AM. The speech began at 10:00 AM, entitled "China in Europe." Secretary-General Xiong of the school first expressed his welcome, and then Dr. Ma took the stage to give his speech. The gist of it was that Chinese culture has had a profound and significant impact on Europe. In ancient times, due to transportation difficulties, the impact was not very obvious. However, since the 18th century, a major change has occurred in European society, and external culture is needed for adjustment. Therefore, the cultural essence of China, such as politics, philosophy, literature, and art, was transmitted to Europe and was very popular. In various aspects of modern European culture, Chinese colors are deeply dyed and become more and more obvious. After Mr. Ma finished speaking, Dr. Xia Zhaoqing continued to give a speech, saying that the school's labor education was very successful and admirable. Dr. Ma is only 28 years old, but his knowledge is profound and he is a model for the students of the school. He hoped that the young people would work hard.

Important News from Jinan University

Since National Jinan University implemented the college-based administrative system, the departments have been thriving. The president's office receives dozens of letters from various places at home and abroad every day inquiring about the enrollment date or requesting regulations. It is heard that due to the limitations of school buildings and funding, the 19th-year enrollment plan has been discussed and decided at the 13th school affairs meeting. (1) Each department is limited to ten students. (2) Each department generally does not recruit transfer students. (3) The middle school department does not accept domestic students except for the children of faculty and staff. (4) Female students are limited to overseas Chinese students and the daughters of faculty and staff. (5) The appropriate time limit for overseas Chinese students to return to China for examinations will be notified to various overseas departments by the Ministry of Culture. The school, due to special circumstances, did not enroll students last year except for the law department. If there are outstanding young people in the country this year who are interested in applying to the university department, they can prepare their homework early for the examination. It is good that the opportunity for the school to enroll students is not easy and should not be missed. In addition, in the recent three years, political science, economics, law, diplomacy, and other specialized subjects have been established in order. The law school has been enriched, and it has also been decided to restore it based on the facts. Due to insufficient housing, it will be temporarily moved to Shanghai for operation. When the new house is completed, it will be moved back to the Zhenru headquarters. Also, according to the decision of the Nanyang Overseas Chinese Education Conference to dispatch Nanyang Overseas Chinese Education Inspection Commissioners, it has also been decided to temporarily dispatch seven people in the 19th year, one each from the five colleges of arts, science, education, commerce, and law, and the middle school department, and the Ministry of Culture, to depart after the autumn semester for a period of three months in October, November, and December. Each member will receive a subsidy of 2,000 yuan. After the inspection, they must make a comprehensive improvement plan for the school in order to express the special spirit of overseas Chinese schools. It is expected that the future of overseas Chinese education will show a different color.

Shanghai Middle School, in order to utilize the summer vacation period to promote education and supplement studies, has a summer school as usual, which has been very successful for two sessions. Minister of Communications Wang Boqun personally visited the Wusong Merchant Marine School at 8:00 AM yesterday. As a result, the country's industry and commerce are difficult to have long-term development. Therefore, the establishment of the merchant marine school is to cultivate talent for the shipping industry, and to study the shipping industry is to do its best for the party and the country.

Local News

Today's June 3rd Memorial

Time... 9:00 AM

Location... Business Readjustment Association

The June 3rd Opium Prohibition Memorial, jointly prepared by the Shanghai Special City Party Department, the Special City Government, and the Chinese National Anti-Narcotics Association, is ready. Yesterday, various levels of Party, government, and organizational bodies in the city held memorial week activities, adding anti-drug speeches and oaths, which were very enthusiastic. Today at 9:00 AM, a memorial meeting will be held at the auditorium of the Business Readjustment Association at Tianhougong Bridge in the city. Each level of the Party, administrative organs, and organizations should send five representatives to participate. A special memorial issue will be published in major newspapers today for publicity. This afternoon, Mrs. Cai Gengshi will give a speech on the radio, with Ms. Bai Zhiying as the chairwoman. The following is a summary of what we have gathered:

Propaganda Outline: The meaning and origin of the June 3rd Memorial. The import of opium into our country was the beginning of imperialist economic aggression. From the Daoguang three years (1823) to eighteen years (1838) of the former Qing Dynasty, the silver lost due to opium exports increased from 17 million taels to 30 million taels annually. At the same time, the entire nation, addicted to opium, was mostly emaciated and haggard, facing the danger of national destruction. At that time, Mr. Lin Zexu handled the opium prohibition, confiscating 20,283 chests of opium from British merchants and destroying them all at Humen, to the joy of the whole country. Today marks the 91st anniversary. Mr. Lin's destruction of opium was to demonstrate the justice of our nation and the fairness of the world, making him the vanguard of China's anti-drug movement. His great spirit is worthy of commemoration. However, due to the destruction, the Opium War was triggered, leading to military defeat and national humiliation, with justice not upheld and fairness not realized. Until now, imperialist aggression has become increasingly severe, and the harm of opium has not been completely eradicated. If we hope to implement opium prohibition, fundamentally eliminate the scourge of opium, and overthrow all imperialist aggression, then it is especially worthwhile to commemorate the fundamental starting date of the Opium War, "June 3rd." The June 3rd Memorial was proposed to the National Government by Dr. Wang Jingqi, the current chairman of the Chinese National Anti-Narcotics Association, who is fighting against drugs in overseas international alliances. The National Government also issued a nationwide unified order for its observance, indicating the importance and greatness of the June 3rd Memorial. Mr. Lin's legacy includes many impassioned statements and methods in his memorial urging the prohibition of opium. We now excerpt a few paragraphs below: The poison of opium is worse than floods and fierce beasts. No one in the world would consider opium not worthy of prohibition. If this disaster is not eliminated, we will have no usable soldiers or resources to plan with in ten years. The spread of opium in the interior is like the spread of carbuncles and sores on the human body. When carbuncles and sores grow, they gradually produce pus. When opium comes, it gradually leads to invaders. We must eliminate opium completely to eradicate the root of the disease. Mr. Lin's opium prohibition after the destruction of opium: After Mr. Lin prohibited opium, Britain sent troops to Guangzhou, Dinghai, Ningbo, and Bohai, one after another, for the sake of the dishonorable opium trade. At that time, coastal border officials failed in their duties, and everyone slandered Mr. Lin, saying he was the culprit who started the war. The Qing court, facing difficult diplomacy, removed him from office. After the peace agreement was reached, the Qing court, under the pressure of imperialism, could not talk about opium prohibition, but opium continued to be imported. Before Guangxu two years (1876), there is no way to verify. From two years onwards until the Republic of China seventeen years (1928), in the fifty-three years in between, the foreign opium imported cost the customs 130 million taels of silver. At the end of Guangxu, a ten-year eradication agreement was finally made with Britain. After the ten-year period expired, it was surprisingly eradicated nationwide. Unexpectedly, after the Republic of China year five, local warlords embraced troops to defend themselves, levied opium taxes to protect the trafficking and consumption of opium, colluding with imperialism, filling the foreign lands. After the end of the European War, narcotics such as morphine, heroin, and cocaine took the opportunity to be imported, spreading disaster throughout the country, making it even more unmanageable. After the establishment of the Chinese National Anti-Narcotics Association, it followed Mr. Lin and the Premier's anti-drug legacy, vigorously advocating to stop the import of foreign opium and narcotics, and to eradicate the domestic cultivation, trafficking, and sale of opium and narcotics. After several years of running around and calling out, it aroused national sympathy. After the establishment of the National Government, the suggestion was made to transition from the opium monopoly system to a complete prohibition policy, establishing a Prohibition Committee. However, in the past two years, due to the deep-rooted habits of the people and the evil forces of imperialism, which have not yet been eradicated, the implementation of opium prohibition has encountered various difficulties. The domestic cultivation of opium has not yet been eradicated, and the trafficking and consumption in various places still cause many problems. Mr. Lin and the late Premier's anti-drug legacy have not yet been fully achieved. Our necessary understanding and efforts: Our country has been brought to this point internationally, and the people's livelihood at home has been brought to such poverty, all because of the Opium War, which wrote a bill of sale in the form of the Treaty of Nanjing and all the unequal treaties that started from it. If we want to abolish unequal treaties, the fundamental thing is for everyone to work hard to completely ban opium and all narcotics that replace opium. Mr. Lin and the Premier's fearless spirit are worthy of our emulation. However, opium prohibition and anti-narcotics are not simple matters. Everyone must take on this responsibility and work hard, either by advising children, relatives, and friends, or by uniting comrades to assist the government. Only with the cooperation of officials and civilians can we achieve complete success.

Meeting Order (1) Opening, Presidium takes seats, (2) Music, (3) Sing the Party Song, (4) Bow to the Party and National Flag and the Premier's portrait, (5) Chairman respectfully reads the Premier's will and anti-drug legacy, (6) Silence, (7) Chairman's opening remarks, (8) Report on the state of opium prohibition (9) Speeches, (10) Passing of proposals, (11) Oath (12) Slogans (13) Music (14) Photograph and adjournment.

Slogans (1) Implement the Premier's anti-drug legacy, (2) Completely ban opium and narcotics, (3) Punish officials who undermine opium prohibition severely (4) Abolish unequal treaties, (5) Stop the import of foreign narcotics, (6) Continue Mr. Lin's spirit, eradicate the harm of opium (7) Complete the national revolution (8) Long live the success of anti-narcotics.

Draft Proposal for the Construction of a Lin Zexu Memorial Hall

Reason: Mr. Lin Zexu was the first to advocate opium prohibition. His heroic spirit is admired forever. Today, the opium scourge is rampant and ever-increasing. Shanghai is the focus of attention both domestically and internationally, and it is the place where sovereignty was lost after the defeat in the Opium War. We advocate anti-narcotics, remember the legacy of our predecessors, promote the spirit of our predecessors, and thoroughly eradicate narcotics, and we should have an appropriate memorial to set an example. As we commemorate the 91st anniversary of Mr. Lin's destruction of foreign opium, at the time of the memorial meeting held in this city, we specially put forward this case to select several items for discussion, and respectfully ask for a decision.

Measures (1) Organize a committee for the construction of the Lin Zexu Memorial Hall and specially invite other members to handle it. (2) The Memorial Hall will be equipped with an anti-drug library to collect Chinese and foreign publications on anti-drugs, both ancient and modern. (3) The Memorial Hall will be equipped with an anti-drug art museum to display various exhibits and other artistic products related to anti-drugs. (4) The Memorial Hall will be equipped with a narcotic drug treatment research institute to engage in chemical experiments and research on smoking cessation drugs. (5) The Memorial Hall will be equipped with a model smoking cessation hospital to accommodate smokers and implement cessation. (6) A portion of the Memorial Hall should be set aside to commemorate people who have made contributions to anti-narcotics, displaying photographs and memorial monuments, etc. (7) The fundraising method for the Memorial Hall can be based on the budget of each part, and donors or groups can be invited to take responsibility separately to achieve integration. (8) The address of the Memorial Hall can be requested from the municipal government to allocate public property to fill it. (9) The construction and equipment of the Memorial Hall can be determined according to the economic situation (original manuscript missing below)

Zhang Zhijiang's Letter to the People Zhang Zhijiang's letter to the people for the Opium Prohibition Memorial Day says: Why is June 3rd the Opium Prohibition Memorial Day? It is because June 3rd, ninety-one years ago, was the beginning of a strong struggle against the opium policy of the imperialists against China in Chinese history. At that time, the government was not a revolutionary government, and the environment was not a revolutionary environment. The sage Lin Zexu alone was able to be unyielding, uncompromising, and irreconcilable, setting fire to 20,083 boxes of opium from British merchants, without the slightest hesitation or consideration, thus chilling the courage of foreign merchants and boosting the spirit of the people. If the Manchu government of that day had not been confused and had not hindered him, allowing him to complete his work, then the opium scourge in China would have been cleared long ago. However, since Qishan misled the country and the war was lost, it has resulted in the land of 5,000 years of civilization, the offspring of 400 million gods, whose qualifications could have surpassed Europe and America and soared in East Asia, being transformed into a weakling unable to recover and faltering under the constraints of unequal treaties by various imperialists, allowing them to oppress and slaughter at will, causing the people's blood and the nation's rights and interests to leak out like a goblet and flow like a river, overflowing and unrecoverable. And now it is approaching poverty and danger. Alas, is this not what Mr. Lin's spirit in heaven is lamenting and what our revolutionary party should strive to achieve after admiring the sage, seeking to achieve the goal of opium prohibition and saving the country? Because since the Opium War failed, it started the trend of ceding land and paying indemnities. Since the Opium War failed, it led to the gradual loss of rights and national humiliation. Since the Opium War failed, the bullying of unequal treaties by various imperialists came together. Since the Opium War failed, opium prohibition was greatly relaxed, and the scourge spread throughout the country like mercury pouring onto the ground, entering everywhere without any holes. Even after repeated strict orders, it could not be saved. If the imperialists were to indulge in harming us with opium and if our people had not transported, sold, or bought it before the Opium War, then Mr. Lin would not have had to destroy opium on June 3rd, and the war could have been avoided. Even after the Opium War, if the people had known shame and aroused themselves, and were all able to take Mr. Lin's heart as their own, there would be no reason why the opium scourge would not be eradicated. But how could they be so immersed in pleasure, wasting their lives away, for nearly a hundred years? June 3rd comes once a year, and the eradication of opium is far off and hopeless. Alas, I think about it, I think about it again, how can I get Mr. Lin down from the Nine Heavens, so that he can transform into 400 million people, holding my stubborn and unresponsive people, one by one, and drumming up their courage, inspiring their spirit, and urging them to rise up together and fight a life-and-death battle with opium, to wash away the great shame of a century of national humiliation and disease, and restore the vigorous and rising atmosphere? If we can do this, is it not a happy event? Unfortunately, it is impossible. Then I think of Mr. Lin back then, as a lonely minister in the Lingnan region, facing great difficulties, overcoming opposition, unmoved by enticements, and undeterred by threats. I can imagine the scene of the opium destruction at that time, with the flames burning brightly and the national prestige being magnificent. His sincerity touched even the pigs and fish, and the foreign merchants who came to Guangdong willingly obeyed. This is recorded in the national history and is not false. His noble character should last forever and be renewed throughout the universe. Although the person is gone, his spirit remains. We do not need to see his full picture, but if each of the 400 million people can each get one percent, one thousandth, or one ten-thousandth of Mr. Lin's spirit as a seed, sprouting as a root and growing, either having the power to resist opium in a country, or having the power to resist opium in a township, or having the power to resist opium in a family, or even having only the power to resist opium in oneself, and thus cut oneself off from opium, if all 400 million people can cut themselves off from opium, the impact on the future of opium prohibition will be extremely rapid and significant. The only question is, how can this be achieved? The June 3rd Opium Prohibition Memorial is precisely to arouse the great attention of the 400 million people on this month and this day, so that each person recalls the humiliation of the Opium War and stirs up their spirits, remotely connecting with the spirit of the sage Lin Zexu ninety-one years ago, striving to transform the spirit of one person, Mr. Lin, on that day into the spirit of 400 million people today. Alas, is this the meaning of the Opium Prohibition Memorial Day being designated on June 3rd? It is hoped that the people of the whole country will use this memorial day to deeply consider the meaning of the memorial, recall the past scourge of opium on the country, and then be startled and admire Mr. Lin's destruction of opium, and then realize and look forward to the future, and then be happy and joyful, startled by the fact that the scourge of opium has reached its highest point and can no longer be allowed to spread, realizing that Mr. Lin is also a person, and so am I, and I but slightly have the spirit of Mr. Lin, and the cause of opium prohibition can be greatly accomplished, happy that if the people work together from now on, opium and narcotics will never be seen again under the clear sky and bright sun. If this is the case, then Mr. Lin's spirit can be passed down to the people through the Opium Prohibition Memorial, and the spirit of the people can also be conveyed to Mr. Lin through the Opium Prohibition Memorial. With this opium prohibition, no opium will not be prohibited. With this eradication of drugs, no drug will not be eradicated. If we can achieve this from this year onwards, and if we can cooperate nationwide, the opium scourge can be hoped to be eradicated, and if we can go through another year, and then go through countless years, the annual opium prohibition memorial will not only commemorate June 3rd, ninety-one years ago, but will also commemorate today's June 3rd as the last memorial day for the opium forces, and at the same time commemorate it. If we can sincerely do this, then I will pray and wish for our people and respectfully wish you success.

Sun Yat-sen Bronze Statue at North Station

Completion by Deadline

The construction of the Sun Yat-sen bronze statue was initiated in the year 17 of the Republic of China, proposed by the Shanghai Special City Party Department, the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, the Shanghai Special City Government, and the Jinghu Huhangyong Railway Administration. Representatives from various agencies and groups were invited to open meetings and make resolutions to organize the Shanghai North Station Construction Sun Yat-sen Bronze Statue Committee. On the birthday of Sun Yat-sen on March 12 of that year, a groundbreaking ceremony for the bronze statue was held at the square of Shanghai North Station. Donation booklets were printed and distributed to various agencies and groups to solicit funds for the statue. Later, due to changes in personnel in various agencies, no one was in charge, and the matter was suspended. In the winter of last year, the Jinghu Huhangyong Railway Administration re-invited representatives from various agencies and groups to meet and discuss the continuation of fundraising. It is now reported that the estimated amount of funds raised is nearly 30,000 yuan. It is reported that eleven agency representatives were recently elected as construction committee members, and a construction committee was established. The Shanghai Special City Party Department, the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, the Shanghai Special City Government, the Jinghu Huhangyong Railway Administration, and Mr. Wang Xiaolai were elected as standing committee members, responsible for carrying out the construction work. At 4:00 PM on the 2nd of this month, the construction committee and the standing committee were reconvened in the meeting hall on the second floor of the North Station Road Bureau. It is reported that those present included representatives from the Lianglu Railway Administration, Wang Jichang and Zheng Shian, representatives from the Shanghai Special City Party Department, Ye Xiufu, representatives from the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, Zhang Taiji, representatives from the Exchange Federation, Wen Lanting, and Wang Xiaolai, Wang Binyan, Wang Yansong, Ye Huijun, and representatives from the Shanghai Local Court, Wang Pengjun. Mr. Wang Xiaolai was elected as the temporary chairman of the standing committee, and Mr. Yu Hongxiang from the Road Bureau took minutes. Regarding the construction matters, it was resolved to publish in the newspaper to solicit bronze statue designs, and then concentrate on the plans of Shanghai's statue casting experts before bidding for construction. It is reported that the estimated completion date is the Double Ten Festival of this year, and the latest deadline shall not exceed January 1, 20th year of the Republic of China. It is reported that Shanghai art experts are very enthusiastically responding to the solicitation, and it is expected that in less than half a year, the bronze statue of Sun Yat-sen, the great man of the world and the leader of the Chinese revolution, will stand majestically in the square of Shanghai North Station, the largest commercial port in our country, attracting the attention of tens of thousands of people.

Public Debt Lottery Repayment

Totaling 8.24 Million Yuan

Yesterday at 2:00 PM, the Ministry of Finance held a lottery for the fifth repayment of the six-percent public debt of the Republic of China year seven, the third repayment of the military supply public debt of the Ministry of Finance of the National Government, the fourth repayment of the short-term public debt of the Ministry of Finance of the National Government for rehabilitation, the third repayment of the disaster relief public debt of the Republic of China year eighteen, and the first repayment of the customs duty public debt of the Republic of China year nineteen at the Bankers' Association on Hong Kong Road. The winning numbers and the total amount of repayment are detailed below.

Lottery Order (1) Ringing the bell to open the meeting, (2) The Chairman respectfully reads the Premier's will, (3) Three minutes of silence, (4) Report by the Director of the Public Debt Department, (5) Examination of the lottery tickets and the lottery ticket ledger, (6) Conducting the lottery, (7) Reporting the total number of winners, (8) Adjournment.

Staff at the Meeting Chairman: Director Zheng Laidai; Supervisors: Wang Laitian from the Audit Court, Hu Mengjia from the Shanghai Bankers' Association, Fu Songnian from the Shanghai Money Industry, Lin Kanghou from the Foundation Preservation Committee (representing Fan Gongtang), Xu Jiyin from the Shanghai Business Readjustment Committee; Lottery Officers: Li Tisheng from the Central Bank, Cheng Muhao from the Bank of China, Jin Wenyuan from the Bank of Communications; Managers: Zhu Zuhao, Guo Binghe, Lu Shutang, He Xiaojuan, Pang Zeen; Document Clerks: He Junchao, Luo Peide; Registration Clerks: Chen Shaochao, Xu Zuhuang, Liang Yaozong; Receptionists: Wang Gongshi, Huang Meizhao, He Yaoqing.

Chairman's Report Today is the day for the lottery for the repayment of five types of bonds, including the six-percent public debt of the Republic of China year seven. I am very pleased to have you all here to observe. The total amount of the six-percent public debt issued in the Republic of China year seven was 45 million yuan. In addition to the first, second, third, and fourth repayments, which have already been drawn and repaid on schedule, today's draw is for the fifth repayment of principal, with five draws, each draw worth 450,000 yuan, totaling 2.25 million yuan. All winning bonds will be paid from the 30th of this month by the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications in various locations, along with the 25th installment of interest. Please ask the supervisors to check the lottery tickets and the lottery ticket ledger for the purpose of conducting the lottery. The fifth repayment lottery for the six-percent public debt of the Republic of China year seven has now been completed, and the third repayment lottery for the military supply public debt of the Ministry of Finance of the National Government should be carried out. The total amount of this public debt issued was 10 million yuan. According to the regulations, the principal is repaid twice a year starting from the year 18 of the Republic of China, with each repayment accounting for one-twentieth of the total amount. In addition to the first and second repayments, which have already been drawn and repaid on schedule, today's draw is for the third repayment of principal, with five draws, totaling about 500,000 yuan. All winning bonds will be paid from the 30th of this month by the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications in various locations, along with the fourth installment of interest. Please ask the supervisors to check the lottery tickets and the lottery ticket ledger for the purpose of conducting the lottery. The third repayment lottery for the military supply public debt has now been completed, and the fourth repayment lottery for the short-term public debt of the Ministry of Finance of the National Government for rehabilitation should be carried out. The total amount of this public debt issued was 40 million yuan. In addition to the first, second, and third repayments, which have already been drawn on schedule, this is the fourth repayment lottery, with ten draws to be drawn, each draw worth 400,000 yuan, totaling 4 million yuan. All winning bonds will be paid from the 30th of this month by the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications in various locations, along with the fourth installment of interest. Please ask the supervisors to check the lottery tickets and the lottery ticket ledger for the purpose of conducting the lottery. The fourth repayment lottery for the short-term public debt for rehabilitation has now been completed, and the third repayment lottery for the disaster relief public debt of the Republic of China year eighteen should be carried out. The total amount of this public debt issued was 10 million yuan. According to the regulations, the repayment began in June of the year 18 of the Republic of China, with two draws to be drawn each year, and each repayment accounting for one-twentieth of the total amount. In addition to the first and second repayments, which have already been drawn on schedule, today's draw is for the third repayment, with five draws, each draw worth 100,000 yuan, totaling 500,000 yuan. All winning bonds will be paid from the 30th of this month by the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications in various locations, along with the third installment of interest. Please ask the supervisors to check the lottery tickets and the lottery ticket ledger for the purpose of conducting the lottery. The third repayment lottery for the disaster relief public debt has now been completed, and the first repayment lottery for the customs duty public debt of the Republic of China year nineteen should be carried out. The total amount of this public debt issued was 20 million yuan. According to the regulations, the repayment began in June of the year 19 of the Republic of China, with two draws to be drawn each year, and each repayment accounting for one-twentieth of the total amount. Today is the first draw, with five draws, totaling about 1 million yuan. Ministry of Foreign Affairs

Sincere Consideration for Chinese Merchants' Shipping

Please Request Anhui Provincial Government to Postpone Pier and Pontoon Construction

The Shanghai Shipping Association sent a letter to the General Administration of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company yesterday, saying: Dear Sirs, previously, the Anhui Provincial Government planned to set up public piers and pontoons in Anqing to attract foreign ships to dock, which would affect the business of Chinese ships and harm the national character and shipping rights. We requested that you submit a request to stop it in order to protect national rights, etc. We have separately submitted reports to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Communications, and the Anhui Provincial Government to instruct them to stop it, and we have also received a copy of the approval from the Ministry of Communications on the 26th of last month. Now, we have received document number 52 from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, which states: Received. Although Anqing is not a trading port, the permission for foreign ships to dock is already stipulated in treaties and regulations. However, passengers and goods have always been loaded and unloaded by civilian ships. According to Inspector Li, it was suggested to set up pontoons, and the Anhui Provincial Government approved the proposal. According to the case report of the Construction Department, the department's expanded special meeting was proposed by member Yu Xizhang and passed by the conference. The Anqing Municipal Administration Preparatory Office also made this request. This shows that the drawbacks are obvious and everyone agrees. This time, the proposed pontoons are purely to facilitate domestic merchants and travelers, not to benefit foreign ships. Moreover, they are set up and managed by us, and pontoon taxes can be levied. This measure is taken for the implementation of administrative power, so how can it be said to damage national sovereignty? Furthermore, the right of foreign ships to dock in Anqing will not be increased or decreased due to the existence of pontoons, and the route of foreign ships on the Yangtze River will not be lengthened or shortened due to the existence of Anqing pontoons. This is very clear. However, according to the association's report that it hinders the business of Chinese merchants, the Ministry of Communications also approved the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's report, which is the same. Now is the time to protect the shipping industry, and the government will never want to harm the people by seeking to benefit them. Since this case has been expressed by the domestic shipping industry as hindering the business of Chinese merchants, the Ministry has already sent a reply to the Anhui Provincial Government, requesting a postponement and finding other ways to ensure the safety of merchants and travelers. You are hereby informed.

Suggestions for Relief Funds

Limit Gold Prices to No More Than 500 Taels

Prohibit Transactions on the Exchange for Gold Speculation

Petition from the District Office: The Sixth District and Tenth Branch of the Shanghai Special Municipality submitted a document requesting the cessation of gold speculation transactions on the exchange, stating: (Omitted above) Due to the soaring gold prices, the market is in turmoil. We implore the government to halt gold speculation transactions on the exchange to safeguard the national foundation. The exorbitant rise in gold prices, reaching over 550 taels, results in significant losses in international settlements. Shops and money houses in Shanghai are collapsing daily, placing our nation's finances in a precarious state. According to the Exchange Law, the government has the authority to suspend trading in the event of substantial market fluctuations, and there are precedents to follow. Currently, gold prices are rising daily, threatening a precipitous decline. If no measures are taken to prevent it, the impact on the national economy and people's livelihoods will be immense. Therefore, after a resolution by the party members' congress, we telegraph the government to issue a clear order to stop gold speculation transactions, thereby avoiding manipulation by foreigners causing drastic price crashes. This will also prevent our national finances from falling into bankruptcy. We hereby record this petition and request that it be forwarded to the government to issue a clear order prohibiting gold speculation transactions on the exchange, thereby safeguarding the national foundation. (Omitted below)

Song Shixiang's Proposal: Mr. Song Shixiang, a member of the Chamber of Commerce Readjustment Committee, proposed a motion to the committee due to the soaring gold prices, market panic, and the shaking of the national foundation. The original text of his motion is as follows: (Omitted above) Believing that the soaring gold prices are of great importance to the national economy and people's livelihoods, the member previously proposed prohibiting the import of silver. Although the government issued a ban a month ago, it was too late to reverse the tide. Now, the price of gold has soared to 550 taels, an unprecedented level, causing extreme market panic, which will inevitably lead our country into a crisis. After repeated discussions among the members, the current relief method should be for your committee to urgently telegraph the government to stabilize the gold price, restricting it to a limit of no more than 500 taels, so that foreign exchange can be stabilized immediately. We also request that the government investigate and follow the Exchange Regulations regarding market price fluctuations, issuing a clear order prohibiting gold speculation transactions. Furthermore, the government already has a clear provision for taxing silver bars for a six-month trial period. We also request your committee to telegraph the government to instruct the customs to strictly enforce this provision. Is this appropriate? We respectfully request a public decision for implementation.

Naval Representatives' Congress

Opened Yesterday

The Second Naval All-Forces Party Member Representative Congress was held yesterday morning at 8:00 AM in the auditorium of the Jiangnan Shipyard in Gaochang Temple. The opening ceremony and the election of the congress presidium and various officers were held, chaired by Ren Guangyu. After the official opening, the second session of executive and supervisory committee members was elected. The committee members were elected at 3:00 PM and immediately took office, with Zhang Qun, the Special Mayor of Shanghai appointed by the Central Government, as the oath supervisor. The meeting adjourned around 5:00 PM. The proceedings of the meeting are recorded in detail below.

Attending Representatives: The representatives attending the congress included representatives from the 1st, 2nd, and 4th Naval Fleets, Training Fleet, Torpedo Fleet, various brigades of the Marine Corps, key ports and fortresses in Minxia, and party branches of various groups in the Compilation and Reduction Office, totaling 96 people.

Supervisory Committee: The Central Party Headquarters, in response to the opening of the Second Naval Representative Congress, specially dispatched Huang Zhongxiang, Director of the Military Organization Section of the Organization Department, to supervise the elections.

Congress Staff: At 8:00 AM yesterday morning, a preparatory meeting was held, chaired by Ren Guangyu, and the following congress staff were elected: (A) Presidium of nine members: Chen Xunyong, Li Shijia, Ren Guangyu, Zheng Youyi, Yang Shien, Deng Xilin, Chen Jigang, Lin Zhenhua; (B) Recorders of two members: Cai Linbing, Lin Hanlai; (C) Proposal Review Committee of three members: Li Mengbin, Ye Yangmin, Chen Zuwang; (D) Ballot Issuers of two members: Liang Xunying, Li Chongjie; (E) Ballot Issuing Supervisor: Zhang Rizhang; (F) Ballot Counters of two members: Wu Wei, Wang Jun; (G) Ballot Counting Supervisor: Meng Xiuchun; (H) Announcers of two members: Wang Zhiguang, Xie Haoen.

Election of Executive and Supervisory Committee Members: After the congress staff was determined, the official meeting began. Chen Xunyong led the ceremony, and then Chairman Ren delivered the opening speech and reported on the past work. The election results were then announced: Ren Guangyu received 89 votes, Chen Xunyong 82 votes, Zheng Youyi 77 votes, Chen Shaokuan 70 votes, Ma Deji 70 votes, Li Shijia 62 votes, Wang Shouting 60 votes, Li Mengbin 56 votes, and Lü Deyuan 37 votes. The above nine people were elected as Executive Committee Members. Chen Jiliang received 78 votes, Chen Ce 56 votes, Zeng Yiding 49 votes, Wu Zhennan 41 votes, and Zhou Zhaorui 38 votes. The above five people were elected as Supervisory Committee Members. Chen Ding received 28 votes, Lin Yuanquan 21 votes, Ye Baoqi 18 votes, Lin Shouguo 10 votes, and Meng Xiuchun 10 votes. The above five people were elected as Alternate Executive Committee Members. Lin Guogeng received 28 votes, and Yu Bangyan 16 votes. The above two people were elected as Alternate Supervisory Committee Members. The election was announced finished, and it was noon. The Chairman announced an adjournment until 2:00 PM in the afternoon.

Submitted Proposals: The congress proposals included: (1) Raising the living standards of soldiers; (2) How to subsidize the expenses of party branches at all levels in the military; (3) Establishing special party branches; (4) Requesting the Central Government to grant permission for the military to recruit party members to expand the organization; (5) Improving the economic situation of marines; (6) Requesting the Navy Department to deploy marines to coastal ports and accompany ships to suppress rebels; (7) Naval educational institutions should be requested to specially set up Party Doctrine teachers for training; (8) Submitting a request to the Central Government for subsidies to the Navy's special party branches; (9) Submitting a request to the Central Government to promptly issue a work program for party affairs during the political tutelage period for compliance; (10) Proposing that the National Government allocate funds to maintain the Jiangnan Shipyard; (11) Submitting a request to the Central Party Department to expand the regulations for the organization of the special party branch of this unit; (12) The congress will send a telegram to the frontline soldiers to express condolences; and more than ten other items.

New Committee Members Take Office: After the Executive and Supervisory Committee Members were elected in the morning, the oath-taking ceremony was held at 2:00 PM in the afternoon. The order of the oath-taking ceremony was as follows: (1) Opening; (2) Singing the Party song; (3) Saluting the Party and National Flag and the portrait of the Founding Father; (4) The oath supervisor reading the will; (5) Silence; (6) Executive and Supervisory Committee Members taking office; (7) The oath supervisor Zhang Qun delivering a speech (omitted); (8) Guest speeches (omitted); (9) Executive Committee Member Ren Guangyu delivering a response (omitted); (10) Shouting slogans; (11) Photograph; (12) Dismissal of the ceremony; (13) Tea reception. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM. All proposals will be discussed starting this morning. The draft of the congress declaration will also be released today.

Committee Members' Oath: The text of the oath taken by each committee member reads: I swear with sincerity to abide by the Founding Father's will, believe in the Party's doctrines, abide by the Party's discipline, obey the Party's orders, strictly guard the Party's secrets, absolutely not organize or join other political groups, absolutely not be selfish, absolutely not act based on personal feelings or impulsiveness. If I violate this oath, I am willing to accept the Party's most severe punishment. I swear.

Central Bank Inspection Report

55th Time

The 55th inspection report of the Central Bank's issuance reserve stated that this committee is responsible for inspecting the Bank's issuance of exchange coupons in accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank's Regulations. The 55th government inspection was held at the Bank's Issuance Bureau on May 31, 1920. The inspection results are announced as follows: The total amount of exchange coupons issued is 15,985,922 silver dollars, including 14,837,229 silver dollar coupons and 1,148,693 supplementary currency coupons. The amount of exchange coupon reserve is 15,985,922 silver dollars, including 11,038,917.20 silver dollars in cash reserve. The cash reserve includes 7,190,478.31 silver dollars stored in the Bank's Issuance Treasury, 1,349,935.14 silver dollars stored in branch banks in various ports, and 2,498,503.75 silver dollars stored in peer banks. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 4,947,004.80 silver dollars. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank Exchange Coupon Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The inspection results show that the cash exceeds 60% and the guarantee is less than 40%, which is in accordance with the regulations. This report is hereby made. May 31, 1920, Chairman of the Supervisory Committee of the Central Bank, Li Fuxun, Supervisors Wang Jingli, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, and Xu Jilong.

Our Newspaper's Old Friend

Demise of Mr. Zhang Shenxiang

Mr. Zhang Shenxiang, an old friend of our newspaper, treasured Shen Bao from issue number one to ten thousand, compiled into a massive volume, and generously returned it to our office, which was admired by our colleagues. Mr. Zhang lived outside the Dalong Road, outside the Great South Gate, this year eighty years old, in his life enthusiastic for public works, such as founding the Third District Fire Brigade, Nanshi Chamber of Commerce and other ways that the locals always took as a role model, now on the first of this month passed away. His family will hold a funeral at noon today and bury him in Zhoupu Town. Relatives and friends are all mournful.

Image of the Late Mr. Zhang Shenxiang

Representatives of the Chamber of Commerce Readjustment Committee Go to Beijing to Petition

To Request the Return of Placement of Unemployed Pharmaceutical Workers

The Chamber of Commerce Readjustment Committee, in order to petition the Central Government to request the return of the placement of unemployed pharmaceutical workers, after a meeting of the entire committee, publicly elected Yu Qiaqing, Ye Huijun, Wang Yansong, Wang Xiaolai, and Wen Lanting as five committee members as representatives, to petition various party and government institutions in Beijing and Shanghai. These five representatives have repeatedly consulted with the Municipal Party Headquarters and Municipal Government in this city, and have obtained considerable solutions. Last night, they took the train to Beijing to petition the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. The petition is recorded below: Submitting for the sake of unemployed pharmaceutical workers, it is proposed to be revised to be introduced by the affiliated merchant pharmaceutical groups themselves, exempt from checking the review list, to place them so as to take care of both sides and resolve disputes, hoping for approval to be followed. Case check: The Pharmaceutical Industry Association of this city, due to the issue of the Central Government's unresolved dispute over the placement of unemployed workers in the pharmaceutical industry, drafted six regulations, only one of which, the replacement system, is factually impossible to exist. According to the list approved by the Party Headquarters, the placement of more than 64 people is considered to still contain mandatory characteristics, and is greatly related to the store's business survival. It is still requested to be transferred back to withdraw the order, etc., and was transferred on the 16th of this month. Various industry groups in this city, because this matter has been prolonged and has not been appropriately resolved, and the wind of the workers of various industries preparing to succeed has become tighter day by day, and they have no choice but to plan methods to deal with it. Therefore, in addition to the last 44 groups that jointly wrote to request the convening of a representative meeting of various industries, there are another 15 industry associations that continue to make this request. The affiliated associations, in view of the increasing agitation of commercial sentiment, convened the 13th plenary meeting on the 22nd and 23rd of this month (May) to propose a discussion. All believed that the panic in various industries was caused by the pharmaceutical industry, and the dispute in the pharmaceutical industry this time, The most important one of the six regulations drafted by the Central Government is to limit the hiring of workers who have passed the review of the Mediation Committee, and the number is about 64 or more. The difference between priority hiring and forced placement is not in the words used, but in whether the store actually has the sovereignty to consider itself. Now, if more than 64 people are limited, the store does not have the power to reduce the quota. The situation is not as before that each store can accommodate a few people. The limit is that the investigation committee secretly checks and passes the qualification. Even if there are those with bad habits and poor skills, the store has no right to deny it. Whether the store actually needs so many people or not, whether the personnel are really appropriate or not, there is no room for control or consideration at all. Even if the word "hiring" is still used in the name, the spirit is mandatory.

The authorities of this city have already expressed the intention to enforce it forcibly. Impartially considering it, there is no difference between it and forced placement.

Since the National Government's approval has determined that forced placement is inappropriate, the pharmaceutical industry cannot but request relief based on this approval. Therefore, for the clause that limits the hiring of more than 64 people who have passed the review, we cannot but request to withdraw the order. Also, Article 27 of the Labor Union Law states that the labor union cannot restrict the employer from using the people it introduces. In other words, it cannot force the introduction. The original purpose of this regulation was to preserve the employer's right to employ people. Even if there are differences in the wording of forced placement, there is no difference in nature. In a word, anything that hinders the employer's right to employ people is not allowed by law.

The labor union itself cannot forcibly demand from the store. Based on the same reason, it cannot request the national agency to forcibly place it.

Moreover, the standard of the so-called "qualified by the party and government agencies," whether the standard of the word "qualified" is consistent with the actual situation, only the store that has worked together for many years can deeply understand the bottom line, and it is definitely not something that outsiders can propose on their behalf. If there is another qualification standard other than this, then the actual situation of the qualified person may run counter to what the store needs, and the store believes that it should request to withdraw the order. This is also the key point. If it is said that without the procedures of the party and government agencies, there is a concern that reactionary elements may be mixed in, then the store regards the reactionary elements almost like snakes and scorpions. There is nothing more to add to their fear and desire to reject them. There is absolutely no opening the door to invite thieves or self-harm. However, this case has been held up for a long time, and both sides are unfavorable, and the Central and Municipal Party and Government authorities in this city have made great efforts to provide relief to unemployed workers in the pharmaceutical industry, and the store should also admire it. However, only if it does not hinder the scope of the central approval, national law, and the store's sovereignty, the pharmaceutical industry should also try its best to make it difficult, in order to achieve both. It is proposed that the affiliated associations and pharmaceutical groups select those with docile characteristics from among the unemployed workers and do their best to take responsibility for introduction, and do not limit the number and names of those who have passed the review. The rest should follow the regulations drafted by the Central Government, separately give funds and send them back to their original places. After this separate processing, there are no more unemployed pharmaceutical workers within the city area, and the replacement system is no longer possible to exist, and should be discussed as a debate and need not be handled separately. The resolution is based on the above two items, and Yu Qiaqing, Ye Huijun, Wang Yansong, Wang Xiaolai, and Wen Lanting are elected to go to the capital to petition the party and government agencies. It is appropriate to prepare a document for submission, and hand it over to the petition representative to submit to the appropriate Ministry and Government. May the audit be approved and implemented, it will be publicly convenient. (June 2nd)

Sharp Decline in Shipping on the Upper Yangtze River

The upper reaches of the Yangtze River, as a rule, during the summer flood season, is the busiest time for import and export goods, but recently, due to various reasons, the situation of stagnation of all kinds of goods has suddenly appeared. The outflow of goods from central Hunan has become increasingly low, and various shipping companies in this port have already agreed to lower the water freight of the largest commodity, cotton yarn, to 1 tael and 9 qian per piece, in order to encourage customers to attract goods. Now, seeing that there is no hope of revival, the companies are even considering reducing the number of shifts. The recent news is reported separately as follows:

Reduction of Shifts on Ships to Yichang: Since last year, various foreign merchants in Shanghai to Yichang Shashi have dispatched direct ships. The Taikoo's Poyang wheel went to Yichang last time to Xindi and collided violently with this company's iron barge Xinyang, and the bow of Poyang was damaged. It was towed back to Shanghai on an empty ship and entered the factory for major repairs. It was completed yesterday and resumed service this morning. However, it happened to encounter a stagnation of goods on the upper river, so the ship decided to only go to Hankou and temporarily not sail to Shashi, to avoid the loss of empty航行.

Sharp Decline in Goods Shipped to Hunan: Starting last week, the outflow of goods from Shanghai to Changsha, Xiangtan, Yuezhou and other places plummeted, and the export business from Shashi also declined sharply. Japanese ships sailing in Hunan have telegraphed Shanghai, requesting the First Overseas Dispatch Team of the Japanese Navy to urgently dispatch the warship Ataka to escort them in Hunan.

Drop in Passenger Ticket Prices on the Upper River: Taikoo, Jardine, Nisshin, and China Merchants Steam Navigation Company agreed that the price of passenger tickets on the Upper River will jointly drop from June 1st, and a new rate has been drafted as follows:

Destination 1st Class New Price Original Price Third Class Price

Xindi 12 yuan None None

Yuezhou 16 20 yuan 3 yuan

Shashi 36 45 6

Changsha 20 25 6

Yichang 40 50 9

Wanxian 36 None 3

Chongqing 72 None 9

Ning Shao Wheel is Approved to Resume Service: Within the past week, it was originally scheduled that the Changjiang Hualun of this area needed 11 ships to stop service, and the Zhaoxing Changxing and other ships were all temporarily suspended. The Ning Shao wheel was originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai today, and after unloading the incoming goods, it would stop commercial shifts. After repeated consultations by the company, it was approved to resume business. Therefore, starting tomorrow, the ship can still resume the Yangtze River, and a total of ten Yangtze River ships have been suspended, but the Changjiang ship of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company can still operate as usual.

Local News Two

An Old Fellow Guns Down a Young Fellow

Big A-Shi and Little A-Shi Playing

Tragedy Strikes While Playing with a Handgun

Around 6:45 last night, a shooting occurred near Route Ferguson in the French Concession, resulting in the death of a five-year-old child. The circumstances are quite bizarre. The details are recorded as follows:

A Laundry Worker's Family: Behind a nine-story building near Route Ferguson in the French Concession, in an area called Chenjia Lane, amidst green fields, resembling a village, lives Qiu Guiquan, a man from Ningbo in his forties. He works as a laundry worker for a Western manager at the Xiangmao Soap factory near Hongqiao Airport. He is married to Wang, and they have a son and a daughter. The daughter, named A-Mao, is seven years old, and the son, named A-Shi, is just five years old. The family rents a flat in the Chenjia Lane from an old widow named Chen.

Li A-Tu Frequently Visits: The homeowner, the old widow Chen, lives next door to Qiu. About a mile northeast in Chenjia Lane, in the Li family residence, lives Li A-Shi, who lives off ancestral land and is essentially an unemployed vagrant. He is acquainted with the widow Chen. Every day at dusk, Li comes to Chen's house to play, which has become his habit. Over time, he has become friends with Qiu. Because Qiu works as a laundry worker, Li occasionally brings clothes to Chen's house, asking Qiu to wash them. Around 6:45 last night, Qiu had not yet returned home. Qiu's wife, Wang, was visiting a neighbor who was ill when Li arrived unhurriedly.

Suddenly Playing with a Handgun: As Li entered the bamboo fence gate of Chen's house, he saw Qiu's son and daughter eating dinner at a small table near the entrance. Li approached the table, chatting and joking with the two children. Somehow, he suddenly took out a handgun to play with. Unfortunately, he accidentally touched the trigger. With a "bang," a bullet came out of the gun and struck Qiu's son, A-Shi, in the right hand, going straight into his mouth and piercing the back of his neck. By the time Wang heard the noise and rushed out to investigate, both the old fellow and the young fellow were pale. Qiu's son immediately fell to the ground and died shortly after.

The Culprit Flees: Wang saw her beloved son shot to death and immediately grabbed Li, shouting for help. The old widow Chen also heard the commotion and rushed out. Li A-Shi then seized the opportunity to escape. At the same time, Qiu returned home and was shocked by the news. He immediately reported it to the Shanzhong Road Police Station. Upon hearing the news, the police chief immediately ordered detectives to investigate and tracked Li to his residence, but Li had already vanished without a trace. The body of Qiu's son was reported for inspection today.

Woman Cries for Help by the Pond

American Sailor Brazen and Shameless

Around 9 o'clock last night, near a small pond in the French Park on Hualong Road in the French Concession, a woman suddenly cried for help. Marrying a Wife Under the Pretense of a Nephew

In Reality, He is Taking a Concubine Himself

Li Qianyi Sues Jin Qidi

Requests a Judgment to Dissolve the Marriage Contract

Lian Di Herself Willing to be a Concubine

Official Advises Out-of-Court Settlement

Li Qianyi, a resident of Tianjin, lives at No. 6 outside the Southeast Gate of Zhenru Town. He has a second daughter named Lian Di, who is sixteen years old. In February of this year, through matchmakers Zuo Kuiyuan and an old woman named Chen Yaoshi, she was promised in marriage to Jin Qidi (also known as Jin Zhixian), the nephew of No. 96, Dajin Lane, Zhoujiaqiao, in the western suburbs of Shanghai.

Jin Marries Her as a Concubine: It was stated that the bride price was 400 yuan. On March 17, 200 yuan was paid as an initial payment, and the remaining 200 yuan was to be paid later. Lian Di was immediately brought into the family. Unexpectedly, she was not betrothed to Qidi's nephew but was taken by Qidi as

His Third Concubine: They were married on the 20th of last month. Li Qianyi was greatly surprised to learn the truth. He believed that Jin Qidi should not have deceived them into the betrothal, using the name of marrying his nephew to take her as his own concubine. Therefore, he hired lawyer Hu Yuanjun to file a complaint with the local court, requesting

Dissolution of the Marriage Contract: The defendant, Jin Qidi, also hired lawyer Lu Jiazi to present a defense. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhang Jinjian specially opened the Fourth Tribunal to hear the case. First, the plaintiff, Li Qianyi, testified that he was 46 years old, from Tianjin, previously involved in the cloth factory business, and now unemployed at home. He also stated the details of the situation and claimed that

a young man came to the matchmaking, claiming to be the defendant's nephew. He never thought that the defendant was deceiving them all along. Now, according to the matchmakers who came to his house, Jin Qidi's nephew is only 21 years old and has houses and land, which would be a good match. At the time, he asked for 600 yuan for the betrothal gift, but they agreed on 400 yuan, and he first sent 200 yuan. His daughter was immediately brought into the family. He later learned that she was actually taken as a concubine by the defendant, but his daughter is only

Sixteen Years Old: The defendant is the same age as him, 46 years old. He really does not want this and asks for the court to order the dissolution of the marriage contract, etc. The defendant, Jin Qidi, testified that he was 46 years old and a local. The judge asked how many women he had in his household. (Answer) Three: his first wife, Lu; his concubine, Min; and Xu. But Lian Di's last name is not Li but Xu because he is

Maintaining Two Ancestral Lines: and has no children. Moreover, his nephew passed away six or seven years ago. As for Lian Di coming into the family as a concubine, it was agreed upon beforehand. On January 26th of this year, he paid a betrothal gift of 212 yuan, and on April 20th, he paid another 58 yuan, totaling 270 yuan. The betrothal gifts have already been paid in full. The judge asked why he was being sued. (Answer) He does not know. At the time, the matchmaker said that Lian Di was a virgin. In reality, Lian Di was sold to

Qingdao as a Prostitute: (Asked) Are your feelings good with Lian Di? (Answer) Yes. The judge ordered Li Lian Di to come to the case to testify. She is sixteen years old and her last name is Xu, not Li. Her biological father has passed away, and she does not know Li Qianyi. (Asked) Who is Jin Qidi to you? (Answer) He is my husband. (Asked) Are you married? (Answer) No. (Asked) Who exactly is Li Qianyi to you? (Answer) He is a friend of my father. (Asked) How did you live after your father's death? (Answer) My father ran a firewood shop before his death. (Asked) Who did you give all the betrothal gifts to? (Answer) I gave them to my grandfather (referring to Li Qianyi). At this point, the plaintiff's lawyer stood up and said, "Please note, Your Honor, that Lian Di admits that the plaintiff is her father, and Lian Di also testified that she

Voluntarily Became a Concubine: etc." The judge ordered witness Chen Yaoshi to come to the case to testify. She is 60 years old and testified that Lian Di is a concubine. Zuo Kuiyuan, 39 years old, from Baoding, testified that he was indeed the matchmaker. The betrothal gift was indeed 400 yuan, and 200 yuan was paid. At the time, Lian Di was betrothed to Jin Qidi's nephew as a wife, but after coming into the family, he did not know how she became Qidi's concubine, but both parties were willing to do so, etc. The judge, upon receiving the testimony, mediated for them in court, ordering the defendant to give the plaintiff some more betrothal gifts. The plaintiff claimed that the defendant's family all smoked opium and he did not want his daughter. If they wanted to settle, then they would have to give

Another Four Hundred: Yuan, etc. The judge ordered both parties to settle out of court. If they could not come to an agreement, they would be summoned again for further questioning.

Those Who Send Letters of Extortion

Are Mostly Acquainted

Lu A-Long's Situation is Good

Fu A-Fang Intends to Extort

Arrested and Found to be an Acquaintance

Resulting in a Sentence of Three Years

Lu A-Long, a resident of Ningbo, lives at No. 521 Dithway Road in Hongkou. His situation is good, which is why he is coveted by criminal gangs. Since the 27th of last month, he suddenly received several threatening letters demanding 3,000 yuan. They said that if he agreed, they would write the words

"Heaven Emperor, Earth Emperor": on a piece of paper and paste it on the front of his house. Someone would then come with a red piece of paper to negotiate. If he did not give the money, they would write

"Heaven Red, Earth Red": as an indication, so that they could take more drastic measures. Lu reported the letters to the Harbin Police Station, asking them to investigate, and on the 30th, he pasted

a Piece of Paper on the Front Door: with the words "Heaven Emperor, Earth Red" written on it. That day, the police chief sent detectives to wait near Lu's house all day, but there was no movement. In the evening, he received another letter from the bandits, saying that the indication was ambiguous and unclear, and that it should be corrected immediately. The next morning, he sent someone to re-paste the paper with the words "Heaven Emperor, Earth Emperor." The next morning, he again ordered his son-in-law, Shao Wenjiu, to go to the police station and lead the detectives to hide in a secluded place, waiting until

Nine O'Clock When a Person Arrived: holding two red pieces of paper and a letter. Shao immediately handed the person a package wrapped in black cloth, saying that it contained 500 yuan in banknotes. The person received it and was about to leave when he was apprehended by undercover Chinese detectives Yan Aqing and Sun Yunqing. They opened the package and saw that it was full of waste paper. They took him back to the police station. According to the person, his name is Fan Nianyi, from Shaoxing, and he works as a waiter at the China Hotel at No. 91 Jiujiang Road. He was asked to pick it up by a tea server from the hotel,

Gu Zhaolin from Chongming: The detectives then arrested Gu, but Gu claimed that he was asked by two guests, surnamed Wang and Fu, who were staying in room 46 to pick up a package from that location. Because he was busy, he asked Fan to do it. At the time, the Wang person, who was staying in room 46, had already left.

Only One Fu A-Fang was Apprehended: Fu is also from Shaoxing. Yesterday morning, he was taken to the Special District Local Court along with Fan, Gu, and the letters, slips of paper, package, and other evidence. Judge Feng Shide presided over the hearing. Lu A-Long first explained the situation and said that he knew Fu A-Fang and that he had been to his house. He had never met Fan and Gu before. When questioned, Fu A-Fang completely attributed the idea to the Wang person who was on the run. Fan and Gu both claimed that they did not know anything about it beforehand. Judge Feng verified the testimony and found that

Fan and Gu Were Not Involved: He ordered their unconditional release. Fu A-Fang was sentenced to three years in prison. The threatening letters and red paper were confiscated.
