Da Yaoxian's

Defense Against the Police's Accusations of Illegality

Letter to the Bar Association

Lawyer Da Yaoxian, who handled the Wang Desheng case, was accused by the police lawyer of exceeding his authority and instigating a confession. This was reported in yesterday's newspaper. Now, lawyer Da has sent a letter to the Bar Association, stating the truth of the matter because the facts were not entirely consistent. The original letter is as follows: Respectfully, when our member was performing his duties, he was accused of "illegal behavior" by the police lawyer Wang Yaotang. The details of the matter are listed below. Wang Desheng was sued by the Huisi Police Station in the Shanghai Special District Local Court for the Zhou Dingwen threatening letter case. The second court date was May 31st in the morning. Our member, having been appointed by Wang Desheng's wife, as is customary, inquired about the details of the case to the parties involved. He contacted the police station to inquire about this matter. At 9:30, the police lawyer and the police chief had not yet arrived. Our member, needing to file a complaint, was concerned that it would be too late if he delayed any further. Therefore, he presented Wang Wang's letter of appointment to the Chinese police officer in charge of the waiting room and asked to see his client, Wang Desheng. He inquired about the details of the case and asked him to sign the letter of appointment. Later, at the request of the family, Wang Wang, he asked him, "Have you suffered?" Wang Desheng heard this, and tears streamed down his face. He cried and said that he had been interrogated and tortured by the police for more than five times, forcing him to admit to the items written on the confession, which were in fact written by them and did not conform to the facts. He was also accused of other crimes that he had never even heard of. He owns a shop and has always contracted with major merchants for various paint works and does not have time to deal with other matters. He also said that this time he was falsely accused because his friend Mao Qingde, nicknamed San Mapis, was a matchmaker and had a feud, colluding with the police to fabricate this unfortunate false accusation, etc. Our member, believing in justice and protecting the interests of the parties involved, instructed him to tell the judge the truth during the interrogation and not to suffer under duress and falsely confess to untrue matters that would harm himself. The judge should also make a judgment based on his own confession. You should choose between the death penalty and torture. When our member spoke, he spoke loudly and clearly. Not only was the Chinese police officer in charge present, but other defendants being held were also present, which can be used as evidence. Unexpectedly, the police officers who handled the case knew about it and were jealous, adding and subtracting facts and reporting them to the police lawyer Wang Yaotang of the case. Lawyer Wang then publicly accused our member of "illegal behavior." Our member responded that the police representative had not arrived in court by 9:30, and that he had asked the police officer in charge to see his client with a letter of appointment. This was a last resort. Now, in order to protect the interests of his client, the lawyer could guide him to tell the truth. If Wang Desheng had been tortured and forced to confess falsely by the police, he should tell the judge about it. Our client's life must not be sacrificed for the police's trap and cannibalistic tactics to gain promotion, etc. Later, during the interrogation, Lawyer Wang first told Judge Sun Yuan about our member's "illegal behavior" and cited Chinese police officers No. 245 and No. 818 to describe the matter, including falsely accusing our member of claiming to have obtained permission from the police to enter and instigating a counter-confession. Judge Sun then approved "Reschedule the interrogation of the concealment of crime part to next Saturday morning and send it to the prosecutor for investigation." The above is the details of the matter. According to our member, he accepted the case of the parties involved for a public fee of 100 yuan. Regardless of the truth of the accused facts, it is customary to inquire about the confession and to persuade the parties involved to make a truthful confession. Moreover, he spoke loudly and clearly in public, with everyone watching. He was then envied by the police officers for questioning, torturing, and forcing a confession, and the lawyer was accused of the strange thing of concealing a crime. In fact, the party involved, Wang Desheng, had denied all the facts in the first interrogation, which can be found in the records and newspapers. Our member's life, honor, and disgrace are not worth mentioning, but it is also too insulting to the authority of our colleagues in the legal profession. Since returning to the country, our member has served as a lawyer in the temporary court of the former Mixed Court for many years. He has also seen the foreign forces of the past doing things against the trend. However, he has never seen any shocking strange phenomena. At a time when the courts are being taken back, there are various unfortunate facts that are unexpected disasters. Because this matter concerns the authority of all our colleagues, please send a committee to investigate the facts and make a legal claim. Thank you very much. To the Shanghai Bar Association Executive Committee, Member Da Yaoxian. June 2nd, 19th year of the Republic of China.

They then submitted a request to the Anti-Smuggling Department of the Ministry of Finance to strictly order the issuance. It was approved, and all the facts of Zhang Tianji's illegal embezzlement and dereliction of duty during his tenure were listed to various officials to expose his bad deeds. Zhang knew that Zheng Fuyu, the director of the document section, was aware of all the evidence of his malpractice. He initially asked old friend Lu Xiquan to mediate, ostensibly promising to issue a portion of the private case rewards first, in order to lure the evidence of his malpractice. On the one hand, he framed and falsely accused Zheng in the police station, in order to carry out his conspiracy to strike first. Why Go to a Hotel to Discuss Marriage?

Cai Huilong Clearly Had Ulterior Motives

Sentenced to One Month in Prison, Allowed to Redeem the Sentence

Zhou Lu, a woman who lives near Tangjiawan in the French Concession, has a nineteen-year-old daughter, Zhou Jinxiu, who works in a sock factory. A male employee of the factory, Cai Huilong, enticed her to a hotel and intended to commit illegal acts. The woman's brother learned about it and reported it to the police station, ordering detectives to go and arrest Cai and Jinxiu together. Yesterday, they were sent to the French court for questioning. The plaintiff, the woman's mother, Zhou Lu, complained about the situation. When questioned, Cai Huilong said that he and Zhou Jinxiu worked in the same factory. Jinxiu voluntarily wanted to marry him, so he asked her to go to the hotel to discuss the matter of marriage. He had no intention of committing adultery. He was accidentally seen by a co-worker, who told the plaintiff and reported it to the police. However, he usually talked to Jinxiu often at the factory, which caused jealousy among other co-workers. He asked for leniency. When Zhou Jinxiu was questioned, her confession was similar. Judge Zhu Cheng told the defendant, Cai Huilong, that if you want to know about marriage, it is a legitimate thing and there is no need to go to a hotel to discuss it. It is clear that you had bad intentions. Cai was sentenced to one month in prison and allowed to redeem his sentence.

Willing to Pay His Rent

Unwilling to Pay Alimony

Xie Zhaoxian, from Guangdong (previously reported as Xie Guixian), rented a two-story house at No. 905 Weihai Lane, Weihai Road, after taking a concubine, as a place to hide his mistress, treating his first wife, Liang Lianzhi, as a stranger. Little Sanzi's Siblings are Detestable

Passenger Jumps into River Midstream

Accused of Theft, Ordered to Compensate

Unable to Raise Funds, Driven to Despair

The No. 9 ferry owned by Zhou A’gen, which operates between the Puxi Customs Wharf and the Pudong Chunjiang Wharf, was loading passengers at the Puxi Wharf yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, heading back to Pudong. As the boat reached the center of the river, a hawker selling Rendan (a type of medicine) began to call out his wares. At the same time, a young passenger offered to buy some. Just as the transaction was taking place, the passenger suddenly threw down his white straw hat and jumped into the river, intending to commit suicide. After sinking, he resurfaced briefly, but before a rescue could be mounted, he was lost to the bottom of the river, never to resurface. Afterwards, the boatman sent the deceased's two companions and the abandoned straw hat to the Customs River Police. He lived at No. 13 Haixing Road in Pudong, and his wife worked at the Rihua Cotton Mill in Lujiazui. They heard that Liu had gone to visit a friend surnamed Wang in Desheng Lane, Haixing Road, the day before yesterday. Afterwards, the Wang family discovered the theft of two gold rings, a gold hairpin, and a child's bracelet. They accused Liu of the theft, so they asked someone surnamed He from Xiangfen Lane to negotiate. Liu was asked to compensate the Wang family thirty yuan in silver dollars to settle the matter. This suicide was likely due to his inability to raise the funds to pay the compensation. The police chief verified the statement and ordered that the person surnamed He, who acted as mediator, be brought to the police station for further investigation.

Worker Dies Tragically

His Wife Unsure What to Say

Only Stated That the Family Was Quite Poor

Did Not Dare to Request Compensation

Yang Wencai, a worker at a certain wharf in Pudong, fell from a scaffold the day before yesterday while working, landing on some wood by the river and suffering extremely severe injuries. He was taken to Tongren Hospital, but died en route. The police ordered a vehicle to transport the body to the morgue. Yesterday morning, Inspector Xu from the Special District Court arrived at the morgue to examine the body. He confirmed that the body was placed in the public area. Yang’s wife stated that she was twenty-six years old and lived in Gaochang Temple. Her husband had died tragically, and the family was very poor. Inspector Xu asked if she had any intentions, but she seemed unsure of what to say and did not dare to ask the court for compensation, only stating that her husband’s death was very tragic and she wished to claim the body. Inspector Xu ruled that the deceased, Yang Wencai, had indeed died from falling while working. According to the wife's statement, she requested to collect the body for burial and had no other requests. This was approved.

Autopsy of a Woman Burned to Death

At the home of Cai Aqing, No. 869 Huade Road, at 2:50 AM on the night of the 24th of last month, a fire broke out. Cai's aunt, Mrs. Pan, was severely burned. She was taken to the hospital for treatment, but died at 3:00 PM the day before yesterday. The police transferred the body to the morgue. Yesterday morning, Inspector Xu Mei from the Special District Court arrived to examine the body and confirmed that it was placed in the public area. According to Cai Aqing's statement, he requested to claim the body for burial. Inspector Xu ordered that the body be handed over to Cai Aqing upon signing a guarantee, for collection and burial.

Two Notorious Thieves Die in Prison

Notorious thieves Chen Jinren and Zhao Weichuan were arrested by the police and handed over to the court. Chen was sentenced to thirteen years and Zhao to fifteen years. Both were sent to the Tilanqiao Prison to serve their sentences. Recently, the two thieves became seriously ill. Chen died at 4:00 PM the day before yesterday. Both bodies were sent to the morgue. Yesterday morning, Inspector Xu from the Special District Court confirmed that they had died from illness and ordered the Pushan Hall to collect the bodies for burial.

Mao Genyang Wounds Wife in Abdomen with Knife

Was it Intentional Injury?

The Injured Party's Statement Will Be Taken

Mao Genyang, a Ningbo native who sells beef at a stall in the Huade Road market, owed his sister, Ge Mao, money. The day before the Dragon Boat Festival, his sister ordered her brother, Quanyang, to collect the debt and demand high interest. Genyang was furious. After closing his stall, at 6:30 PM in the evening, he intended to go to his sister's house to argue, but his wife, Zhong, tried to stop him. In the ensuing commotion, Mrs. Zhong's waist was injured by the sharp knife used for cutting beef, causing profuse bleeding. The Huishan Police were notified and sent detectives to rush to the scene. They took Mrs. Zhong to Guangren Hospital for treatment and detained Genyang. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Special District Local Court and charged with assault. Mrs. Zhong's injury was severe, posing a threat to her life, so she could not appear in court. Her son, Mao Qianchang, brother, Mao Quanyang, and Mrs. Zhong's sister, Zhong Caifeng, were all summoned to court. Regarding whether Mao Genyang intended to harm his wife, they all said they did not know. Genyang claimed that his wife held him and did not allow him to go to his sister's house. He wanted to break free, causing him to knock against the knife on the refrigerator, which fell and injured his wife's waist. He added that his wife did not cry out in pain at the time, so he did not pay attention. He only learned of the arrest when he returned from his sister's house. The court ordered the defendant to be detained and to wait for a statement from the injured party from the hospital before further verification.

Worker Zhang Jinkui Electrocuted to Death

The Public Utilities Bureau Pays Close Attention

Zhang Jinkui, a tire-fitting worker at the Shanghai South Public Bus Company garage, was using a motor pump supplied by the Asiatic Petroleum Company to inflate tires at 6:00 AM on May 19th when he was suddenly electrocuted and fainted. Driver Chen Jinrong saw him and rushed him to Southeast Hospital for an injection before transferring him to Shanghai Hospital. However, he died due to prolonged exposure to electricity. Upon receiving the report, the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau immediately sent personnel to investigate and took the faulty air compressor to the bureau for inspection. It was found that its insulation was above 220,000 ohms, which met the required standard. How the worker was electrocuted to death at the time could not be determined after the fact. However, the garage's electrical equipment was deemed to have some deficiencies that needed to be rectified for safety. It is reported that the bureau will soon send personnel to the garage to inspect its electrical equipment and supervise the improvements. The company has already been instructed to take note of this matter.

Grand Opening of Competition

Second Competition This Thursday

Added Amateur Chinese Program

The arrival of eleven members of the world motorcycle daredevil team in Shanghai has been repeatedly reported. The opening night was held the night before last at the cinder track specially built in Shen Garden. Thousands of spectators attended, a grand and bustling scene. This skill was particularly commendable, and their spirit of courage and adventure matched the term "daredevil team." The audience was both thrilled and applauded, exclaiming at the incredible skill. The second competition will be held this Thursday (the 5th) starting at 9:15 PM. Mr. Li will be able to provide detailed information on the vehicles used and training procedures. This amateur competition is not just for this week's race, but will continue permanently in the future.

Lawsuit Over Copyright of Modern Novel Selection

Asia & Co. and Kaiming Bookstore

Had Reached a Settlement But Each Unwilling to Yield

Now the Plaintiff Must Provide Evidence

Asia & Co. collected the best of modern novels and compiled them into a volume entitled "Selection of Modern Chinese Novels," which was printed and sold. Six other publishers, including Kaiming Bookstore, sued Asia & Co. for copyright infringement. The Special District Local Court previously summoned the parties for trial. The defendant engaged lawyers Jiang Rong and Xu Shihao to defend them. The court ordered them to settle out of court, but neither party was willing to give ground, and the settlement failed. Yesterday morning, Judge Yang continued the trial. The plaintiff's lawyers argued that the plaintiff had already applied for registration of the published works and had obtained copyright. The defendant's lawyers argued that although the plaintiff had applied for registration, it was not yet clear whether it had been approved. Therefore, the plaintiff could not bring a lawsuit against others. The case should first be decided on whether the plaintiff could file a lawsuit. Furthermore, there was no sufficient evidence of the copyright prior to applying for registration. Therefore, even if the plaintiff's books had been registered, the procedure was improper, not to mention that it was still uncertain whether it had been approved. Each side held its ground and argued. Judge Yang ordered the plaintiff to present evidence of registration and adjourned the trial for another day.

Sorrowful Passing of Dr. Shih Fei-pi

Dr. Shih Fei-pi was originally from Huangmei County, Hubei Province. She was the third sister of Dr. Shih Mei-yu, from a prominent family with a long tradition of scholarship. Her father founded the Jiujiang Christian Church. Dr. Shih received her early education from her mother and then entered the Jiujiang Ruli Girls' School. She graduated at the age of eighteen and went to the American Gaoqiao Women's University, where she graduated with the best academic record, ranking first. The school awarded her a scholarship for the most outstanding achievement to continue her medical studies at Johns Hopkins University, where she received her Doctor of Medicine degree. She then interned at Worcester City Hospital. In 1919, she returned to China and was hired as the director of the Jiujiang Maternity and Children's Hospital. In 1920, she came to Shanghai with her sister, Mei-yu, and founded the Bethel Hospital and nursing and obstetrics schools. She began practicing medicine in Shanghai and, within a year, her reputation grew significantly. Thousands of people from far and wide sought medical treatment from her each year, and hundreds of students sought admission to her schools. Dr. Shih did not spare her efforts, seeing patients day and night. Regardless of their wealth or social status, she treated them with dedication once she was consulted. She taught her students, whether they were intelligent or dull, with kindness and guidance. She worked so diligently for seven years, performing five to six deliveries and making four to five house calls every day. In addition to her dozens of outpatient visits and seeing patients at Bethel Hospital, she personally taught her students, tirelessly imparting knowledge. She never ate on time. As a result, she was exhausted. In 1926, she went to Europe for treatment, but her condition did not improve. She returned to China in 1927 and then went to Korea for recuperation, but her illness was too severe and incurable. Her body had been ailing for four years and never fully recovered. She finally passed away at 2:00 PM on May 29th of this year. Dr. Shih was known for her kindness and never sought fame or fortune. She died at the young age of forty. Her funeral was held at Bethel Hospital at 2:00 PM last Saturday, and she was buried at the Hongqiao Road International Cemetery at 5:00 PM. Important figures such as Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek and his wife, Minister Kong and his wife, and Minister Song and his wife all sent wreaths. Medical professionals such as Niu Huilin and his wife personally attended the funeral. More than a thousand people from all walks of life attended the funeral.

Reply Regarding Pigment Industry Contract Case

The pigment department of the German firm Lihe Foreign Firm in this city and Ma Shangjie, the owner of Shangda Pigment Company, a member of the Pigment and Indigo Industry Association, entered into a goods contract (for lake-colored pigment). Due to the sharp decline in the gold pound, disputes arose, attracting the attention of the entire pigment industry and society in general, as reported in this newspaper. The case was referred by Yang Yi, Judge of the Civil Court of the Special District Court, to the Pigment Industry Association for mediation. After receiving the order, the association sent a letter to the firm, setting the date of the 28th of last month for the firm to send a responsible representative to attend the mediation. Subsequently, the firm replied by letter refusing, showing contempt for the dignity of our country's judiciary, which caused great indignation. The association submitted a reply to the Special District Court, stating: "Regarding the reply of the association, on the 26th of last month, Yang, Judge of the Civil Court of your court, ordered that the case of a dispute between Ma Shangjie of Shangda Pigment Company, a member of our association, and Lihe Foreign Firm regarding a goods contract, be mediated by our association by summoning both parties involved. After receiving this order, our association sent a letter to Lihe Foreign Firm requesting them to send a responsible representative to attend the meeting on the 28th of the same month for mediation. Subsequently, the firm replied by letter refusing, clearly violating the order of the judge of your court, showing contempt for the dignity of our country's judiciary. The main points of the original dispute can be summarized as follows: (1) The method of Lihe Foreign Firm, due to the sharp decline in the gold pound, intends to default on the goods, displaying the imperialist firm's reliance on power to undermine our country's weak commerce, fabricating deceptive arguments, and lacking genuine reasons for the dispute. (2) On the side of Ma Shangjie, the goods contract signed with the firm should be performed based on material evidence according to legal, customary, and commercial practices, which is verifiable. There is no precedent for requiring additional written documents beyond the original evidence. The plaintiff and defendant have been trading goods for more than ten years without any such illegal practice. Furthermore, the pigment industry in this city has never heard of such an eccentric and perverse custom. Taking a step back, even if the contract contains English records, it is as if this type of contract between Chinese and foreigners is a mere formality. Questioned in this way, Lihe Foreign Firm would likely be speechless and unable to justify itself, contradicting itself and revealing flaws. If, unfortunately, they are allowed to proceed with their deception, and this precedent is set, it will cause major disputes in society and the judiciary, and the future of Chinese merchants will be in great danger. Furthermore, after this case occurred, not only did the pigment industry in the city, whose interests were directly affected, rise up in anger, but public opinion was also unusually agitated. The association's concern for the interests of its members is minor compared to the harm caused by the taking and discarding of contracts between Chinese and foreigners throughout Shanghai and China, undermining our country's commercial rights. Our association feels a lump in its throat and cannot remain silent, and dares to appeal and submit this reply, hoping that the court will consider the law, commercial practices, and carefully review the facts, illuminating the truth and eliminating the evil. We also ask that this be forwarded to Judge Yang Yi to make a ruling in accordance with the law, so as to uphold the judiciary and protect national rights. We are extremely grateful."

A Tragic Scene in a Hospital

French Woman Jumps to Her Death

A certain French woman residing in the Wangjiazai Garden had been suffering from a nervous disorder. Two weeks ago, she attempted suicide by drinking spirits and was sent by her family to Baolong Hospital on Baike Road for treatment, where she was placed in room 304 on the third floor. Unfortunately, her illness was deep-seated and showed no signs of improvement. Yesterday morning, her maid brought her breakfast, which she reluctantly ate. After a while, her mother came to the hospital to visit her. They talked for about an hour until around 10:00 AM, when her mother left. About ten minutes later, the woman suddenly changed her demeanor, sat up in bed, walked to the window, opened it, and jumped out towards the courtyard. People noticed, but it was already too late to save her. Her mother was informed and rushed to the hospital, but the woman had already passed away. She cradled her lifeless body and wept loudly, touching the hearts of all who heard. The deceased was about twenty-eight or twenty-nine years old. Her parents visited her every day, often three or four times.

Settlement of Edison Factory Strike

Full Resumption of Work Expected Today

Some Workers Entered Factory Yesterday

The strike by workers at the General Electric Edison bulb factory on Roberts Road in western Shanghai, in protest against the factory's dismissal of workers and demanding improved treatment, has lasted for a week. Through the efforts of Party, government, and police agencies to mediate between labor and management, progress has been smooth. The factory informed all workers a few days ago that they should return to work starting yesterday. A portion of the workers entered the factory at around 7:00 AM. Beforehand, Ren Lupiing, the district chief of the Caogadu 6th District Public Security Bureau, ordered all police officers to take good care of the factory vicinity and maintain order. All went well. At lunchtime, there was a disturbance among the female workers, but it was quickly resolved with the care of the police officers. District Chief Ren, along with representatives from the Party headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau, personally persuaded and comforted the workers. The workers agreed to resume work in full starting today. The labor union issued a notice to the workers, instructing them to enter the factory together at 10:00 AM this morning. All pending conditions will be addressed by Party, government, and police officials in negotiations with the factory. Therefore, the Edison factory workers are expected to resume work in full today.

Fresh Meat Industry Association Reorganization Committee Meeting

The Shanghai Fresh Meat Industry Association held its third reorganization committee meeting yesterday at the Xiangxue Hall of the Yuyuan Garden at the City God Temple. Huang Yexin was elected chairman, and the proceedings followed the established protocol. The following resolutions were made: (1) All properties and contracts of the Xiangxue Hall and Chengren Hall will continue to be managed by the original handlers during the reorganization period. (3) For the market shutdown in Pudong, the two standing representatives Huang Yexin and Shen Xie will be instructed to discuss with the reorganization committee to request upper-level concern for the difficulties of the merchants and to build a slaughterhouse at a suitable location. Until it is completed, they will be allowed to operate as usual. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Continued Rise in Intestinal Market Prices

Chinese livestock intestines (i.e., pig and sheep small intestines) are exported to Europe and America and are a major export commodity. The raw materials, in addition to those from Jiangsu and Zhejiang, are mostly produced in northern Anhui and southern Henan. Therefore, large factories such as Lishunji have established branches there to produce semi-finished products, which are then shipped to Shanghai for reprocessing and then exported to Europe and America. The current value of gold is soaring, and foreign merchants are calculating that it is profitable. Yihua and other firms have been sending telegrams to procure goods. Therefore, the price of first-class spot goods has risen by three to four cents per pair. However, the inventory in Shanghai is low, and there is a market but no goods. The goods from Anhui and Henan cannot be shipped to Shanghai due to the impact of the war. Therefore, the market price is expected to continue to rise.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory issued the following weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday: The sky is cloudy, indicating a change. The south wind in Shandong is light and very undirected. A low-pressure system is approaching the Sea of Japan, followed by a high-pressure system that will cause a strong northwest wind in Korea and the Bohai Sea area. The highest temperature in this city in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday was 90.0 degrees, and the lowest was 68.2 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 88.3 degrees and the lowest was 55.0 degrees.

Special Issue Commemorating the Anti-Opium Campaign, Edited by the Anti-Opium Committee

Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Instructions Regarding the Prohibition of Opium

"The business of opium absolutely cannot coexist with the national government that has the power granted by the people. The will of the Chinese people is to oppose opium. Anyone who advocates allowing the business of opium by law, or who expresses submission to the evil forces of opium, is a public enemy of the people. The war against opium must absolutely not be compromised. If the responsible government agency lowers its flag and ceases fighting opium for its own private convenience, even temporarily, it is an act of treason. To achieve the goal of opium prohibition, a nationally consistent plan that is followed by all must be adopted by the national government. However, before the warlords are overthrown and the civil government can unify the country, anti-opium organizations must persevere and not abandon the determination to fight with perseverance and without compromise, and must always adopt a thorough and uncompromising policy."

Introduction by Zhang Zhijiang

This special issue is dedicated to the gracious words and valuable insights provided by comrades of the Party and the Nation. These contributions greatly benefit the people and are of significant value. On behalf of the Anti-Smoking Committee, I extend our deepest gratitude.

The work of banning opium relies on two critical areas. On the one hand, the government must diligently enforce the prohibition. On the other hand, the public must awaken and voluntarily quit. Only through the cooperation of both sides can we hope to achieve complete success. In the past, when asked about the results of the ban, government agencies were, of course, deeply ashamed. However, aside from the enthusiastic efforts of anti-drug organizations, the majority of the public seemed to remain in a dream. How heartbreaking and painful this is. Yet, it is not surprising. According to the principle that practice is easy, but knowledge is difficult, the public does not yet understand. How can we blame them for not practicing?

June 3rd - Discipline

Continuing the Spirit of June 3rd to Thoroughly Eliminate the Scourge of Opium

He Yingqin

The work of the Anti-Smoking Committee, in addition to supervising the implementation of the ban by the provincial and municipal governments in accordance with the law, includes the important task of publicity. The publication of this special issue on Discipline Day is one aspect of this publicity effort. It is hoped that prominent individuals across the country will offer guidance on the progress of this work, and that insightful and significant articles will continue to flow in. These contributions will be compiled into a volume and distributed among the people. I also represent the people in thanking you for your generosity.

Inscription for the Special Anti-Smoking Issue by Wang Chonghui

The Anti-Smoking Committee has published a special issue on June 3rd Discipline Day to expand publicity and raise national awareness. When asked for my thoughts, I believe that the harm of opium has a long history. Before the Yuan and Ming dynasties, it was regarded as a precious product for nourishing life and stopping disease. However, it was only used as a medicine, unlike later generations when addiction became prevalent and poisoned society. By the early Qing Dynasty, its harm gradually spread. During the Yongzheng and Qianlong reigns, prohibitions were issued. During the Daoguang reign, Mr. Lin Zexu recognized the harm of opium and requested a strict ban. He seized and destroyed opium that British merchants had brought. The British used this as a pretext for war. The Qing government’s response was ill-conceived. Mr. Lin was severely punished, leading to the Treaty of Nanjing and the loss of national sovereignty.

The poison of opium is hotter than fire and deeper than water. It destroys your industry, wastes your time, and must be resisted with determination. The foundation of national salvation lies in this prohibition.

Inscription by Xu Shiying

The situation has never recovered and the nation has fallen as a result. The scourge of opium has become even more severe. The National Government has established its capital in Nanjing, and has specifically set up the Anti-Smoking Committee to handle the matter. June 3rd has been designated as a day of commemoration. Now the government has shown determination to govern diligently and start anew, and has strictly laid out regulations. The eradication of the scourge of opium lies in the resolute actions of the entire nation. While enforcing the law and eliminating harm is the responsibility of the government, summoning courage and striving for strength lies in the self-awareness and revitalization of the national spirit. The active publicity efforts of social organizations will not only be highly effective, but also lead to swift success. What is past cannot be changed, but what is to come can still be pursued. I am willing to encourage this together with the people.

Future Paths for Implementing the Opium Ban

Wang Boqun

Tracing the harm of opium in our country, it spans hundreds of years. In recent times, its poison has become increasingly severe, surpassing the calamities of war and epidemic disease. When considering the reasons for our nation's long-term weakness, the harm caused by opium is the greatest. For over a decade, the orders banning opium have been quite strict, and the anti-drug movement has been quite vigorous. However, the scourge of opium has increased rather than decreased year after year. Not only are sales openly conducted in the inland provinces, with opium addicts used as a source of profit, but major cities also harbor filth and accept dirt, treating the ban as a mere formality. Despite the government's repeated orders and

The poison of opium is indeed a form of imperialism bewitching China, humiliating the Yellow Race, and causing us to stoop. We must bravely extricate ourselves, become angry, and strive for self-improvement to reverse the decline and wash away past humiliations.

repeated instructions, opium users remain ignorant and oblivious. If this continues, our nation will be trapped in an irrecoverable state. When considering national construction, which is at its initial stage, the people should be working hard to produce in order to develop the people's livelihood. At a time when foreign insults are becoming increasingly urgent, the people should be training their bodies to strengthen the race. Thoughts on the Opium Ban by Zhang Wohua

The Anti-Smoking Committee is publishing a special issue on the occasion of the upcoming June 3rd Commemoration to expand publicity. I, Wohua, have been asked to contribute my thoughts. I humbly quote:

Sun Yat-sen stated that those who engage in the opium business are public enemies of the people and acts of treason. How magnificent are his words! We must uphold

Sun Yat-sen's teachings and deeply and strictly remember these words. If we do not jointly devise fundamental measures to completely eliminate the scourge of opium, how can we fulfill Sun Yat-sen's unfinished mission of eradicating opium? Since opium flowed into China, it has been more than a hundred years. It has harmed the nation and the people more than anything else. It has not only had a significant impact on the economy, but it has also weakened the race. The label of "sick man of East Asia" is largely due to this. Since the Republic of China, opium prohibition ordinances have been promulgated many times and have been vigorously enforced, but it has been repeated many times. Those who ban ban, but those who plant still plant. June 3rd Anti-Smoking Day Special Edition Title

Alas! Our compatriots are sinking into the darkness, unable to see the light of day.

Suddenly, a bright star appears in the wilderness, illuminating the world, and evil spirits hide.

What is this bright star? It is the secret treasure of Hongwen, cleansing away filth and saving the masses.

The compassionate boat of the sea of suffering is a widespread salvation for the people. Guangzhou looks back and rallies its spirit.

Respectfully inscribed by Song Ziwen

Those who transport still transport, and those who sell and smoke still sell and smoke. Not only has the toxic atmosphere not been cleared, but it has also continued to grow and increase. The reason for this is that during the warlord era, while anti-smoking agencies were nominally established, they actually disregarded the laws and even encouraged the people to plant opium in order to extract illegal income. Some even ordered each county to plant a certain number of acres of opium seedlings, rewarding those who exceeded the quota and punishing those who fell short. The greed and dereliction of duty of those in power were like this. Moreover, treacherous merchants and local traffickers used the military and police as their protectors. Opium dens and opium transport businesses initially acted secretly, but then became openly unscrupulous. Dishonest officials colluded and divided the spoils, turning a blind eye. Even those who were truly serious about investigating and banning opium found themselves unable to act alone and dared not offend those in power. The disregard for the opium ban by those below was also like this. It is truly a great lament. However, these are the facts of the past. Now, the National Government has established an Anti-Smoking Committee, and all anti-smoking laws and regulations are thorough and comprehensive, needing no further elaboration. Banning opium requires four essential elements: prohibiting planting, transporting, selling, and smoking. Everyone knows this. Prohibiting planting, transporting, and selling are the most fundamental measures. If those who plant opium can be severely punished according to the law and the opium seedlings can be eradicated, and if those who transport and sell opium can be strictly searched and prevented from escaping the law, then the source will be cut off and the smoking addicts will naturally quit. It is hoped that the anti-smoking administrators and all anti-drug comrades across the country will be determined to eliminate evil, implement the National Government's opium prohibition policy, supervise anti-smoking officials in various places, and work hard. On the part of the people, those who are addicted should sincerely quit, and those who are not addicted should encourage each other to abstain, using their strong and resolute power to eliminate the scourge of opium, in order to realize

Sun Yat-sen's legacy of rejecting drugs. This is what Wohua sincerely prays for. In the past, Lin Wenqing, seeing the prevalence of the opium scourge, stated that if this scourge is not eliminated, China will have no usable soldiers or funds in a few decades. He then decisively punished corrupt officials who sheltered foreign and local opium merchants, and burned all the opium that the British merchants had imported. His noble spirit and heroic actions are still remembered today. We, as comrades, uphold the revolutionary spirit and embrace the concept of strengthening the race. Compared to our predecessors, how can we allow ourselves to be outdone? Let us eliminate the scourge of opium, and we will wait and see!

On Commemorating Lin Zexu by Wang Weifan

Two figures from non-revolutionary times are perpetually commemorated by the National Government: Confucius, whose birthday is August 27th, and Lin Zexu, who destroyed British opium on June 3rd. Confucius's vision of the Great Unity established the ultimate goal of the revolution, making commemoration appropriate. Lin Zexu was merely a Qing official. However, he was able to disregard personal gain and loss in a non-revolutionary environment and actively fight against imperialism and wage a deadly battle against opium. These actions serve as a model for our revolutionary comrades, inspiring feelings of shame for falling short. This is truly a model for our party comrades. This is the reason why the National Government designated the Opium Prohibition Commemoration Day. Although, over the past thousands of years, only Lin Zexu has been able to be placed alongside Confucius and receive such great importance in today's revolutionary era. Alas, Lin Zexu is truly honored!

The Opium Ban Over the Past Year by Zhong Ketuo

Time flies, and years pass quickly. This year's June 3rd Opium Prohibition Commemoration Day is a year away from last year's June 3rd 90th Anniversary of Lin Zexu's. In this past year, what has been the situation regarding the opium ban? This is something that the people of the country want to know, and I, serving in the anti-opium organization, am most happy to report. Today is the day of the publication of a special issue on the sixth and third anti-smoking commemoration, and I am not afraid to be wordy, and I will report to the elders, brothers, sisters and sisters all over the country.

Sun Yat-sen's legacy of resisting drugs states: "There can be absolutely no compromise on the issue of opium." In the past year, although the committee's measures could not be fully implemented according to plan due to frequent military activities and a harsh environment, it still adhered to the spirit of drug resistance and did not dare to relax. Here are the most important aspects of the opium ban in the past year, covering nine things:

The poison of poppy is more poisonous than a collapsing river. The whole country is dying, raise your voice, wake up the stubborn, end the descendants, and save the whole.

（一） Regarding Opium Ban Policies: Last year, a timetable for work during the period of political tutelage was drafted. It detailed how the opium ban work should be allocated and carried out. It is still under review by the Central Political Council. Once approved, it will be implemented in an orderly manner. In addition, the rules for the implementation of the opium ban law stipulated that opium ban committees should be established in various provinces and cities, and inspection offices should be established at various important ports, all in order to eradicate the opium scourge as soon as possible and provide supervision. Although the organizational rules for the above items were drafted and sent to the court, due to the ongoing military activities and the limitation of the economy, the establishment is still slightly pending. However, the overall trend is inevitable.

（二） Regarding Opium Ban Laws and Regulations: There are more than ten items in total: （A） Opium Ban Law （B） Rules for the Implementation of the Opium Ban Law （C） Rules for the Verification of Public Servants （D） Regulations on the Performance Evaluation of Opium Ban （E） Regulations on the Inspection of Opium Seedlings by County Magistrates （F） Measures for Inspecting Ships, Vehicles, and Airplanes for Smuggling Opium （G） Regulations on the Establishment of Drug Rehabilitation Centers and Local Hospitals Handling Drug Rehabilitation Matters （H） Regulations on the Distribution of Opium Ban Fines （I） Measures for the June 3rd Opium Ban Commemoration Day （J） Simple Rules for Reviewing Accusation Documents. The above laws and regulations cover the prohibition of planting, transporting, selling, and smoking opium. Since their promulgation, they have gradually been put into practice. One example that can prove this is that the counties in western Fujian have always been opium-producing areas. Recently, Lin Shouguo, commander of the Marine Corps, together with the county magistrates, eradicated more than 10,000 acres of opium seedlings. From this, it can be seen that the formulation of opium ban laws and regulations has had a significant effect. （三） Regarding the Verification of Public Servants: Repeated requests have been sent to various agencies in the capital to reply. Verifications have been conducted separately. A total of eighty-eight people were suspected of smoking opium. They have been suspended from their posts at any time. Other provinces and cities have also handled them in order. The guarantees of the members are attached and sent to the meeting. Now, in order to eliminate malpractices, it is planned to conduct random checks and re-verifications in order to purify officialdom and set an example with the first name.

（四） Regarding Drug Rehabilitation Work: All provincial and municipal governments have now been notified to order the establishment of drug rehabilitation hospitals within a limited time, so that opium users can surrender themselves and be admitted to hospitals for drug rehabilitation, and show the government's intention to show mercy and not kill without teaching. It is expected that they will be established one after another in the shortest possible time. This is also good news for opium users. For the funds of the drug rehabilitation hospital, it is also stipulated that 20% of the fines will be used to cover it. Those who are found to have committed opium crimes must be sent to the hospital for drug rehabilitation before being convicted, because they are afraid that they will still have their addiction after they are released from prison. They have to plan a fundamental plan for removal, and also announce to the people that they must submit the collected opium paraphernalia within a limited time for collection and destruction, and make fundamental elimination.

（五） Regarding the Investigation of Opium Ban: Initially, members were sent to the three northeastern provinces, Jiangsu, Anhui, Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Hubei, Guangdong, Guangxi, Shandong, Shaanxi, Sichuan, and other provinces to investigate the opium ban situation in various places. The places where the work was neglected were corrected based on the reports. Then, members were sent to Fuzhou, Xiamen, Jinan, Qingdao, and other places to investigate the situation of Japanese ruffians poisoning China and transporting narcotic drugs. After the evidence was collected, it was reported to the League of Nations and announced in Chinese and foreign newspapers, which has won the League of Nations' attention to China's determination to ban opium. An agreement to unanimously abide by the Hague Convention has now been passed. All of these have achieved the effects of the above-mentioned investigation. It is now planned to send special commissioners to the League of Nations to jointly study international opium issues in order to deal with them.

（六） Regarding the Assessment of Opium Administration in Various Provinces: Repeated requests have been sent to various provincial and municipal governments to conduct assessments in accordance with the provisions of the Opium Ban Performance Evaluation Regulations. Those who have approved the reports to the meeting have been rewarded and punished separately according to their performance, which is to reward the meritorious and warn the ineffective.

（七） Regarding Opium Cases and Accusation Cases: The opium case statistics have been published in detail in each issue of the gazette and need not be repeated. As for the accusation case statistics, there were more than 800 cases in total in the past year, of which more than 200 were more serious and more than 600 were less serious. As long as the accusation procedure is complete, it will not be rejected.

（八） Regarding International Aspects: It is now scheduled for the International Opium Ban Committee to hold a special meeting in August, and convene an international conference on restricting narcotic drugs in Geneva on December 1. It is closely related to China's opium ban issue and should be dealt with vigorously. The Ministry of Internal Affairs, Health, and Foreign Affairs are now preparing proposals to limit the output of industrial-grade narcotic drugs to the lowest possible extent. The League of Nations is also paying close attention to the use of medicines and drugs containing narcotic drugs, and has consulted with the Ministry of Health to take action in accordance with the regulations on medicines and drugs.

（九） Regarding the Cooperation of the Party, Government, and Military: The authority of the party is higher than everything. The people of the whole country know that the association has requested the central government to order party departments at all levels to supervise the local governments where they are located to strictly implement the opium ban in order to implement the opium ban, in the hope of eradicating the opium scourge as soon as possible and using the party's authority to supervise it, so as to avoid slackness. In addition, such as requesting the Ministry of Internal Affairs to notify the land and water public security organs to crack down on and punish opium offenders, and requesting the Ministry of Military Affairs to order the military inspection stations in various places not to confiscate the opium seized without authorization, all are plans to benefit the opium ban.

The above is just a summary of the most important aspects of the opium ban. Other trivial matters related to the scope of the opium ban are even more difficult for me to enumerate. A detailed report was submitted to the government and the academy for record every month. However, due to the limited space of the special issue, it is impossible to describe the events one by one. Although it is tomorrow's yellow flower, it is not as plain as it seems. I hope that the people of the country will not look at it indifferently. In the future, I hope that the government and the people will cooperate in the spirit of cooperation, and hold the perseverance of common struggle. On the June 3rd Opium Ban Commemoration Day, they will always print it in their minds and never forget it. Then, the century-old poison will not be difficult to eradicate completely. How can we not worry about the abolition of unequal treaties with foreign countries within the time limit? And the association's planning of the opium ban in the past year will not be in vain. I would like to encourage this with the people of the whole country.

Sun Yat-sen's Anti-Drug Legacy

Preface to the June 3rd Commemoration by Chen Dezheng

The beginning of our country's conclusion of unequal treaties with foreign countries was the Treaty of Nanjing. The source of the disaster of the Treaty of Nanjing belongs to opium, which is a great disaster. Therefore, we who are striving for revolution should deeply feel that if we want to implement the abolition of unequal treaties, the first step is to start from prohibiting opium and all narcotic drugs.

Opium and all narcotic drugs are the main reasons for our country's diplomatic failure, internal affairs failure, banditry, and the rampant corruption. The spread of poison will inevitably lead to the destruction of the country and the extinction of the species. This is something that anyone can know and say. However, those who ban ban, those who sell sell, those who reject reject, and those who smoke smoke. Even now, the root cannot be blocked and the flow cannot be cut off. This is because our whole nation has not truly awakened. Now we can see the spread of poison everywhere we go. Under the rule of the revolutionary government, it has been discovered. This is something we cannot but be heartbroken about.

In recent decades, many of our people have been ruined by smoking opium. The foundation of social economy is increasingly shaken. The degree of danger can make us shiver. And from the perspective of the harm of poison, it damages the body and mind and wastes academic studies. It turns a strong and excellent nation into a sick man of East Asia. How terrible is the title? If we want to become stronger, we want to avenge ourselves, we want all the people of the country to truly wake up and unite to reject poison. It is necessary to have an agency with special responsibility to actively carry out it, so that practical results can be seen.

The Anti-Drug Association of the Republic of China has responded to our request and is doing such a difficult and important job. It has already achieved considerable results and has been praised by people all over the country. Its continued efforts to move forward are even more admired by us. Now, on the occasion of the publication of the Sixth and Third Special Edition, I am happy to say a few words, hoping to make more progress.

June 3rd Commemorative Special Issue

The opium scourge has been around for more than a hundred years. Floods and beasts are not comparable to it. Those who are harmed are like carbuncles attached to the body. The people are getting weaker and the country is getting greedier. Lin Gong's perseverance is to eliminate people, wash away filth and dirt, and not be afraid of stubbornness. June 3rd Commemoration and Our Efforts by Huang Jiahui

For more than a hundred years, imperialism has attacked weak nations with the means of plunder and annexation in order to achieve an advantageous economic position, not hesitating to shed people's blood and exterminate their species. The most cruel and sinister plan is the opium policy. Since the British used the power of warships and cannons to import opium into our country, the country has become weak and the people have become poor, and in recent years it has fallen into the position of a semi-colony. The British have succeeded in their economic invasion policy, not only filling the four treasuries, but also consolidating their position in the Far East. After that, all countries that developed to the Far East followed in the footsteps of the British and sought inspiration from the abundance of income from opium and narcotic drugs. Today, the drug scourge in our country is like a flood and cannot be contained. On this day of the Sixth and Third Burning Earth Commemoration, when we think back to Lin Gong Zexu's legacy and look at the rampant drug scourge in the country, we cannot help but shed tears. The past is gone, and the future is difficult. We should think about ways to remedy the situation and save the country's destiny. Today, those who run international opium and narcotic drugs, in addition to the giants of Britain, Germany, France, and Japan, also have small Switzerland, the Netherlands, Austria, Persia, Turkey, and so on. They are too numerous to mention. They are all putting their full effort into our country, and the evil-doer behind the scenes is still the opium culprit that Lin Gong fought but did not win ninety years ago. During the spring, I was ordered by the Anti-Drug Association of the Republic of China to travel to the colonies of various countries in Southeast Asia. The facts I heard and witnessed deeply know that the success of the colonial policy and the prosperity of the colonial government all depend on the income from opium trade. The opium tax rate for overseas Chinese in the British and Dutch colonies alone has reached more than 130 million yuan in national currency every year, and the amount of Indian-Persian opium exported from Singapore last year also exceeded 19 million taels, and 90% of those who use these poisons are our people. We who are engaged in the movement of rejecting drugs and saving the country should have a deep understanding of this enemy, make a thorough determination, and follow in Lin Gong's footsteps to attack this poison that destroys the country and exterminates the species. In order to achieve final success, we must break this inhuman conspiracy between countries. As for the poisonous seedlings that have not been cleared in the country and the opium that is full of it, they cannot be tolerated under the clear blue sky and the bright sun. We should unite as one and eliminate them completely. We should comfort Lin Gong and Sun Yat-sen's spirits in heaven, and not waste this day's commemoration every year.

Famous Quotes and Candid Remarks on the June 3rd Commemoration by Tan Yankai

The harm of opium has been around for a long time. The whole world is indulged in it, but only Marquis Lin of Fujian rose up to eliminate it. Although his ambition was not fulfilled, it is still in people's eyes and ears. He is vigorous and energetic. Now the government is vigorously implementing the opium ban. In memory of the former sages, he is spreading it to show the world the precision and sincerity of the former sages in dealing with affairs and the strategy of resisting foreign countries. His majesty is so radiant that it is beyond what we can imagine today. Who made me leak and tie up for ninety years and shake my hands and feet? Alas, alas. Although there are no old adults, there is still a model. It is still in the palm of your hand to be determined and have something to do.

Hu Hanmin

Hanmin grew up in Guangdong. As a child, he often heard people tell stories about Commissioner Lin burning opium. Later, when he studied, he saw many records of Commissioner Lin's achievements. When he was twenty, he tutored at the home of Mr. Lin's grandson, Mr. Shen, who often recounted stories of Mr. Lin. This made him admire him even more. Commentators said that Mr. Lin strictly enforced the opium ban to assert national rights and eliminate the people's suffering. Everything he did was appropriate. However, the eight characters "goods to be confiscated, people to be executed" were implemented too hastily. At first, Hanmin did not know how these eight characters were applied at the time. It was only after reading the imperial edicts of the 17th and 21st days of the ninth month of the Jihai year that he understood that foreign merchant ships were required to sign a bond. If they violated the opium ban, their goods would be confiscated and the people would be executed. The various countries had already agreed to the first four characters, but they protested only against "people to be executed." However, Mr. Lin's integrity and unwavering principles were enough to make those who had been self-deprecating and obsequious to foreigners for a hundred years blush with shame. At that time, the entire Qing court was incompetent and cowardly, and a fear of everything had become the prevailing atmosphere. It was especially rare that Mr. Lin was so upright and unyielding. The so-called "too hasty implementation" should not be considered a flaw in Mr. Lin. In his later years, when someone asked him about foreign affairs, Mr. Lin said, "England is a maritime nation. In the future, the one who will cause trouble for China will be Russia." Since the late Qing dynasty, Mr. Lin's words have seemed remarkably accurate. With his profound knowledge, he was sent to the border region, and what he saw and heard gave him foresight. However, only someone who worried about the nation for his entire life could have achieved this. Mr. Lin was not just a capable minister for a time. Today, the people are highly aware of the harm of opium. The government has established a committee to strictly manage this matter and commemorate Mr. Lin. Recalling what I saw and heard as a child, I cannot help but admire and lament.

Wang Chonghui

When Chonghui was young, he read the political writings of Lin Wenzhong and learned about the Opium War. Later, when he studied in Europe and America, people there often praised Mr. Lin's character but deeply regretted that the Qing court did not tolerate his uprightness. Chonghui often wondered about this. From Genghis Khan in the early Yuan dynasty to Wenzhong, their intention was not to invade but to seek justice. Therefore, the Opium War was actually the first cry of struggle between the Chinese nation and foreigners. In that case, Wenzhong was actually rich in anti-foreign sentiment. Yet, foreigners praised him as virtuous. Is this what is meant by justice? In a war for justice, right and wrong are more important than success or failure. Even if one fails, it is not one's fault. The people of the country would naturally feel regret and astonishment. Even foreigners would be shocked and respectful, believing that the cause of the failure lies with those who should be held responsible, and not with that person. Alas, how can this be compared to a war of anti-foreignism? After the defeat in this war, Wenzhong was slandered and died. The scourge of opium has persisted for a hundred years until today, still troubling the government with concerns about prohibition. Recalling the past deeds of Wenzhong, it is not only our country's misfortune but also the lack of justice in the world. Chonghui once read Western history. The Boston Tea Party in America was triggered by resistance to British tea taxes. At that time, the Americans threw all the tea carried by British ships into the sea. This event is very similar to Wenzhong's destruction of opium. However, America gained a Washington, won a war, and became independent from England, now hailed as a powerful nation. We lost a Lin Wenzhong, suffered a defeat in a war, and were bound by unequal treaties, which grew even more severe. Alas, although there is luck and misfortune, it is enough to see how important it is for a country to have the right person dealing with foreign affairs. The relationship is so crucial.

Wang Zhengting

A natural poison has brought disaster to China, almost causing the nation to perish. It is the second greatest scourge, like a flood or a beast. Who is greater than Lin Zexu, who knew the great harm it caused a hundred years ago and used all his strength to resist it? In the end, the Opium War exposed the inhumanity of imperialism, so that after thousands of generations, when we look back on the past, the pain remains. This can truly be said to be a contribution no less than that of Yu the Great. I have always said that in the Qing dynasty's two hundred years, Mr. Lin was the only one who knew the world situation. At that time, the deaf and blind officials were terrified by the force of the cannons and exiled Mr. Lin before surrendering and making peace. This is truly a historical tragedy, like the sudden recall of Yue Wu Mu in the Southern Song dynasty. Now, having suffered for too long and too severely, the world uses this as a warning. The people of the country are gradually becoming aware. From a state of anesthesia, they suddenly cry out loudly. The anti-drug movement has become a universal indignation. With the success of the revolution, the powers have changed their views. The British also dare not openly commit injustice. After extreme deprivation, recovery is near. Therefore, since the national government announced the anniversary of Mr. Lin's burning of opium, the people of the whole country have risen in response, singing in harmony. A grand commemoration is held to publicize the opium disaster, which is deeply engraved in the minds of our people, serving as a warning.

Outline for the Construction of the Lin Zexu Memorial Hall

Lin Zexu was the first to advocate banning opium. His heroic spirit is admired for eternity. Today, the opium disaster is rampant and even worse. We advocate rejecting drugs and fighting against the opium devil daily. Recalling the legacy of the sages and promoting their spirit, it is especially important to have appropriate commemorations to serve as models. Now, we respectfully present the following methods:

(1) This association will contact Mr. Lin's family, sympathetic organizations, and government offices to formulate detailed plans for implementation.

(2) The memorial hall will be the location for the office and meetings of this association.

(3) The memorial hall will include a library for rejecting drugs, collecting Chinese and foreign publications on rejecting drugs, both ancient and modern.

(4) The memorial hall will include an art gallery for rejecting drugs, displaying various touring exhibits of this association and other art products related to rejecting drugs.

(5) The memorial hall will include a research institute for the treatment of narcotic drugs, engaging in chemical experiments and research on drugs for quitting opium.

Dr. Wang Jingqi, the Initiator of the June 3rd Commemoration

(6) The memorial hall should include a model hospital for quitting opium, admitting opium addicts for rehabilitation.

(7) The memorial hall should set aside a portion to commemorate individuals who have made contributions to rejecting drugs, displaying photographs and commemorative plaques.

(8) Other undertakings of this association will be located here.

(9) The fundraising methods for the memorial hall can be based on the budget of each section, asking donors or organizations to separately undertake the responsibilities to facilitate the collection of funds.

(10) The construction and equipment of the memorial hall can be carried out in phases depending on the economic situation. Respectfully established by the Anti-Narcotics Association of the Republic of China.

Announcement of the August 29th Commemoration

The June 3rd commemoration was already held with great fanfare. On the one hand, it shows our country's determination to ban opium. On the other hand, it promotes the awakening of the powers. After June 3rd, there is also the August 29th commemoration—the 88th anniversary of the national humiliation when the British imperialists forced the signing of the Treaty of Nanjing after the Opium War. The Treaty of Nanjing was the beginning of unequal treaties in our country. It is an important reason for our country's diplomatic failures over the past eighty years, the lack of internal governance, the rampant bandits, and the rampant treachery. We want to complete the revolution, eliminate opium, save the nation from danger, and relieve the people's suffering. For this kind of commemoration, we should have four goals: (1) Strive for revolutionary diplomacy to abolish unequal treaties. (2) Effectively ban opium to eliminate harm to the people and wash away national humiliation. (3) Reform officialdom to eliminate the root of misleading the country and harming the people. (4) Complete the construction of the Three Principles of the People to relieve the various oppressions that our country has suffered since the signing of the Treaty of Nanjing.

Regulations for the June 3rd Essay Competition

Purpose: To promote anti-drug education and awaken students nationwide to study the scourge of opium and participate in the anti-drug movement.

Topic: Choose one of the following six topics:

(1) The responsibility of colonial governments for the opium disaster among overseas Chinese.

(2) The new awakening that the public should have when the government fails to implement the opium ban.

(3) The fundamental remedies for the opium disaster in Shanghai.

(4) The relationship between opium and our country's diplomatic failures over the past century.

(5) The responsibilities that women should bear in rejecting drugs.

(6) The lessons that Lin Zexu left us.

Style: Vernacular or classical Chinese are both acceptable.

Word Count: Limited to 5,000 words.

Eligibility: All university students at home and abroad in China are eligible to participate.

Deadline: (A) Submissions will be accepted until August 29th of this year; late submissions will not be accepted.

(B) The results will be announced during the Anti-Drug Movement Week.

As the saying goes, a national treasure flows when circulated; stagnation stops the bloodstream. The poison of opium not only harms individuals but also harms the nation's lifeline. This is what is meant by "exhausted wealth and depleted life, what else is there to wait for but death?"

Ma Xiangbo, the Elder of Hua Feng, aged ninety-one.

Judges: To be appointed by this association.

Prizes: Three essays will be selected from the submissions. The first place winner will receive a gold medal, and the second and third place winners will each receive a silver medal. In addition, if there are excellent essays, additional books published by this association will be awarded. If the essay competition committee of this association believes that there are no excellent essays, the number of selected winners may be reduced.

Submission Rules: (A) Each person is limited to one submission. (B) This essay competition emphasizes originality and practical investigation. References to other books must be listed at the end of the essay. (C) The text must be clearly written in brush; it must not be too casual. (D) The submission must include the author's detailed address, signature, seal, and a four-inch half-body photograph.

Addenda: (A) Unselected submissions will be returned with a one-dime stamp if a prior declaration is made. (B) The copyright of the selected essays belongs to this association. Established by the Anti-Narcotics Association of the Republic of China.

Commercial News

Financial Institutions Closed, Interest Rates Weak, Short-Term Loans Firm

Copper Coins Rise Again by Two Thousand

Market Overview: The day before yesterday was a national holiday, and businesses were closed as usual. Because the day before yesterday also fell on a Sunday, banks were required to observe an additional day of closure. As a result, yesterday all banks on the Bund, except for the Central Bank, were equivalent to a normal Sunday. The Jianghai Customs also collected taxes as usual, but because the banks were closed, tax revenue was very low. It is said that short-term silver loans in the money market were slightly firmer, and foreign interest rates continued to weaken.

Interest Rate Prices: (Foreign Interest Rates) The opening price was 7 yuan, 1 fen, 7 li, 7 hao, and 5 si, half a li lower than the price at the end of last month, showing a very weak trend. The afternoon price continued to drop by a fraction of a hao and 2 si, to 7 yuan, 1 fen, 7 li, 6 hao, and 2 si. It has fallen by as much as 3 to 5 li in a few days. (Silver Loans) The morning price was slightly firmer at 2 qian. The afternoon price was reduced by 3 fen, calculated as 1 qian and 7 fen. There were no market conditions for bank postings and markups.

Subsidiary Currency Market Conditions: The morning price of Jiangnan small foreign coins remained at 6 qian and 2 fen, with little change from before. In the afternoon, it suddenly rose by 3 li, calculated as 6 qian, 2 fen, and 3 li. The trading volume was 2,500 jiao in the morning and 3,500 jiao in the afternoon. Yarn and Cotton Yarn Market Retreats After Rising

Profit-Taking Occurs, Raw Cotton Remains Expensive and Supportive

The yarn market has turned flat and is slightly weaker. The actual reason is that the continuous rise in recent days has prompted profit-taking, leading to a market correction. However, a major decline has not been observed, as raw cotton remains firm and expensive, and manufacturers cannot make a profit. Therefore, the situation can still be maintained. For a time, it seems impossible for the majority of targets to temporarily break through 60 liang. Therefore, there are still many people shorting the market. The market sentiment has turned peaceful. Actual sales in the market are still good. In short, there are still bottom goods available. 20-count Five Blessings Shepherd dull yarn sales are stagnant. Therefore, the near-month price is still suppressed by it. Sellers are still confident.

American Cotton Remains Sluggish

Excessive Rainfall Recently Requires Replanting

Boll Weevils Gradually Appear in the Atlantic States

Anticipation of Cotton Crop Panic in the Summer

A New York dispatch from the 30th reported on cotton market conditions, stating that there was no one listening to cotton crop news. Trading on the cotton exchange this week was unusually light. Bad trade news offset any unfavorable developments in cotton production. Recently, there has been excessive rainfall, and there have been repeated reports that replanting is necessary in Mississippi, Arkansas, and Texas, delaying agricultural work. Some sources say that cotton production will be four to five days behind previous cotton seasons after June. Boll weevils are gradually appearing in the Atlantic states, Mississippi, and southwestern Texas, but there are not many yet. The representative of the local brokers, the cotton industry cooperative, received a total of 492,000 bales for the May period in New York and 84,000 bales in New Orleans. Speculation is not strong. When prices fall, some people buy in, anticipating a cotton crop panic in the summer.

The cotton market is currently sluggish and uninteresting after the unprecedented delivery. Spot cotton demand is weak. The domestic spinning industry is in very poor condition and continues to reduce production. Cotton planting is progressing well, and the weather is better than before.

Japanese Yarn Mills Decide to Reduce Working Hours Again

Plan to Reduce by One Tenth Starting the 6th

An Osaka dispatch from the 30th stated that the directors of the Japan Spinners' Association have decided to further reduce production by 10 percent, bringing the total reduction to about 27 percent including the existing reductions. This decision must be submitted to the general meeting on June 7 for approval. If passed, this new plan will be implemented from June 16 to the end of this year.

Grain and River-Bottom Rice Market Rises

Store Sales Are Refreshed After the Summer Festival

Zhabei: The total number of boats arriving from various groups has been only about twenty since the 20th. The market sales are brisk because store sales are refreshed after the summer festival. The price of Northern Japonica rice has risen by more than 2 jiao. The price of top-quality Japonica rice has reached 21 yuan. Although medium and lower grades of Japonica rice have also risen, transactions are fragmented. However, the current river-bottom stocks of high-grade rice are perceived to be scarce. The market is uniformly tight. There are fewer shipments of thin rice. Shipments from this street have slightly increased, and the market price has risen by 1 jiao. The top-quality mutton dujian is scarce and has good sales. The price has risen by about 1 jiao. The market situation is that goods are sold as soon as they arrive. Biànyuán sales are not strong, and dining sales are also on the sidelines. The overall market is similar to before the suspension of sales.

South Shanghai: The market was very firm in the past two days. More than ten boats arrived from river-bottom areas, and the sales of each stall varied. Changshu and Xichang machine-milled Japonica rice have been in demand in the countryside, so most prices have been raised. Small numbers of customer groups are purchasing, so prices have risen by 1 jiao. The price of particularly top-quality Japonica rice here is more than 20 yuan. The retail sales of Suzhou and Tongzhou machine-milled Japonica rice are also not quiet, and it is after the Dragon Boat Festival, so shops must replenish their supplies, so the overall market has also risen by about 1 jiao. The source of Southern early thin rice is inherently limited, and inventory has also decreased, so the market price is very stable. Because there are only a few sales, the inventory and arrivals of mutton dujian rice are still scarce. Due to the influence of foreign rice, the market is very quiet. The market is still lacking in vigor. Biànyuán sales continue to be weak, and prices are gradually decreasing. The whole market is generally tight and active, except for the stagnant Xiangyuan rice.

Foreign Rice Rises in the Morning and Falls in the Afternoon

A Rise and Fall of Two Jiao

Yesterday's foreign rice market conditions were very good after the opening. Due to the strike in Rangoon, arrivals have decreased. The cargo owners are unanimously bullish and firm. In the morning, Hankou merchants and inland customers purchased actively, and the price rose sharply by 2 jiao. In the afternoon, various groups stopped purchasing due to high prices. The cargo owners, because the price had already risen sufficiently and were worried that arrivals would surge after the Rangoon strike subsided, took the opportunity to sell, and the price immediately fell by 2 jiao. As a result, the market remained similar to the previous day, only leaving a trace of a sharp rise. A total of 15,000 bags were opened, half of which were small grades. The prices were: No. 1 Saigon, 16 yuan and 2 jiao to 16 yuan; No. 2, 15 yuan and 5 jiao and a half; small grades, 15 yuan, 7 jiao, 2 fen to 15 yuan and 4 jiao; large grades, 15 yuan and 4 jiao; Min Dang, 15 yuan, 7 jiao, 2 fen to 15 yuan and a half; one-week delivery, 15 yuan, 5 jiao, 6 fen; Annam long-grain rice, more than 17 yuan and 3 jiao; small grades of brown rice, 14 yuan, 2 jiao, 3 fen.

Flour Market Opens This Year's New Record

New Bulls Compete with Factories

Inland New Wheat Prices Open Very High

Market Prices Open Wild

Yesterday's flour market conditions were rising across the board after the opening in the morning. Because the buying sentiment was very good, coupled with the competition from new bulls such as Xibang merchants, Changbang merchants, and factories, prices immediately rose by 1 or 2 fen. After the second round, prices rose step by step. Furthermore, the inland new wheat prices opened very high, and factories firmly refused to sell. The September price was up 5.5 fen, the August price was up 4.5 fen, the June price was up 2.75 fen, and the July price was up 4.25 fen.
