The Soaring Price of Soybean Cakes

Soybeans: Yesterday's market experienced a meteoric rise. The good news from Dalian was undoubtedly a factor, but the influence of the gold market was also a major contributor. Upon investigation, it was found that the source of the problem was the unfavorable price difference between Dalian and Shanghai, which had severely hampered market activity. Fortunately, local inventories were sufficient, resulting in a stable market situation before the holiday. However, yesterday's market saw a drastic change in circumstances. Existing soybean traders suddenly became active, and major hoarding firms were also eager to participate. However, sellers, recognizing the changing situation, adopted a wait-and-see approach and resisted selling. As a result, the price of ordinary soybeans soared by one cent, opening at a high of 5.60 taels. The standard June futures contract also surged by nine cents to 5.68 taels. The market showed strong demand, and shipments of Yangtze River soybeans, which were previously slow-moving, also followed the upward trend, with over 5,000 bags traded. Currently, the small-scale oil mills and traders on this street are all very active.

Soybean Cakes: Due to the sudden surge in raw material prices and the continuous upward movement in the Dalian market, sales are becoming increasingly brisk, and the market is rapidly rising. Dalian cakes opened at 1.88 taels yesterday, a significant increase of three or four cents compared to the pre-holiday price. This kind of price surge is truly rare. The futures market is experiencing a gradual increase in sales due to depleted inventories and strong customer demand. As a result, the afternoon market was very strong, with the June and July futures contracts moving in tandem with the spot market, also opening at 1.88 taels, a jump of three cents. All traders are actively buying, and further price increases are inevitable.

Tonghai Silkworm Cocoons Average 40% Yield

Cocoon Prices Average 56 Yuan

This year's silkworm crop in Tongzhou and Haimen suffered due to the unrest caused by bandits. The number of households raising silkworms decreased, and the unfavorable weather conditions led to significant losses of silkworm eggs. The new silkworm harvest yielded only 40% of a normal year's crop. After the opening of the cocoon market, the amount of cocoons collected was sparse, with only five days of weighing completed. Each household's total collection was only around 1,000 piculs. Foreign silkworm varieties fetched higher prices, opening at 60 yuan, while domestic varieties ranged from 48 to 50 yuan, with an average price of 56 yuan. The quality of the cocoons is said to be poor.

Jintan and Liyang Cocoon Markets Close

Most Acquisitions Fall Short, Cocoon Prices Range from 56 to 63 Yuan

This year's new cocoons in Jintan and Liyang counties were generally of poor quality, with yields only 30-40% of a normal year. Cocoon markets only operated for 30% of the usual time, with weighing lasting six or seven days. Acquisitions were very limited, but the cocoons were of reasonable quality. Each market collected at most 1,000 piculs, and at least 600-700 piculs. Cocoon markets have now closed. The highest price was for improved varieties, which opened at 72-73 yuan. The average price in Jintan was 55-56 yuan, and in Liyang, 62-63 yuan.

Xiaoshan New Cocoons Are of Inferior Quality and Price

The Western Township Cocoons are the Worst, with Prices Averaging 55 Yuan

This year's silkworm crop in the four townships of Xiaoshan suffered due to the local unrest, resulting in a reduction in the number of households raising silkworms. The inconsistent climate also contributed to a poor cocoon harvest. The number of cocoon markets operating was only 40-50% of last year's. The cocoon market has now closed. This year's cocoons from Xiaoshan are of poor quality, with thin shells. The domestic cocoons from the western townships are the worst, while those from the eastern townships are slightly better. However, the foreign cocoons have the best shell quality. The markets are not accepting inferior cocoons, and cocoon prices are relatively low. Domestic varieties are opening at only 50-55 yuan, while foreign varieties are at 60 yuan, with an average price of 55 yuan.

The Department of Agriculture Dispatches Personnel to Supervise Silkworm Egg Production

China's silk industry is making rapid progress, with silkworm egg production farms springing up in various provinces, showing great potential for rapid development. The Director of the Department of Agriculture and Mining attaches great importance to the production of silkworm eggs and has established a silkworm industry control office to oversee the process. As the current silkworm market comes to a close, various farms are now in the silkworm collection and egg production period. Therefore, more than ten inspectors, including Su Jing, have been specially selected and dispatched to various provincial silkworm egg production farms to provide guidance.

Waterproof Raincoat Fabric: Since opening after the New Year, it has been increasing steadily, for ten or more times, with a total increase of seven or eight cents per yard (last year, the highest price was only 2.95 taels). Shipments to Shanghai began about ten days ago, but the number of goods remained insufficient. Its shortage, firm prices, and prolonged upward trend are the best in the woolen industry this year.

Social News

The Southern Society Holds Its Third Public Performance

Since its second public performance in July of last year by the Drama Group, the Southern Society has focused more on literature and art over the past year. Now, as the dramatic arts are in a period of high development, the Drama Group is willing to share what it has been actively preparing for in recent months. The Society's performance is divided into three parts. The first performance is Tian Han's adaptation of Prosper Mérimée's "Carmen," starring Ms. Yu Shan, in six acts and eleven scenes, making it the Southern Society's longest drama to date. Although Mérimée's novel was written over a century ago, the play allows us to hear the voices of the Spanish people today. The second major performance includes Kolontai's "Red Love" and Tian Han's "New Year's Eve Trial." The third performance features Tian Han's group dramas "Waterway" and "Take Back the Pledge." The first performance is scheduled to take place from the 11th to the 13th of this month, with a three-day run at the Central Grand Theater. The second and third performances will follow in quick succession, in order to live up to the expectations of the community over the past year.

A Few Days of Theatrical Life by Peng Chenghui

I was born active. Whatever I enjoy or am willing to do, I do with all my heart. Therefore, whether at home or abroad, many people say that I "don't know the limits" and have a "childlike nature." However, I let them say what they will, and I continue to run wild with my passionate personality.

This time, the Shanghai Drama Association performed Shakespeare's masterpiece, "The Merchant of Venice," at the Central Auditorium. At the warm invitation of teachers and friends, and fueled by my active emotions, I happily joined in. As a result, I found myself occupying a position among the dozens of lively actors.

Although I did not play a major role, I enjoyed the theatrical life of those few days all the same. I found these experiences to be truly interesting, something that cannot be felt in everyday life. Although the period was very short, it felt particularly meaningful, particularly interesting, and particularly invigorating in my monotonous and rigid daily life. Now, I will write down everything I have felt below:

A Harmonious Group: I was truly amazed by the spirit of cooperation within the Drama Association. Although there were more than fifty actors from all walks of life, everyone was very cooperative, very hardworking, and very responsible. There was no sign of anyone shirking their duties, and everyone was very gentle and amiable, with no air of arrogance. I am a newcomer, but after some introductions and conversations, I felt like everyone had a smile on their face, everyone was very approachable, and everyone was like an old friend. As a result, I did not feel awkward or uneasy at all. I did not feel like they were new acquaintances. We talked freely, we laughed freely. Indeed, I felt like it was a truly harmonious group.

The Earth as a Table: Because the place was too cramped, there was no proper dining table like the neat, orderly, and solemn tables in our school. At mealtime, we had to use the earth as a table. But even so, we did not feel uncomfortable at all. On the contrary, we felt very interesting and very happy. We ate fried rice. Whenever the restaurant staff brought the rice, they would place bowl after bowl on the ground, and we would smile at each other and squat down to pick them up. Some sat to eat, some stood to eat, some walked to eat, and some squatted to eat. If you didn't have enough, I would give you some; if I didn't have enough, you would give me some, until everyone had eaten to their heart's content. I felt that this way of eating was much more interesting than sitting in some big hotel, enjoying the bright lights and fine wines, and eating expensive delicacies.

Going to the Guillotine: In some scenes of this play, some members needed to have their faces painted like the bottom of a pot. Therefore, we called these actors "Pot Bottom Faces" or "Azrica." The process involved first applying cold cream and then painting various colors on it. However, this painting method caused the face to experience an unbearable itch, and you couldn't scratch it because the colors would be smeared. So, every time it was my turn to have this kind of face painted, I was lazy and reluctant to accept it. Therefore, I called this painting of the face "Going to the Guillotine," and the person who painted me would also call me "Going to the Guillotine." "Hey, Going to the Guillotine!" Every time I heard this order, I knew that I had to have the pot bottom face painted.

Competing to Be a Noble: Several of us, fearing that we would have to go to the guillotine, were constantly looking for opportunities to switch roles. Once, one of the actors playing a nobleman was absent due to some matter. Several of us comrades who feared having our faces painted were smiling and competing to do it (in the same scene). "Hey, let me do it!" one said with a smile.

"Your face doesn't look like a nobleman at all," one replied with a smile.

In the end, it was given to me. Some said I didn't look like a nobleman at all, while others said I looked exactly like one. I didn't care. I just put on the nobleman's clothes, put on the nobleman's hat, and went to the courtroom with a relaxed attitude.

The Director Dancing: Naturally, this play itself is a world-renowned and immortal masterpiece. And the actors in this performance were indeed able to fully express its greatness. The sad parts could make people cry, the humorous parts could make people laugh, the angry parts could make people gnash their teeth, and the serene parts could make people feel like they were sitting in a deep mountain valley. The expression of the entire play can indeed make the audience's feelings change in a thousand ways, forgetting that they are in a theater. This is not me deliberately nitpicking, but it is indeed the case. Those who have seen it will know that what I say is true. In all five acts, applause could be heard from the audience like thunder. Our director, Mr. Ying Yunwei (what kind of person he is, Mr. Wu Zhen introduced him in this column a few days ago, so there is no need for me to say more), could not help but dance when he heard the audience's enthusiastic applause. Under his happy emotions, he worked even harder to direct the actors and encourage them, and the actors became even more lively and vigorous. Ah, he is truly a great advocate of art, he is truly someone I admire.

Teasing Each Other with Jokes: There are many places in this play that can make people laugh their heads off. I think the funniest part is when Morocco (the ugliest face) says a series of foolish words when he proposes to Portia, such as "Don't dislike the color of my skin, it is the outer garment that hides the light," "This knife of mine has killed the kings and princes of Persia, and defeated the great Suleiman three times," "Speaking of family, talent, and appearance, I am worthy," and "Oh, bad luck, a skeleton!" Every time I hear these words, I can't help but laugh. The other actors have the same feeling. Therefore, when we are idle backstage, we tease each other with these jokes. Even now, when we meet our comrades and someone recites these words, we still can't help but laugh. May 28th, at Jinan University

The Story of World Literature (1)(6)(4) by John Macy, translated by Hu Zhongchi

Chapter 41: German Literature After Goethe

Around the same time as Liliencron and Dehmel, another school of poetry emerged in Vienna, consciously departing from the northern objective realism and gradually transforming all elements of life into bright, timeless beauty. Among this group of accomplished writers, three are particularly memorable: Stefan George, Hugo von Hofmannsthal, and Rainer Maria Rilke. George was a stern and flawless master; none of his works contain a flawed verse, nor any verses that are not imaginatively and philosophically deeply suggestive. Hofmannsthal, through his choice of dramatic forms and his collaboration with Richard Strauss, achieved international popularity for his group and school of works. However, translation has failed him; the completeness and brilliance, the mystery and magic of his poetry cannot be conveyed. Standing somewhat apart from these two is Rainer Maria Rilke, strict in form yet mystical, the master of all young Expressionist lyric poets born in the ancient capital of Prague. This is because he reconstructs the world from within, recasting it closer to his own refined, musical soul. In recent years, a storm and upheaval of new Expressionism has arisen around him, achieving the most solid accomplishments not only in novels or plays, but also in lyric poetry and philosophical poetry. Among these young contemporaries, at least one name is worth recording: Franz Werfel.

Modern drama, which arose after Holz's experiments and first gathered in the famous Free Stage Association in Berlin, is composed of a collection of works that are exceptional in scope, richness, complexity, and power, and has an international reputation. Hermann Sudermann, though deeply interesting, is not a great playwright. The two outstanding geniuses are Gerhart Hauptmann and Arthur Schnitzler.

Although Hauptmann achieved success with his grand style of poetic drama, such as "The Sunken Bell" and "Henry of Ofterdingen," his naturalist dramas are perhaps his greatest and most characteristic achievements. In plays such as "The Lonely Ones," "The Weavers," "The Beaver Coat," "Hannele's Himmelfahrt," "Michael Kramer," and "Rose Bernd," there is reality and a complete illusion. No words recorded in writing are more certain or more incisive. Secondly, there is a complete reversal of the mythological conception of human sin. The tragic sin in these plays lies within the universe or the human community, not within individual lives. The main characters in Hauptmann's plays are all suffering people; they are more accused than guilty. He is a sympathetic playwright, a representative poet of the industrial and social-minded era. His greatest achievement lies in the creation of characters. No existing writer has created a world filled with such active people, a world from which future generations can glimpse the life of an era or a country.

The Viennese Schnitzler is as realistic and precise as Hauptmann, but he expresses a complex society, a society dedicated to art, accustomed to self-reflection, slightly disillusioned, and feeling weary. He lacks Hauptmann's power, but possesses elegance, refinement, and gentleness. His finest plays, "Liebelei," "Fair Game," "The Vast Domain," and "The Lonely Way," have a combination of honesty, elegiac sadness, and spiritual enchantment. The same can be said of his stories, written in a clear, musical style.

In Germany, the novel lags behind lyric poetry. What hindered the novel was the late maturation of German prose, which only after Nietzsche acquired a modern simplicity, elegance, and documentary nature. Among many interesting and often capable novelists, Gustav Freytag, the recorder of North German peasant life, and Clara Viebig, equally well-known among the proletarians of Berlin and the fortunate children of the Rhine, achieved something close to international fame. Such fame will sooner or later also belong to Ricarda Huch, a scholar, poet, and novelist of artistic purity and imaginative depth, a woman of abundant talent. However, above all these stands two giants, not only of the novel but also of artistic prose: Thomas Mann and Jakob Wassermann.

Thomas Mann is an extremely rigorous writer. A long novel, "Buddenbrooks," and two volumes of short stories and novellas—not to mention his essays—these almost constitute his entire body of work. However, "Buddenbrooks," the story of the decline and fall of a Lübeck aristocratic family, is a vast and complete, splendid and clear work. The short stories and novellas, especially "Death in Venice," are works of unparalleled beauty and restraint. No one in this era has written prose nobler than his.

Wassermann, whose major work "The World's Illusion" was well-received by English readers, is a mystic with broad creative power, great enthusiasm, and prolonged development. He has a taste for fantasy and has always been compared to Dickens and Dostoevsky. Through long effort, he developed an eloquent poetic form and a style appropriate to expressing his enthusiastic view of things. Wassermann has some prophetic power in his blood. Like Schnitzler and Hauptmann, he is Jewish. His contrast with Thomas Mann, just like the contrast between Schnitzler and Hauptmann, illustrates the passion and agitation, the joy and the search for the divine that characterizes the works of many young contemporary German poets, playwrights, and novelists whose writing belongs to a future that is more promising than the present.

Book Review

New Book Monthly Review

Two Female Writers by Wang Tiran

The Female Juror

By Ms. Zhang Wenjuan

Published by Guanghua Bookstore

We have "discovered" two female writers.

One's debut work is a collection of novels, the other's is a collection of poems. Although both are thin volumes, they can bring readers the joy of discovering a wonderful new realm. These two small books are certainly not entirely satisfactory, but it is very difficult to achieve such results with a debut work.

Let's talk about the collection of short stories, "The Female Juror." We simply have praise for this collection of novels, especially for the differences between this female writer and other female writers. The difference lies in the technique of writing novels. We all know that there are already several female writers who write novels, but their works are all the same, excelling in so-called "delicate psychological descriptions." And these so-called "delicate psychological descriptions" are mostly the psychology of these young ladies in the current period, casually written when they are in a state of "elegant inspiration." Therefore, they write not only in great detail, but also with a sense of reluctance to part. So they write about psychologies that don't need to be written, and they like to talk about things in detail that could be written more concisely. Therefore, most of the works of female writers are not economical, and the more delicate the psychological description, the less economical they are. As a result, the story is dull and the length is verbose. The result, in addition to being delicate, has no other advantages, and in addition to psychology, it has no other content. Naturally, this is also one of the natural phenomena in the world, because women are generally not very economical in their speech, and they pay more attention to their own lives. Therefore, it seems that there is no other way except to write a lot about themselves and their psychology. But the novel is a novel after all, it doesn't matter if a person is a little fat or thin, but they must have skin, flesh, and bones. If we write a novel so delicately that it is messy, with unclear features, it is like a person with only three bones, and the whole body is covered with meat. Not only is it paralyzed and unable to stand up, but it is simply half like a person and nine and a half like a ghost. So such novels are really incompletely developed freaks. Although they can be counted among novels, they can never be counted as perfect novels, and they are not worth holding up on our shoulders to parade everywhere. However, in fact, although female writers always like to produce some freakish works, in the eyes of gentlemen who have a liking for scabs, they are all celestial beauties and unprecedented masterpieces. Of course, we dare not say that female writers cannot produce good works. Heaven and earth are our consciences, we would never dare to say that. But, we feel that if they are willing to produce their works slowly, and at the time of creation, give more deliberation, more cutting, and at the same time pay more attention to the lives of others, we believe that they will definitely write better works. However, it seems that most of them are impatient to do so, so we always only have the blessing to see that kind of loosely structured and verbose novels.

This is originally the old temper of our "Chinese writers." When writing short stories, they must write them like a long novel, and they will never write them like a short story. When writing long novels, they must write them like several short stories, and they will never write them like a long novel. Although this method seems inappropriate, it is extremely clever, because only in this way can it be like this and like that. Therefore, as long as you write one thing, it can be like a long novel and like a short story, like a poem (the so-called "someone's novel is simply like a "poem" is also), like a theory, like a text, and like a leaflet. In this way, of course, it can be all-encompassing and can deal with everything.

But, also because there are few things that are like this and like that, such things are particularly valuable. The same is true of short stories. Precisely because there are few novels that are like short stories, we feel particularly happy when we see the several short stories in "The Female Juror." Indeed, the biggest feature of this collection of novels is that it gives us a real short story, and what we want to praise the author for is also this, that is, she is willing to write and can write a "real" short story.

The so-called "real short story" is a work that conforms to the laws of short stories. Such a work must have the elements of economy, compactness, and power. Here we do not want to discuss the definition of short stories, but we can say that if a short novel can tell us a single story, give us a clear impression, and after reading it, we feel satisfied with the characters, environment, plot, etc., then this work is undoubtedly a good short story. Several of the short stories in "The Female Juror" mostly meet this condition, so they are quite satisfying. These seven short stories are all centered on women. The protagonists of the stories are all women, so what is written is of course the lives and psychology of women. But there are many more places to write about life than to write about psychology, but we still clearly see the psychology of those female protagonists, and this is because the author knows how to use life and action to express psychology. This is a very skillful and powerful technique, and it is also a technique that must be adopted when writing short stories. Unfortunately, most of our female writers do not know this method, and only know how to "delicately" "describe psychology" ramblingly. According to the author's "Preface," she wants to "pick up this bald pen and write a few paragraphs about the suffering of our female compatriots, just enough to vent the boredom in my chest." Therefore, in the book, we can easily see this kind of female resistance, especially in "The Female Juror," "Old Woman Ma the School Supervisor," "The Female Beggar," etc., and the resistance mood in "The Female Juror" is especially direct and strong. But the personalities of the female protagonists in these three articles are all written very well, and their stories can also arouse the sympathy of the readers, so we feel that these three articles are the best in the whole book. Because the female juror did not accept the court's verdict that sentenced a woman who visited her husband in prison to death, she tried her best to rescue this woman. Her indignant, enthusiastic, resolute, and serious personality was vividly written by the valuer with some short sentences and simple facts, which is very touching to the readers. The article "Old Woman Ma" is written purely from an objective perspective about this strange female protagonist, writing about her appearance, her behavior, her personality, and her history, all of which are written deeply and clearly, giving the reader a deep impression, and grabbing the reader's attention from beginning to end. Technically, this novel is very commendable. The protagonist's thoughts are indeed a bit old, but she is still a very touching character. There is a description that says,

When she walks, she sticks out her chest, raises her head, and is full of spirit, like a strong man on the battlefield, if you cover up her two small feet.

When I went, she was sorting out books, she handled these books like handling cannonballs. (Page 64)

These two short sentences can very well show the author's flexible descriptive skills and keen observation. In addition, "The Female Beggar" writes about the simplicity and pity of women in rural areas with simple thoughts. "Ms. Xu Yin" writes about the spirit of sacrifice of knowledgeable women. "Blood Book" writes about the infatuation of men and the meanness of women, which on the one hand can arouse the reader's interest, and on the other hand can express the personality and life of various types of women, and has a very sincere tone. Only the protagonist of "A Woodcutter Woman," a modern woman who escaped into the deep mountains to live a primitive life because of the disillusionment of love and revolution, is quite like the fact of the novel, but it is written into a fact that makes people hard to believe, which is a relatively poor article.

After reading this article, we feel that the author seems to be very influenced by foreign novels, so although the structure of these articles is very natural and realistic, it is very similar to foreign novels. The descriptions in them also show the influence of foreign literature. But from a technical point of view, this phenomenon is commendable. Don't we introduce foreign literature because foreign literature can affect the quality and technology of our literary creation? Therefore, the more works like "The Female Juror" are produced, the better.

Lake Breeze

By Ms. Yu Yan

Published by Modern Bookstore

"Lake Breeze" is a collection of poems. In this era when the style of poetry is not flourishing and female writers only love to write novels, the sudden appearance of this debut collection of poems is indeed a noteworthy thing.

This collection of poems of ninety pages, including small poems, contains a total of more than forty poems. These poems are obviously the songs of a girl. Although there are also sorrows and feelings, these sorrows and feelings are also obviously "girlish." Gentle emotions, quiet and soft thoughts, and fresh words are not only fully feminine, but also shining with the brilliance of a girl's era. Poets are inherently sentimental, but the feelings of youthful poets are ultimately only bitter but not spicy. The author of "Lake Breeze" is no exception. Her melancholy and depressed feelings are certainly very vigorous, but there seems to be no deep sorrow in them. Therefore, we should rather say that these poems are phenomena of adolescence, full of rosy dreams of young men and women, who, after first coming into contact with the cold reality, often have a psychological reaction due to the shattering of illusions, that is, a melancholy and world-weary mood. But this kind of mood is completely different from the world-weary mood of the defeated soldier who is covered in wounds and has suffered many blows. The difference, to put it simply, is the difference between disappointment and despair. Young men and women immersed in rosy dreams, once they wake up and see only dirty black brambles, the shock and disappointment at this time is of course conceivable. But although disappointed, they still have lingering feelings for the world and are still attached to it. Therefore, the world-weary mood and pessimistic tone at this time, although quite gray, are not gloomy and terrible, as if on a sunny spring day, although black clouds suddenly cover the sky, there is still a vague sunlight revealing in between, so it is ultimately different from the dark night. The impression that our female poet gives us in "Lake Breeze" is also as if like this. The reason why those poems are full of dim words, melancholic tones, and pessimistic colors, but still do not go to the warm and lovely demeanor, lies in this.

The female poet's melancholy and depression are obviously very deep, so it is "touching the scene to generate sorrow" and "borrowing things to express feelings." Therefore, in "Spring Night Boating on West Lake," the moonlight and singing all stirred up the female poet's sadness, and thinking of the tour on the lake, she couldn't help but sigh:

A small boat,

aroused infinite sorrow,

When, ah, when,

will I get to visit here again. 丨 "To a Friend by the Lake"

In "Small Poems," we can more easily appreciate the poet's sensitivity and sadness. "Small Insects Under the Steps," she feels that they are "wailing." "Fallen Flowers in the Muddy Catkins" are "only able to recall the tenderness of spring." The skull in the sunset wilderness cemetery, she asks it "Were you a beauty in your previous life?" But some are like

The idle sorrow of green grass,

The remnant smile of roses,

Life has passed like this. 丨 "Small Poem" Two

The clouds blown by the gust,

It is just like people's hearts,

Shaking uncertainly. 丨 "Thoughts" Ten

But they are quite lovely small poems with quiet thoughts. Speaking of small poems, we feel that the most regrettable thing is that the female poet wrote too few small poems and too many "large" poems, the so-called "large" poems are those longer poems, such as "Intoxication," "A Broken Ship," "To Ms. SS," etc., because we feel that the poet is good at writing short poems but clumsy at writing long poems. This can be proved by long poems. Many long poems often only have a small part of the lines that really have poetic flavor. For example, the first only has "That gentle rising and falling sound of beating pulp, shattered the moonlight in the lake, broke through the loneliness of life," three lines are really poetry. The sixth "Night's Groan," only the first two sections are full of poetic flavor. The last section of "Moonlit Night with a Gentle Breeze" is good. "Envy" is also good in the last section. "Rainy Night" only needs the first section. The traces of old poetry in the last two sections are too deep. There are too many examples like this, so there are several poems, such as "Night's Groan," "In Sickness," "Night of Losing Heart," and the scenery-writing "Summer Night" "Seashore at Early Dawn," etc., although the whole article is lovely, there are only a few lines in several articles that are good. We feel that if the author uses a "contraction policy" on these poems and writes them into short poems of less than ten lines, wouldn't it be good? There are also several hundred poems that have too thick an old poetry flavor. Too many words such as "Tuan Fan," "Chàng Wàng," "Guan Shan," "Qing Hui," "Xiao Xiao," "Sa Sa," and "Li Ge" are used, which are a bit clichéd.

Manuscript Examples for Book and Newspaper Reviews

(1) The text is limited to introducing the latest publications at home and abroad. In addition to literary works, all political, economic, legal, scientific, educational, etc. books and newspapers are included in the introduction, but boring books will not be introduced.

(2) Texts on textual research or research on ancient Chinese books will not be published.

(3) Pictures and photos are limited to those related to the text.

(4) Each text should not exceed three thousand characters.

(5) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(6) Do not write the manuscript horizontally, and the characters should not be scribbled. Western characters can be omitted. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached under the translation.

(7) When attaching pictures to the manuscript, do not use blue ink to draw, and do not use colored paper. White paper and black drawing must be used.

(8) Please indicate that the incoming manuscript is received by the book and newspaper introduction department.

(9) Incoming manuscripts will not be returned whether they are published or not. If you need to return them, you should declare in advance and attach sufficient postage.

(10) The remuneration for texts is divided into three types: four yuan, three yuan, and two yuan per thousand characters. The same applies to pictures and photos. If there are special manuscripts, the remuneration will be calculated separately.

Group News

Shanghai Jiangwan National Labor University is the highest institution of labor education in the country. It is divided into: 1. School of Social Sciences (with departments of Sociology, Education, Economics, Politics, and History and Geography); 2. School of Engineering (with departments of Mechanical Engineering, Civil Engineering, Electrical Engineering, Chemical Engineering, and Architectural Engineering); 3. School of Agriculture (with departments of Horticulture, Agricultural Chemistry, Agronomy, Biology, and Sericulture). In addition, there is an attached middle school department. The treatment for male and female students in the university department and middle school department is the same, and all tuition, board, and lodging fees are waived. The school also provides uniforms. Since its opening, the achievements have been remarkable. The school's Yu Zhongbiao, Wang Yingming, and Tang Yougeng, in view of the fact that those who come from afar to take the exam have no way of knowing the situation of Labor University, and also because friends from all sides have repeatedly written letters asking for details, in order to avoid the trouble of answering each one, they have collected rich materials and compiled a booklet called "National Labor University Application Guide," which contains detailed information on the situation of Labor University, the living conditions of students, and the entrance examination questions over the years, so that applicants can have something to inquire about. Each book costs 14 cents for printing. Mail orders can be sent to Yu Zhongbiao at the school.

The Taijiquan special class of the Sixth Training Ground of the Municipal National Martial Arts Hall, originally located on the third floor of 61 Nanjing Road, Paoball Ground, has been relocated to the New World Northern Amusement Park on June 4 due to the lease of the premises being terminated. Mr. Wu Jianquan will continue to teach at the original scheduled time of 7:00 am to 9:00 am every Monday, Wednesday, and Friday.

However, there are not many sample cars available, and each person is limited to purchasing one vehicle.

It specializes in installing various screen windows and screen doors. The project is exquisite and beautiful. Whether it is a residence or a public office, it can be installed. Opening doors and windows allows air to circulate as usual, and it can also prevent flies, mosquitoes, and other insects from flying in, which can provide a lot of assistance to hygiene. If there are hospitals, factories, schools, hotels, restaurants, or theaters and other public places that want to install this project, they can write to the company, and the company can send personnel to estimate the price and install it at cost. This is also a way to demand universal hygiene.

Theater News

The Summer Peacock Theater announces that it has specially secured, at a considerable rental fee from the American First National Company, the most renowned sound production of that company, "The River of No Return." This film is the masterpiece of Frank Lloyd, the most famous director in America today. Mr. Lloyd once visited China two or three years ago and was very popular with filmgoers in Shanghai. This film is his first major work after returning to his home country. The lead actors in the film are two of America's top movie stars: male lead Lew Ayres and female lead Betty Compson. Mr. Ayres also sings the melancholic song "The River of No Return" and performs a piano solo in the film, achieving exceptionally beautiful results. His spoken lines are also very clear. It can be described as the only large-scale sound production of the year, and also Mr. Ayres' first successful venture into sound films. The film is scheduled to be shown simultaneously at this theater and the Apollo Theater starting this Thursday. It was submitted to the Concession and Chinese Inspection Committees for review a few days ago, and was highly praised by the committee members, who claimed that the film has the potential to influence people's hearts, and so on.

The Lone Star Film Company announces that after the successive completion of "Pirate's Blood," "The Knight," and "The New Jade Hall Spring," the company immediately began work on the drama "Flying Swallow," produced by Huang Wenchun and directed by Lu Fuyao, starring Qian Siying, Zhang Lijun, and Bao Gusong. In the plot, the characters of Flying Swallow and Purple Swallow are played by Ms. Qian Siying and Ms. Zhang Lijun, respectively. Ms. Zhang studied abroad and is not only knowledgeable but also beautiful in appearance and skillful in her performance, fitting the role in the play very well. Several performances were filmed yesterday, and the results were very satisfactory. It is suspected that the exterior scenes of the drama will be filmed by the Taihu Lake. Director Lu will lead the entire cast to depart tomorrow, and so on.

The Xin You Theater Troupe, which is currently holding a "Difficult Drama Movement," reprised its first-day play, "Uncle Vanya," at the Central Auditorium on North Sichuan Road on the day before yesterday (May 31). The play is a masterpiece by Chekhov, with an extremely ordinary story, breaking away from the usual legendary clichés. The troupe spent several months rehearsing with great effort to achieve perfection. In addition, all the actors are talented and have stage experience, and the sets and lighting are meticulously realistic. Therefore, although the weather was gloomy that day, the audience all held their breath and focused their attention on the stage, it is said.

The Paris Grand Theater announces that starting today, the hilarious and romantic film "Mother and Daughter Competing for Love" will be shown, which is both sad and joyful, full of humor and wit, and has similarities with Ernst Lubitsch's "Trouble in Paradise." The theater's general manager, Mr. Han Yibin, in order to treat the audience favorably, has also specially hired the famous singing flower, Ms. Lei Qi, to perform romantic and seductive songs on stage at 5:30 and 9:15 PM, with the ticket prices remaining the same, it is said.

Publishing News

The Shanghai-Ningbo Steamboat Teahouse Workers' Union announces that "Hang Sheng," the union's propaganda section publication, the tenth issue commemorative special edition, was published yesterday. The cover is printed in double-layered color, and the content includes various copperplate illustrations and many types of forms printed in color, as well as inscriptions by Chen Dezheng, Chen Junyi, Tong Xingbai, Zhao Tieqiao, and others, and congratulatory messages from various labor unions. In terms of text, it includes "Narratives, Opinions, Special Items, Novels, Travelogues," and other concise essays. The entire book is a well-bound, thick volume. This publication is not for sale. Anyone who wishes to obtain a copy only needs to attach a two-cent postage stamp and mail it to the union at No. 80 Qiaojia Road, Xiaonanmen, this city, and it will be sent to them immediately, it is said.

Cai Diaotu announces that the Dragon Report Tri-Weekly has been published for two years and has always been popular with readers, with a wide circulation. However, due to the publication of a certain manuscript, it was detained, and the Dragon Report was also suspended. Now the newspaper is scheduled to continue publication today, to meet readers again. The content is quite exciting, it is said.

The Luye Society, organized by students of Jiji University, announces that the society will publish a literary publication, named Oasis. The content includes literature, drama, and music, with approximately 60,000 words per issue. The inaugural issue will be published before June 15, and the general distributor will be Zhenrun Nanxin Bookstore, it is said.

Medical News

Weiling Pharmaceutical Company announces that the company has recently released two kinds of medicinal solutions, one called Anzhi Detoxifying Solution and the other called Insecticide Solution. Repeated tests have shown that they have miraculous effects, and they have been tested and certified by the Central Health Bureau. Anzhi Detoxifying Solution specializes in treating rheumatism, swelling pain, skin ringworm and scabies, and other diseases. Insecticide Solution specializes in killing various germs, mosquitoes, fleas, bedbugs, etc. Manager Deng, in order to promote widely, is selling them at reduced prices. Anzhi Detoxifying Solution is priced at 15 cents per bottle, and Insecticide Solution is priced at 20 cents per bottle. The general sales office is located at No. 6 Yurun Lane, Dongbao Xing Road, south of Yokohama Bridge, North Sichuan Road.

Calligraphy and Painting News

Mr. Lu Gongwang of Beiping sells his calligraphy in Shanghai. As a military man who is proficient in calligraphy and painting, he is highly respected. As the summer season arrives, requests for fan paintings from this city and other places are especially numerous. His calligraphy is vigorous and powerful, his style is novel, and his prices are relatively low compared to others, making it popular with both refined and common tastes. The number of admirers is increasing. Although he is now practicing quietly by West Lake, all writing requests are sent daily by a special representative from his main receiving office at No. 129 Bai'er Road in the French Concession, and the items can be picked up in approximately three days. All major stationery stores in this city and other places are acting as receiving agents, it is said.
